# 2.2 DL Scheduler

## 2.2.1 Scheduler Overview

**2.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `11147496`)

Scheduler Overview

- Basic tasks of the PBCH Scheduler (3GPP) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21948\_replaced([11173661](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuVOafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- DL Scheduling for the artificial load generation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4104\_replaced([11183791](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvNYI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

#### 2.2.1.1.0-1 DL Scheduling of 5G UEs DL Scheduler Overview (UE Traffic only) (ID: 11147508)

**2.2.1.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11147562`)

DL Scheduling of 5G UEs
[CNI-127108]

DL Scheduler Overview of FR1

[End CNI-127108]

link:

<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:u:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20L2%20Entity%20Level/2%205G-L2-PS%20Component%20Requirements/2.2%20DL%20Scheduler/5G_L2_9852_%20DL_scheduler_overview%20FR1_24R2.vsd?d=w374275ec5c39420798fdf099daad7258&csf=1&web=1&e=1vzykS>

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a scheduling process in a communication system. The flowchart is divided into several sections, each representing a stage in the scheduling process.
The top section, labeled "Pre Scheduler," shows a "Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set" which is divided into "highest priority UEs" and "lowest priority UEs." These are then fed into "Candidate Set 1."
The next section, labeled "Candidate Set 2," receives input from the previous stage and then proceeds to "UE selection." Following this, there is a horizontal bar containing several UE types: "New Tx UE," "Prio Bearer UE," "MACCE UE," "New Tx MU-MIMO UE," "ReTx MU-MIMO UE," "Re Tx UE," and "MACCE/SRB On Init BWP UE." Below this bar is a box labeled "Round robin distribution prb."
The "Allocation resources" section contains three numbered steps:
1. "round robin allocation to MU-MIMO UE"
2. "allocate remaining prb to MU-MIMO UE"
3. "allocate remaining prb to SU UE"
The bottom section, labeled "FD Scheduler," contains a box labeled "allocated FD ressources." This section then branches into two components: "PDCCH Sender" and "PUCCH Sender." The "PDCCH Sender" contains "DCI" and has a "PDCCH Send Request" output. It also receives a "PDSCH Receive Request." The "PUCCH Sender" contains "UCI" and has a "PUCCH Receive Request" output. It also receives a "PUCCH Receive Request."[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1062.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

DL Scheduler Overview of FR2 (UE Traffic only)

<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:u:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20L2%20Entity%20Level/2%205G-L2-PS%20Component%20Requirements/5G_L2_5449%20DL_scheduler_overview%20FR2.vsd?d=w4dc22d75a7c346d7970af2cbb086056b&csf=1&web=1&e=B1XiNG>

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a scheduling process in a communication system. The flowchart is divided into several main sections: Pre-Scheduler, TD Scheduler, FDM Scheduler, and two FD Schedulers (first and second).
The **Pre-Scheduler** receives a "served DL resource request" and a "new DL resource request". It has a "Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set" which categorizes UEs into "highest priority UEs" and "lowest priority UEs". The output of this stage is "Candidate Set 1", which is also influenced by "UE PDSCH scheduling occasion".
The **TD Scheduler** takes "Candidate Set 1 Selected" as input. It then generates a "Candidate Set 2 list", which is further divided into "first carrier CS2" and "last carrier CS2", indicating a time-division multiplexing aspect.
The **FDM Scheduler** receives the "Candidate Set 2 list" and produces "To-be-Scheduled UE lists", categorized by "first subcell UE list" and "last subcell UE list", suggesting a frequency-division multiplexing aspect.
The flowchart then splits into two parallel paths, representing the **first FD Scheduler** and the **second FD Scheduler**. Both FD Schedulers receive "allocated FD ressources". Each FD Scheduler has two sub-components: a **PDCCH Sender** and a **PUCCH Sender**.
The **PDCCH Sender** handles "DCI" (Downlink Control Information) and generates a "PDCCH Send Request".
The **PUCCH Sender** handles "UCI" (Uplink Control Information) and generates a "PUCCH Receive Request".
There is also a "PDSCH Send Request" originating from the FD Scheduler and going towards the L1 layer.
Both the "PDCCH Send Request" and "PUCCH Receive Request" from both FD Schedulers are directed to the **L1** (Layer 1) interface, which is the physical layer.
The entire process is described as "slot synchronous".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1062.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Pre-Scheduler: refer to 5G\_L2\_21809.

Time Domain Scheduler (TD Scheduler): refer to 5G\_L2\_21811.

[CNI-127108]

Spatial Domain Scheduler (SD Scheduler): refer to 5G\_L2\_21813.

[End CNI-127108]

Frequency Domain Scheduler (FD Scheduler): refer to 5G\_L2\_21815.

#### 2.2.1.1.0-2 DL Scheduling of 5G UEs Pre-Scheduler overview (ID: 11147570)

**2.2.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147577`)

DL Scheduling of 5G UEs
The pre-scheduler maintains the “pre-scheduler candidate set” (5G\_L2\_226) of UEs with resource requests of downlink direction (such as VoIP or data transmission, or HARQ retransmission). This set contains a list of UEs that are categorized in resource request classes defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9465\_replaced([11174010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuXqrvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) excluding ‘systemInformation’ and ‘paging’, each UE belongs to only one resource request class and the highest priority class among all it’s serving cells (in case of CA) is selected.

[CB012734-E] If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = TRUE and rdActEnhBeamSelection = TRUE, the DL pre-scheduler maintains in addition a list per beam for the DL DRB traffic request class. The UE with this request class is added to the list associated with its primary beam. [End CB012734-E]

In each list, new UEs are added to the back of the list, such that UEs are ordered by the age in the list (5G\_L2\_226). The UEs in this set meet the criteria defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4185\_replaced([11174341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Pre-scheduler Candidates Based on Buffer Utilization”, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18928\_replaced([11174508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (pending RACH Msg2 / Msg4 and SRB0) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22397\_replaced([11174529](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (pending retransmission), with exceptions defined in any of following requirements:

[Before CNI-127108]

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4188\_replaced([11174351](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (user setup reception for SgNB addition)

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4189\_replaced([11174355](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Measurement Gap (MG) handling for SA”

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22395\_replaced([11174363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (beam failure recovery)

[CNI-127108]

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4188\_replaced([11174351](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "user setup reception for SgNB addition"

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4189\_replaced([11174355](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Measurement Gap (MG) handling for SA"

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22395\_replaced([11174363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVBfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "beam failure recovery"

[End CNI-127108]

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8181\_replaced([11153814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksolSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Reception of PsUser\_UserModifyReq” (force DCI 1-0 transient phase)

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4196\_replaced([11174380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Excluding UE from Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set” (PUCCH F3 transient phase, HARQ A/N feedback confliction with SR/CSI report)

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6609\_replaced([11174409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Excluding UE from Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set due to SCell release”

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4201\_replaced([11174422](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8E_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Excluding UE from DL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set due to A-CSI scheduling with large k2 timing and no k1 available”

[CNI-127108]

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14878\_replaced([11174430](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Excluding UE from DL pre-scheduler candidate set due to HARQ-AN bit size restriction"

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23479\_replaced([11174440](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8F_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Excluding UE from DL pre-scheduler candidate set due to BetaOffsets update"

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25360\_replaced([11174462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8HPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Excluding UE from DL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set on Scell due to reconfiguration"

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25378\_replaced([11174474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Excluding UE from DL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set on Scell due to Measurement Gaps"

[End CNI-127108]

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4204\_replaced([11174481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Check UE DRX status”

[Before CNI-127108]

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4205\_replaced([11174491](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (URLLC)

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4208\_replaced([11174539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (User Stop/Delete and SCell release).

[CNI-127108]

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4205\_replaced([11174491](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "URLLC"

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4208\_replaced([11174539](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kucjLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "User Stop/Delete and SCell release"

[End CNI-127108]

UEs stay in the “pre-scheduler candidate set” until their resource request has been served (5G\_L2\_226), or the UE is no longer eligible for scheduling, e.g., due to one of the exceptions mentioned above. Note: UE may have more than one resource requests, only all its resource requests are served, UE is not added into “pre-scheduler candidate set”.

[Before CB012734-E]

At each PDSCH scheduling occasion, the pre-scheduler creates the “Candidate Set 1” (CS1) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4209\_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on the pre-scheduler candidate set.

[CB012734-E] At each PDSCH scheduling occasion,

* If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = False or rdActEnhBeamSelection = False, the pre-scheduler creates the “Candidate Set 1” (CS1) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4209\_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on the pre-scheduler candidate set.

-Else, the pre-scheduler performs the beam selection as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27542\_replaced([11174581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudKOfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and determines the   set of UEs the selected beam serves to create the “Candidate Set 1” (CS1).

-End

[End CB012734-E]

For this set UEs are selected in the order of the pre-scheduler candidate set, i.e., in order of their request class priority (note: request class sub-priority is not considered). The pre-scheduler selects either up to rdMaxNumUeTdDl UEs (when CPU overload control is disabled) or up to schedulingCapacity UEs (when CPU overload control is enabled) from the pre-scheduler candidate set [Before CNI-127108](5G_UP_ALG_4825_replaced([11195013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4tnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[CNI-127108](5G_UP_ALG_4209_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CNI-127108]. For detail about CPU overload control, please refer to 5G\_L2\_1820.

---

#### 2.2.1.1.0-3 DL Scheduling of 5G UEs TD Scheduler overview (ID: 11147585)

**2.2.1.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11147592`)

DL Scheduling of 5G UEs
The Time Domain (TD) scheduler takes “Candidate Set 1” (CS1) as the input for TD scheduling decisions.

[Before CB012734-E]

In case of analog beamforming, the TD scheduler selects all UEs corresponding to the beam which is associated with the highest priority UE (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4251\_replaced([11175632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuke-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the “CS1 Selected” set (i.e. rrmDlCandidateSet1Selected of 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4258\_replaced([11175719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Here priority considers both the priority class (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9465\_replaced([11174010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuXqrvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), as well as the sub-priority of the priority class (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4147\_replaced([11174034](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in case multiple UEs have the same priority class, as described in 5G\_L2\_223.

[CB012734-E] In case of analog beamforming,

-If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = False or rdActEnhBeamSelection = False, the TD scheduler selects all UEs corresponding to the beam which is associated with the highest priority UE (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4251\_replaced([11175632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuke-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the “CS1 Selected” set (i.e. rrmDlCandidateSet1Selected of 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4258\_replaced([11175719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Here priority considers both the priority class (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9465\_replaced([11174010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuXqrvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), as well as the sub-priority of the priority class (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4147\_replaced([11174034](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in case multiple UEs have the same priority class, as described in 5G\_L2\_223.

-Else the selection of UEs corresponding to the beam associated with the highest priority UE is skipped as it's already performed in Pre-scheduler as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27542\_replaced([11174581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudKOfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). As a consequence, “CS1 Selected” is identical to "Candidate set 1".

-End.

[End CB012734-E]

In case of digital beamforming or if beamforming is not enabled, “CS1 Selected” is identical to CS1 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4258\_replaced([11175719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Based on “CS1 Selected”, the TD scheduler creates “Candidate Set 2” (CS2) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4257\_replaced([11175678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuke_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which is a set of carrier-specific UE list. CS2 is created on carrier (or cell) basis, that is, one and only one CS2 is created for each carrier (or cell). For FR1 (where only one carrier or cell is served by each DL Scheduler instance) or when CA is disabled (so only one serving cell is provisioned to UE always), for each element (or each UE) in “CS1 Selected”, the TD scheduler assigns this UE to appropriate CS2. For FR2 (where multiple carriers / cells may be served by each DL Scheduler instance) and when CA is enabled (so more than one serving cell may be provisioned to UE), a CA UE may be assigned to more than one CS2 according to the number of serving cells provisioned to it and the DL scheduling eligible status of each serving cell. Some UEs may be excluded due to carrier (or cell) based (rather than sub-cell based) physical resource availability checking or scheduling constraints, e.g. for the scenario specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9485\_replaced([11175683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “DTX optimized specific CS1 UE handling”, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4263\_replaced([11175793](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kultHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Limit Scheduling Opportunities of UEs with few DRB Data in DL Buffer”, etc.

To distinguish the “to-be-scheduled UEs” set mentioned below which is subcell based, let’s call the CS2 created by now ‘CS2\_candidate’, and call the “to-be-scheduled UEs” set mentioned below ‘CS2\_tobescheduled’. When term ‘CS2’ without any postfix being referenced, it could mean to either ‘CS2\_candidate’ or ‘CS2\_tobescheduled’ depending on the text context referencing to it.

After CS2 has been determined on carrier basis, the TD scheduler builds the “to-be-scheduled UEs” set on sub-cell basis based on CS2 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4292\_replaced([11177281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuuP-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is called CS2\_tobescheduled. For each “to-be-scheduled UEs” set, this set contains a list created by subsequently adding UEs in the same order of as CS2 building up to a maximum of rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl UEs in all BWPs (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4302\_replaced([11177392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuu3CfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rrmNumUesFdmDlInitialBWP in initial BWP (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11177413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuu3DfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), while ensuring there are sufficient resources available according to the Checks specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4297\_replaced([11177362](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuu3A_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), supposing resources for SIB1 and SI messages (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3747\_replaced([11165240](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktgH9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) & 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3800\_replaced([11166015](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktjyW_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and resources for Paging (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4293\_replaced([11177286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuuP-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) have been excluded already.

FDM Scheduler are used to schedule multiple UEs in a single slot:

- FDM Scheduler is used for the scheduling of multiple UEs in a single slot by giving each UE different frequency resources.

- Mu MIMO scheduler is embedded in FDM scheduler.

Note: FDM Scheduler is only needed for FR1.

---

#### 2.2.1.1.0-4 DL Scheduling of 5G UEs SD Scheduler overview (ID: 11147599)

**2.2.1.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11147604`)

DL Scheduling of 5G UEs
In case of digital beamforming:

* when actDlMuMimo in PsCell\_CellSetupReq is true, the CS2 list created by TD Scheduler shall be the input of SD scheduler, SD scheduler shall generate multiple CS2 lists and send each one to the corresponding FD scheduler, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4358\_replaced([11141887](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* when actDlMuMimoEnh in PsCell\_CellSetupReq is true, the SD scheduler shall be merged into FD scheduler, for the DL pairing algorithm in FD scheduler and virtual UE concept, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7427\_replaced([11142415](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.2.1.1.0-5 DL Scheduling of 5G UEs FD Scheduler overview (ID: 11147611)

**2.2.1.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11147618`)

DL Scheduling of 5G UEs
Frequency Domain (FD) scheduler takes the “to-be-scheduled UEs” set as the input for allocating frequency resources, i.e., physical resource blocks (PRBs) as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4487\_replaced([11179166](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku4A_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “assignment of the number of PRBs” and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4522\_replaced([11183696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvMxEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “DL resource assignment for 5G UEs with carrier aggregation” to serve the UEs request, with the considerations specified in following requirements:

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4525\_replaced([11184113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvP0a_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “DL HARQ handling”

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4537\_replaced([11185465](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTew_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “Bearer Prioritization and Multiplexing”

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4563\_replaced([11187069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvYXRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “DL PUCCH Scheduling”

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7383\_replaced([11187558](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvcBo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) “PLMN and Slice Awareness”

[CNI-127108]

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4621\_replaced([11192057](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kviITvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Transport Block Size Calculation"

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4665\_replaced([11192609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvlyp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Configuration of 5G-L2-LO and 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission"

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4703\_replaced([11193195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvqrIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "Handling of eCPRI fields"

- 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4709\_replaced([11193263](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvrSM_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) "MBSFN and LTE CRS Rate Matching based Dynamic Spectrum Sharing"

[End CNI-127108]

After frequency resources are allocated, the FD Scheduler calculates Transport block size (TBS) for DL transmissions for each UE, and possibly downgrade the MCS for DL scheduling in case of no enough pending data for transmission (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4621\_replaced([11192057](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kviITvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The FD Scheduler finally constructs message notifications targeting to L2-LO, L1-DL and L1-UL to trigger DL TB sending and DL HARQ A/N feedback reception:

- LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq, to request L2-LO to send the new to be built Transport Blocks (concerns initial HARQ transmissions only, excludes RA Msg2) (5G\_L2\_315). Note: L2-LO requests L1-DL to send a DL transport block over PDSCH via DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq.

- DlData\_PdcchSendReq, to request L1-DL to send one or multiple DCI on PDCCH (5G\_L1\_IF\_71\_replaced([11512538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRqbFPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- DlData\_PdschSendReq, (together with DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq that either sent by L2-PS or sent by L2-LO as the consequence of LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq reception) to request L1-DL to send a DL transport block over PDSCH (5G\_L1\_IF\_80\_replaced([11512696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpNPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq, to request L1-DL to send the transmission of the built SIB1, OSI, Paging and RA Msg2 Transport Block (5G\_L2\_317)

- DlData\_PatternConfigReq, to provide to L1-DL a message which carries the 5G RF Beamforming Control message (5G\_L1\_IF\_55\_replaced([11512426](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRpM-fvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- UlData\_PucchReceiveReq, to request the reception of PUCCH from L1-UL

[Before CNI-127108]

Implementation Note 1: in downlink direction, FD Scheduler runs on separated EO than DL scheduler EO (i.e. PS-DL EO) and part of the message sending to L2-LO / L1-DL is carried out within the post scheduling procedure of DL Scheduler EO.

Implementation Note 2: For FR2, up to 2 FD Scheduler (EO) instances are running at the same time for parallelized scheduling of frequency domain resources within each DL Scheduler (EO) instance; For FR1 in non supercell mode, only 1 FD Scheduler (EO) instance is created, in other words, there is no parallelization for frequency resource scheduling on FR1 although FD Scheduler runs on a separated EO than DL scheduler EO. In case of supercell mode enabled according to 5G\_L2\_7884, depending on the number of supercell subcells up to 6 FD Scheduler (EO) instances are running at the same time for parallelized scheduling of frequency domain resources among supercell subcells within each DL Scheduler (EO) instance.

[CNI-127108]

Implementation Note 1:

* In downlink direction, FD Scheduler runs on separated EO than DL scheduler EO (i.e. PS-DL EO) and part of the message sending to L2-LO / L1-DL is carried out within the post scheduling procedure of DL Scheduler EO.

Implementation Note 2:

* For FR2, up to 3 FD Scheduler (EO) instances (refer to 5G\_L2\_4595) are running at the same time for parallelized scheduling of frequency domain resources within each DL Scheduler (EO) instance;
* For FR1 in non supercell mode, only 1 FD Scheduler (EO) instance is created, in other words, there is no parallelization for frequency resource scheduling on FR1 although FD Scheduler runs on a separated EO than DL scheduler EO. In case of supercell mode enabled according to 5G\_L2\_7884, depending on the number of supercell subcells up to 6 FD Scheduler (EO) instances are running at the same time for parallelized scheduling of frequency domain resources among supercell subcells within each DL Scheduler (EO) instance.

[End CNI-127108]

PDCCH Sender

Based on the allocated resources from FD scheduler the PDCCH Sender creates the DCI (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4436\_replaced([11178038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuzvivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and sends it to the L1 in form of a “PDCCH Send Request”, or DlData\_PdcchSendReq.

PUCCH Sender

According to the PUCCH resource allocation result for HARQ A/N feedback which is possibly multiplexed with SR and periodical CSI reception, and according to the PUCCH resource consuming for SR and periodical CSI alone scheduling, PUCCH Sender constructs UCI receiving request and sends it to the L1 in form of a “PUCCH Receive Request”, or UlData\_PucchReceiveReq.

Note: Overview about PDCCH Scheduler and PUCCH Scheduler are not given out here separately as PDCCH / PUCCH resource reservation and/or allocation scenarios are involved in (almost) all scheduling phases of DL scheduler.

---

#### 2.2.1.1.0-6 DL Scheduling of 5G UEs CORESET and pdcch configuration for FR1-TDD Narrow Bandwidths (ID: 11147624)

**2.2.1.1.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `12533029`)

DL Scheduling of 5G UEs
The CORESET configurations defined in (see 5G\_UP\_IF\_636\_replaced([11502317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSfS6vv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and (see 5G\_UP\_IF\_638\_replaced([11502627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSfS7_v1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR1 TDD 10MHZ and for FR1 TDD 15MHz.

Since there are only 24PRBs bandwidth in FR1 TDD 10MHz and only 38PRBs bandwidth in FR1 TDD 15MHz, Aggregation Level AL16 is not supported (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_110\_replaced([11095231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmkZgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The TDD time domain configurations and resource set allocations for FR1 TDD 10MHZ and 15MHz is defined in (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_113\_replaced([11095331](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmlAlvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_134\_replaced([11095535](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmmOuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The CORESET0 on 3 symbols, which is only allowed in FR1 TDD 10MHz**is not supported in SSB slots.**

In FR1-TDD 10MHz, the CCE split in slots with Common channel is supported under specific conditions specified in requirements 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16831\_replaced([11169117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt1fIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (slots with paging) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16832\_replaced([11169126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt1fJfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (slots with SIB1 or any other SIB (OSI)).

In FR1-TDD 15MHz, the CCE split in slots with Common channel is not supported (Paging and SIB scheduling require at least 4 CCEs (default value is 4 for parameters dciSiAggregationLevel and dciPagingAggregationLevel) whereas only 8 CCEs available on CORESET(0) that is only on 2 symbols for FR1-TDD 15MHz (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_134\_replaced([11095535](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmmOuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))).

In FR1-TDD 15MHz, the CCE split (4+4 CCE) on CORESET(0) is supported in all non-common channel slots if the third PDCCH symbol is not used (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8917\_replaced([11169038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt04EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8917\_replaced([11169038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt04EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) specifies the Pdcch capabilities and capacity still to maintain the CCE split. The CCE split condition and CCE split start index calculation are determined according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12060\_replaced([11169840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3955\_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB009422-D]

Note:

1. For FR1 TDD 10 MHz and 15 MHz with tdLteConfig0 frame structure, CORESET-0 with 2 symbols and CORESET-1 with 1 symbol shall be configured.
2. For FR1 TDD 10 MHz and 15 MHz with tdLteConfig0 frame structure, no common channel in slot 2/3/12/13, if there's 1 K1 and 2 K2 configured in these slots, the CCE split shall be supported to schedule 1 DL and 2 UL slots, the CCE split index can refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32469\_replaced([11169885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_nnkeoPvNEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB009422-D]

#### 2.2.1.1.0-7 DL Scheduling of 5G UEs PDSCH configurations for FR1-TDD Narrow Bandwidths (ID: 11147641)

**2.2.1.1.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11147652`)

DL Scheduling of 5G UEs

[CB009355-A] Since PDCCH on 3 symbols is supported in FR1-TDD 10MHz and FR1-TDD 15MHz, the pdsch start symbol 3 with corresponding SLIV is supported (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_184\_replaced([11095973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmqgIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB009355-A]

5G\_UP\_ALG\_532\_replaced([11099194](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knC6vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_534\_replaced([11099252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knDhsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). CSI-RS transmission for beam refinement is not supported in TDD FR1 10MHz [CB009355-A]and in FR1 TDD 15MHz[End CB009355-A] due to limited bandwidth.

#### 2.2.1.1.0-8 DL Scheduling of 5G UEs Pre-PreScheduler (ID: 11147659)

**2.2.1.1.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11147665`)

DL Scheduling of 5G UEs
If actTwoCoresL2DeploymentFddFr1 (see 5G\_L2\_16485) is set to True and DL EO receives SlotSynchroInd message for a given CellGroup (see 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_669\_replaced([11177443](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeTEwPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), an additional Pre-PreScheduler phase is executed for each cell within a cell group.

During Pre-PreScheduler phase, PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlSchedulingInd messages are sent to SCells.

RaD parameter rdSlotSynchroIndOffset2CoresDep (see 5G\_L2\_19650) is used to advance SlotSynchroInd message in order to compensate time needed for Pre-PreScheduler phase - otherwise OLC algorithm might detect slot start delay.

Rationale: If there are multiple DL schedulers run on the same core, it is necessary to complete some actions at the beginning of a slot for each cell (e.g. due to message timing requirements).

---

## 2.2.2 Pre-Scheduler

### 2.2.2.0-1 Pre-Scheduler FA: [Internal Domain] Pre-Scheduler Document Owner: Chandan Kumar Mishra (Nokia) (ID: 11147677)

### 2.2.2.1 Scheduling Metrics

#### 2.2.2.1.0-1 Scheduling Metrics Joint Priority and Subpriority Metric for Resource Requests (ID: 11147688)

**2.2.2.1.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `13447347`)

Scheduling Metrics
The priority of a DL resource request r can be quantified by the following metric which takes into consideration both the priority of its request class (mPrio), its sub-priority (mSubPrio) and sub categorization within request class(mSubPrioX)

rrmDlTdResReqMetric(r) = mPrio(r) << (numOfBitsSubPrio + numOfBitsSubPrioX) + mSubPrioX(r) <<  numOfBitsSubPrio + mSubPrio(r)

* mPrio can be set to the configured priority value for that request class (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9891\_replaced([11174018](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or to whatever integer value reflecting the same priority order;
* mSubPrio is the subpriority metric defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4148\_replaced([11174036](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRtfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
* numOfBitsSubPrio must be large enough such that the range of any sub-priority metric can be accommodated.
* mSubPrioX- is the subcategory within resource request class
* numOfBitsSubPrioX must be large enough such that the range of sub categorization can be accommodated

Within drbTraffic class, UEs belonging to NBR category shall always be prioritised over UEs belonging to the normal nonGBR. CP2 reference : 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22067\_replaced([11175521](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kujQ3PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). msubprioX to differentiate between normal nongbr and Nbr category within Drb Traffic resource request class and shall keep Nbr priority with higher metric values compared to non gbr category

Note: CB008227 introduces Nbr category within Drb Traffic Resource request class (CP2 reference 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4178\_replaced([11174242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuaG5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  Nbr category scheduling metric will be as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4232\_replaced([11175151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0nPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For Nbr the definition of UE scheduling weight is as  per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9885\_replaced([11175183](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuhbofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

radioLinkStatus = 1 in all other cases.

The table below analyses the range of mSubPrio for each resource request class:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Resource Request Class** |  | **Range mSubPrio** |  | **Range mSubPrioX** |  |

| [CB014699-B] criticalHarqRetransSrb1 [End CB014699-B] |  |  |  |  |  |

(\*) Msg4 and SRB classes are not needed in Non-Standalone mode (which is the only one supported in 5G18A release). They are initially kept in L2-PS to allow the starting of 5GC000523-A test if the NSA L3 call functionality (5GC000509) is not available yet in the gNB. The calculation of the sub-priorities for these classes is not required: if multi-UE scenario is tested in SA mode, the UEs shall be set-up in sequence such that at each time no more than one UE is included in such classes.

SRB3 is supported in NSA SgNB.

(\*\*) SRB0 or SRB1 messages combined with Msg4 shall be treated in the same class as Msg4 transmission. Standalone SRB0 messages shall be treated with the lowest (zero) sub-priority. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4156\_replaced([11174072](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRvfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

### 2.2.2.2 Scheduling Sets

#### 2.2.2.2.0-1 Scheduling Sets Priority Lists for Pre-Scheduling (ID: 11147731)

**2.2.2.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11147746`)

Scheduling Sets
L2-PS SW shall maintain the UEs from the pre-scheduler candidate set already organized in different priority lists. For each priority class there's a priority list and each candidate UE is member only of the list corresponding to the priority of its highest-priority pending resource request.

At each PDSCH scheduling occasion, before starting to build the CS1 list, L2-PS takes care that the priority lists have been updated according to UE specific events that have been received: a new resource request is pending, a pending resource request has been served, the UE state has changed, etc.. When a UE is added to a priority list it is added at the bottom of it.

Then the CS1 list is prepared as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4209\_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) on the base of these priority lists.

Round Robin selection in the drbTraffic [CB008238-A] or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request [End CB008238-A] class means that, if in a given round N UEs from position x to position x+(N-1) in the DRB list are selected by the pre-scheduler, at the next round the pre-scheduler shall start taking the UEs of the DRB list from the position (x+N).

CP2 reference(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4209\_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) UEs selection for CS1

[CNI-76982-B]

Name numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL is used for total number of UEs present in all piority lists.

[End CNI-76982-B]

---

#### 2.2.2.2.0-2 Scheduling Sets Removing UEs &amp; bearers from L2PS lists upon receiving deletion request (ID: 11147752)

**2.2.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147757`)

Scheduling Sets
In the frame of the arrival of PsUser\_UserDeleteReq message for a specific UE, this UE shall be removed from all L2-PS internal lists (5G\_L2\_226), that are keeping track on the UEs, which having DL data in the DL buffer that are used to process the PM Counters in 5G\_L2\_346.

[5GC000795-B] In the frame of the arrival of a PsUser\_BearerDeleteReq message for a specific UE, this UE shall be evaluated, whether its rmaining bearers have still data in the DL buffer. If not, the UE shall be removed from all L2-PS internal lists (5G\_L2\_226), that are keeping track on the UEs,  which are having data in the DL buffer that are used to process the PM counters in 5G\_L2\_346.

---

#### 2.2.2.2.0-3 Scheduling Sets Removing UE from L2PS lists upon HARQ release (ID: 11147764)

**2.2.2.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11147771`)

Scheduling Sets
When an HARQ process instance is released because the retransmission is not possible due to lack of resources, the UE shall be removed from the Pre-scheduler lists via the appropriate event.

---

#### 2.2.2.2.0-4 Scheduling Sets UE reassignment from dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic to drbTraffic request class (ID: 11147777)

**2.2.2.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11147783`)

Scheduling Sets
The conditions for the reassignment to drbTraffic request class are specified in 5G\_L2\_5938.

The PF metric is not reset upon this reassignment.

---

#### 2.2.2.2.0-5 Scheduling Sets PUCCH tokens preallocation (ID: 11147789)

**2.2.2.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11147796`)

Scheduling Sets
[CB008593-A] if the UE's startingPrb of perSrConfig for periodic SR is aligned with sharedSrPrb and actSharedSr is True in PsCell\_CellSetupReq, and if the DL transmissions HARQ timing will overlap with the UE's F1 SR timing (no PUCCH F3 resource for the UE at the time), the PUCCH resource won't be allocated to the UE and the UE shall be skipped for DL transmission this time, even the UE is the only UE using sharedSrPrb for SR or the UE will have PUSCH transmission in this UL slot [End CB008593-A]

---

#### 2.2.2.2.0-6 Scheduling Sets Excluding UE from DL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set due to HARQ-AN bit size restriction (ID: 11147802)

**2.2.2.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11147807`)

Scheduling Sets
For CA UE with PUCCH allocated by DPA (Distributed PUCCH Allocation), in any serving cell, if cDai[Before PR704798] and tDai values were [PR704798] is [End PR704798] set to INVALID\_VALUE during step 4 of the common algorithm of cDai/tDai/symbol0Restrict determination (see 5G\_L2\_8820\_replaced([11158574](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25LY2PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then this UE shall be removed from DL pre-scheduler Priority Lists for the given DL slot.

As PUCCH resource has already been allocated to UE by DPA, PM counter M55316CRD50005 (Number of CA UE blocked scheduling due to lack of PUCCH resource units, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2958\_replaced([11124049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnzEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall not be incremented.

CP2 Reference: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14878\_replaced([11174430](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kub8FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 2.2.2.2.0-7 Scheduling Sets Excluding UE from DL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set due to dropped K1 (ID: 11147814)

**2.2.2.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11147822`)

Scheduling Sets
For CA UE attached to FR1 TDD PCell with long PUCCH, if K1 value of the PCell was dropped (see 5G\_L2\_8944\_replaced([11156854](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25CO1_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then this UE shall be removed from DL pre-scheduler Priority Lists for the given DL slot.

CP2 Reference: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14929\_replaced([11116229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

#### 2.2.2.2.0-8 Scheduling Sets Calculating sum of scheduling weights based on Priority Lists (ID: 11147826)

**2.2.2.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11147834`)

Scheduling Sets
If NRCELL.actEnhancedFlowControlETh = TRUE, the calculation of sumOfWeightsOverAllEligibleBearersOnCarrier(refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11650\_replaced([11192708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is based on N UEs in drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class in CS1 list, and additional total of M UEs in the drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic piority list [PR739128]and L empty buffer UEs in UE context DB[End PR739128].

where

N + M [PR739128]+ L[End PR739128] <= rdMaxNumUeTdDl, as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11650\_replaced([11192708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

M <= number of UEs in drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic priority list;

[PR739128]L <= rdMaxEmptyBufferUeInSumOfWeights(refer to 5G\_L2\_16438\_replaced([11182693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27d3w_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If the UE of eth is being calculated is an empty buffer UE, it shall be included as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11650\_replaced([11192708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End PR739128]

In the drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic piority list, additional UEs, which are following the UEs selected into CS1 list, are taken into account in the calculation of sumOfWeightsOverAllEligibleBearersOnCarrier: if N UEs from position x to position x+(N-1) are selected as per 5G\_L2\_226\_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), additional M UEs from position x+N to position x+N+(M-1) are considered.

### 2.2.2.3 Pre-build table (only applied for FR2)

#### 2.2.2.3.0-1 Pre-build table (only applied for FR2) Pre-build table (ID: 11147845)

**2.2.2.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11147865`)

Pre-build table (only applied for FR2)
This requirement is only applied to FR2 [CB012734-A] and only when parameter actDedicatedCsiSlots, received in PsCell\_CellGroupSetupReq, is not TRUE (i.e. FALSE or Absent)  [End CB012734-A].

Background:

The CPU performance is critical for FR2 especially in case of DL 8CC CA. DL TD scheduler take more time than expected so that it cause FD scheduler delay too much.

So removing unnecessary handling in DL slot and moving them to UL slot could relieve the burden in DL slots effectively.

Solution:

The solution is introducing a pre-build table.

1.Content of pre-build table

Array of beamSelectionForCsiOrSib: beamSelection result of SIB slot for next continous DL slots.

Array of CsiSendReqInfo: CsiRsSendReq for the UEs which have periodical CSI RS configured in next continuous DL slots.

2.Procedure related to pre-build table

Step1: Cell setup phase

DL scheduler create a pre-build table for every cell when cell setup.

Step2: UL slot

1.reset the pre-build table and initiate it by counting how many DL slots.

2.DL pre scheduler create CsiRsSendReq in advance which is corresponding to CSI RS configured in next continous DL slots and buffer them in pre-build table as CsiSendReqInfo.

CsiRsSendReq for TRS

CsiRsSendReq for UE specific CSI RS for channel measurement acquisition

CsiRsSendReq for refine beam ( if exist )

3.If it is the last slot of a frame ( UL slot ), check if SIB activation or not. SIB beam selection is determined when SIB activation. Then save the beam selection result in pre-build table.

Step3: DL slot

DL TD scheduler check and fetch buffered CsiRsSendReq from pre-build table and send out them to L1.

DL TD scheduler get SIB beam selection result from pre-build table.

Original performance result and idea is <https://nokia-my.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/personal/hao_2_hu_nokia-sbell_com/_layouts/15/Doc.aspx?sourcedoc=%7B11B29C5C-A439-46B5-8522-C5B25FDF94F6%7D&file=UP%20SW%20arch%20optim%20%20brain%20storm%20v1.0.pptx&_DSL=2&action=edit&mobileredirect=true>

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating a process related to cellular network slots, likely in a 5G context. The diagram features a horizontal bar representing a sequence of time slots, each labeled with a letter indicating its type: 'D' for Downlink, 'S' for Synchronization, and 'U' for Uplink. The slots are colored blue for 'D', green for 'S', and orange for 'U'.
Above the slot bar, there are two bullet points describing actions related to the current DL slot:
\* Get csiRsSendReq of current DL slot from pre-build table
\* Get beamSelectionForSib for current DL slot from pre-build table
Several downward-pointing arrows are positioned above specific 'D' slots, suggesting an action or event occurring at those points.
Below the slot bar, there are two sets of bullet points, each describing a process initiated at specific 'S' or 'U' slots. These bullet points are identical and appear to describe a parallel or subsequent process:
\* Initiate pre-build table for next 3 DL slots
\* Create csiRsSendReq including TRS/channel measurement/beam measurement
\* save them in pre-build table
\* Select beam for SIB
The sequence of slots shown is: D, D, D, S, U, D, D, D, S, U, D, D, D, S, U. The arrows are pointing to the first, second, third, and fourth 'D' slots in the sequence. ### 2.2.2.4 Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2

Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2

#### 2.2.2.4.0-2 Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2 2.2.2.4.2 Beam Metric Computation (ID: 11147888)

**2.2.2.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147894`)

Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2
Beam Weight

---

**2.2.2.4.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11147900`)

Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2
If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = TRUE and rdActEnhBeamSelection = TRUE, L2PS shall maintain the beamWeight in DL of each configured beam as below:

beamWeighti=sum(ueWeightk of all UE served by the beami)

With :

beamWeighti: the beam weight of the beamId i,

ueWeightk= sum(schedulWeight of all nonGBR bearers with non-empty buffer configured for the UEk), schedulWeight: the schedule weight for a non-GBR DRB reported in drbAddReqPs struct (5G\_L2\_IF\_397\_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The ueWeightk is updated each time the bufferBytes of one lcId goes from empty to non-empty and vice versa.

The beamWeighti is updated each time:

- ueWeightk of an UE already served by the beami is changed,

- A UE in beami, with ueWeight>0 becomes eligible/non eligible to be candidate for scheduling as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4183\_replaced([11174302](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuat9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- A UE performs a beam switch from/to beami

---

**2.2.2.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11147908`)

Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2
rrmAvgBeamSchedRate

---

**2.2.2.4.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147912`)

Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2
If NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/actHighNumberOfUes = TRUE and rdActEnhBeamSelection = TRUE, the DL post-pre scheduler shall compute if needed\*, the rrmAvgBeamSchedRate at the end of the slot, for all configured beams as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27543\_replaced([11174602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(\*) The rrmAvgBeamSchedRate computation is needed in the case that at least one UE was scheduled over the PDSCH for nonGBR DRB traffic in the cellGroup, in the current DL data slot.

**2.2.2.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11147919`)

Beam Metric

---

**2.2.2.4.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11147925`)

Beam Selection for Analog Beamforming in FR2

- Option2: at the beginning of the slot.

Note: In Option1, the eligibility criteria for UEs is not considered in the beamWeight computation(5G\_L2\_20093\_replaced([11147894](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NvevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

#### 2.2.2.5.0-2 UEs selection for CS1 list UEs selection for UEs in Pairing Group (ID: 12586255)

**2.2.2.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12586256`)

UEs selection for CS1 list
​​​when ZF\_MU is enabled (actDlMuMimoEnh=True, actDlMuPairingGroup = True), aims to improve the zero forcing Mu paring possibility, 5G\_L2\_PS will use bucket algorithm for selecting UEs in DL paring group and prioritize the selecting UEs by put those UEs under a same sub-category in drb traffic ([11148498: Handling of DRB Traffic Request Class For NBR bearers](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24RZ0vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

IF PG>=1 && N>=2

5G\_L2\_PS shall use bucket algorithm to select n UEs in PGs that with ZF\_MU capability to prioritize to CS1 with request class as drbTraffic  and sub-priority as subBandBfUeInPG ,  2=< n =< N.

other UEs in PGs will be added to CS1 without checking ZF\_MU capability with request case as drbTraffic  and sub-priority as drbTraffic

ELSE

5G\_L2\_PS doesn't distinguish that in PG  UE's ZF MU capability , and UE shall be selected using legacy algorithm ,( for legacy UEs'  selection for cs1 [11147936: UEs selection for CS1 list](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWgvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

1,   n>= 2 , it  means per step at least two ZF\_MU eligible in a paring group shall be selected, or this paring group shall be skipped. IF all the paring Groups with less than two ZF\_MU eligible UEs in per PG , then exit bucket algorithm.

2,  PG=1, with or without using bucket algorithm to select ZF MU capability UE will have same result, but without updating bucket value.

where

-PG is number of pairing group

-N is  room that in every step of bucket algorithm.

- ZF\_MU capability see [12571009: ZF\_Mu Candidate List](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_m4HnYS8BEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

- request class and sub-priority see [11148498: Handling of DRB Traffic Request Class For NBR bearers](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24RZ0vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

CP2 reference:  [12447143: Bucket algorithm for selecting DL pairing groups](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_EGVwwAmBEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

#### 2.2.2.5.0-3 UEs selection for CS1 list CS1list UEs selection Optimization for FR2 (ID: 11147953)

**2.2.2.5.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11147966`)

UEs selection for CS1 list
[Before CB012734-E]

For FR2, when rdCs1CandidateUeNumCoeff>0, cs1List UEs selction optimization is enabled, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23553\_replaced([11193808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvvjtfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rdCs1CandidateUeNumCoeff.  In this case, for drbTraffic priority class UEs, following steps are optimized:

* To select max CS1Size number of UEs to Cs1List from pre-scheduler candidate set(5G\_L2\_226\_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the searched and inspected UE number can be much more than CS1Size when numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL greater then CS1Size, due to only CS1 eligible UE can be added to Cs1List. To limit the search UE number, for drbTraffic priority class UEs in pre-scheduler candidate set, only max maxCs1SearchNumber UEs will be searched and inspected.

maxCs1SearchNumber = rdCs1CandidateUeNumCoeff \* CS1Size

The CS1Size is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4209\_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The numOfUesInPreSchedCandSetDL is defined in 5G\_L2\_226\_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* For the drbTraffic priority class UEs, the cs1List UEs are chosen in a roundrobin manner, while the roundrobin start position shall only be moved for the slot when UlData\_PucchReceiveReq has been sent and new PUCCH token become available. The move distance is the max number of drbTraffic prioirty UEs in cs1List of each slots of current HARQ window.

Note that this cs1List UE selection optimizaiton is not applied to UEs with traffic priority higher than drbTraffic priority class.

Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4209\_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB012734-E]

In FR2, analog beam selection and UE selection for CS1 list is performed as follows:

Input Parameters

- actHighNumberOfUes (5G\_L2\_IF\_3117\_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- actPucchBeamConstraintFR2 (5G\_L2\_IF\_3117\_replaced([10966509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UPCB_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- rdActEnhBeamSelection (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27553\_replaced([11193947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvxY0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Algorithm

If actHighNumberOfUes == TRUE And actPucchBeamConstraintFR2 == TRUE

Calculate pucchBeamIdList (Cf. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26785\_replaced([11174828](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kueYWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If rdActEnhBeamSelection == TRUE

If siez of pucchBeamIdList ≥ 2

enforcedBeamList = pucchBeamIdList (with removal of duplicate if any, and sorted by beam metric)

Else

enforcedBeamList = empty

EndIf

selectedBeamId = invalid

cs1List = empty

maxNbrRntisInCs1List = max CS1 size computed by the Overload Controller

atLeastOneRntiEligibleSelectedBeam= FALSE

If Slot with SIB And sibBeamId is configured

selectedBeamId = sibBeamId

EndIf

If selectedBeamId == invalid And Slot with Paging And pagingBeamId is configured

selectedBeamId = pagingBeamId

EndIf

Step1: Through highPrioClassRntis of priorityOrderRntis

Step2: Through drbTrafficClass Rntis is performed

Else

Legacy algorithm based on priorityOrderedRntis with PUCCH beamId constraint is performed (Cf. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26785\_replaced([11174828](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kueYWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If UE is eligible  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4209\_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) And cs1ListSize < maxNbrRntisInCs1List

Add RNTI in cs1List

EndIf

EndIf

Else

Legacy algorithm based on priorityOrderedRntis is performed (Cf. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4101\_replaced([11173728](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuV1dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If UE is eligible  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4209\_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) And cs1ListSize < maxNbrRntisInCs1List

Add RNTI in cs1List

EndIf

EndIf

Step1: Through highPrioClassRntis of priorityOrderRntis

isInitialSelectedBeamIdValid = FALSE

For each DL High Prio Request class supported in FR2 (\*)

Get the listOfRntis associated to the Request class

For each RNTI of the listOfRntis

If Request class == RACH msg2 (Cf. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26785\_replaced([11174828](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kueYWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If selectedBeamId == invalid

selectedBeamId = ueBeamId

Attempt to add RNTI as in \*\*

Else

isInitialSelectedBeamIdValid = TRUE

If ueBeamId == selectedBeamId

Attempt to add RNTI as in \*\*

EndIf

EndIf

Else

If selectedBeamId == invalid

If enforcedBeamList is empty Or ueBeamId is included in enforcedBeamList

selectedBeamId = ueBeamId

Attempt to add RNTI as in \*\*

EndIf

Else

isInitialSelectedBeamIdValid = TRUE

If ueBeamId == selectedBeamId

If enforcedBeamList is empty Or ueBeamId is included in enforcedBeamList

Attempt to add RNTI as in \*\*

EndIf

EndIf

EndIf

EndIf

Until out of listOfRntis OR cs1ListSize == maxNbrRntisInCs1List

Until out of DL high prio request class list OR cs1ListSize == maxNbrRntisInCs1List

(\*\*) Attempt to add RNTI:

If UE is eligible (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4209\_replaced([11174627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudxRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Add RNTI in cs1List

atLeastOneRntiEligibleSelectedBeam = TRUE

Else

If atLeastOneRntiEligibleSelectedBeam == FALSE & isInitialSelectedBeamIdValid == FALSE

selectedBeamId = invalid

EndIf

EndIf

(\*) Request classes handled in Step1 are all classes between rachMsg2 (included) to DRB traffic (excluded)

Step2: Through drbTrafficClass Rntis

If enforcedBeamList is empty

beamIds = sortedBeamIds

Else

beamIds = enforcedBeamList

EndIf

For each beam from beamIds

Get the listOfRntis associated to the beam

For each RNTI of the listOfRntis

If selectedBeamId == invalid

selectedBeamId = ueBeamId

Endif

If RNTI is eligible AND ueBeamId == selectedBeamId

Add RNTI to cs1List

atLeastOneRntiEligibleSelectedBeam = TRUE

Else

If atLeastOneRntiEligibleSelectedBeam == FALSE AND isInitialSelectedBeamIdValid == FALSE

selectedBeamId = invalid

Endif

Endid

Until out of listOfRntis OR cs1ListSize == maxNbrRntisInCs1List

Until out of beam list OR cs1ListSize == maxBnrRntisInCs1List

Output Parameters

- selectedBeamId

- cs1ListSelectedBeam

Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27549\_replaced([11174585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudKOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB012734-E]

### 2.2.2.6 Micro-DTX optimized scheduling

#### 2.2.2.6.0-2 Micro-DTX optimized scheduling Micro-DTX overview (ID: 11147986)

**2.2.2.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147993`)

Micro-DTX optimized scheduling
The purpose of DTX optimized scheduling is to reduce the RU power consumption (that is not a linear function of the number of transmitted PRBs) by trying to bundle transmission of non-GBR  data (excluding 5QI5) with the transmission of mandatory Physical Signals or Common Channels of a cell or with Delay sensitive SRB or DRB bearer(s) of same or different UE(s).

For this reason, a dtxMaxRetentionDelay delay applies to non-GBR data (excluding 5QI5) usually related to drbTraffic request class, CA activated UEs with at least one activated SCell being excluded by default. The UE is temporarily assigned to the dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class during this configurable retention delay. Then, UE is reassigned to the drbTraffic request class to schedule any remaining data.

[CB008238-F] In order to optimize the TCP slow start procedure or TCP connection  opening phases (possibly including security), this configurable retention delay may only apply when all buffered data in 5G-L2-LO buffer(s) have been scheduled since less than dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling [End CB008238-F].

---

#### 2.2.2.6.1 Micro-DTX enabling

##### 2.2.2.6.1.0-1 Micro-DTX enabling Enabling/Disabling of Micro-DTX (ID: 11148003)

**2.2.2.6.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148014`)

Micro-DTX enabling
The Micro-DTX feature is enabled when actDtxOptimizedScheduler = True [CB008238-D] and the cell load is low.

To assess the load, 5G-L2-PS considers the ratio between the number of UEs in the CS1 list and the corresponding maximum number avgMaxNumUeCS1 (reduced in overload condition, refer to its definition in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8945\_replaced([11174992](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kufmffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9949\_replaced([11174961](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kufmdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

* The feature is disabled when the ratio is greater than or equal to rdDtxCellNbUeCs1ThresholdHigh\_percent (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9388\_replaced([11193368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvr5TfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* The feature is enabled when the ratio reaches a value lower than or equal to rdDtxCellNbUeCs1ThresholdLow\_percent (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9463\_replaced([11193377](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvsgUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and remains lower than rdDtxCellNbUeCs1ThresholdHigh\_percent during a predefined duration of rdDtxCellEnablingTimer\_ms (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9390\_replaced([11193387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvsgU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a graph illustrating the behavior of a system over time, likely related to network or signal processing, given the labels. The graph features a blue line representing a fluctuating value, with two horizontal lines indicating thresholds: a red line labeled "rdDtxCellNbUeCs1ThresholdHigh\_percent" and a green line labeled "rdDtxCellNbUeCs1ThresholdLow\_percent". Below the graph, a timeline is segmented into "enabled" (green) and "disabled" (yellow) states, representing the "DTX state".
Several vertical dashed lines and markers are present:
- Yellow dashed lines appear to mark the beginning or end of certain states or events.
- Blue dashed lines connect points on the blue graph to a horizontal segment, which in turn connects to a red diamond marker. These segments seem to indicate a change or a specific event related to the "DTX state".
- Red dashed lines also connect points on the blue graph to a horizontal segment and a red diamond marker, similar to the blue dashed lines.
The blue line fluctuates significantly, crossing both the high and low thresholds multiple times. The "DTX state" timeline shows periods of being enabled and disabled, which appear to correlate with the fluctuations of the blue line relative to the thresholds. For instance, when the blue line drops below the green threshold, the state seems to transition to "disabled". Conversely, when it rises above the green threshold, it may transition to "enabled". The red diamond markers and associated dashed lines suggest specific trigger points or events within the "disabled" state.
The text present in the image is:
- rdDtxCellNbUeCs1ThresholdHigh\_percent
- rdDtxCellNbUeCs1ThresholdLow\_percent
- rdDtxCellEnablingTimer\_ms

- disabled[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1132.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Note: The processing of the cell load is part of the post-Pre scheduler and is only described here for the reader convenience.

[End CB008238-D].

The "Enabled" condition is only checked before assigning a DTX eligible UE to dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic instead of drbTraffic request class as per 5G\_L2\_5933\_replaced([11148047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24O9k_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Therefore, enabling or disabling of the feature does not impact UE already assigned to these classes until totalBufferednonGbrData returns to 0.

---

##### 2.2.2.6.1.0-2 Micro-DTX enabling Enabling/Disabling of Micro-DTX for CA active users (ID: 11148020)

**2.2.2.6.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11148034`)

Micro-DTX enabling
[Before CB009333-C]

Although Micro-DTX feature does not officially apply to CA active UEs (with at least one activated SCell), rdDisableMicroDtxForCaUes (refer to 5G\_L2\_5932\_replaced([11182433](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27bbjPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) could be used to extend the feature to these UEs for test purpose:

[End CB009333-C]

* When [Before CB009333-C] rdDisableMicroDtxForCaUes = False [CB009333-C] caSupportEnabled (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_1862\_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = True [End CB009333-C]

CA active UEs are handled as standard UEs from Micro-DTX viewpoint.

* When Micro-DTX feature is enabled and [Before CB009333-C] rdDisableMicroDtxForCaUes = True [CB009333-C] caSupportEnabled (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_1862\_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = False [End CB009333-C]

Already activated CA UEs cannot be assigned to the dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class (refer to 5G\_L2\_5933\_replaced([11148047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24O9k_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and configured CA UEs shall be reassigned to the drbTraffic request class upon activation of its first SCell (refer to 5G\_L2\_5938\_replaced([11148077](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24O9lvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The main reason is that CA active UEs have pre-defined scheduling opportunities on PDSCH slots selected earlier by PUCCH pre-allocation (DPA) and interworking study with DTX is not complete.

---

##### 2.2.2.6.1.0-3 Micro-DTX enabling Enabling/Disabling of Micro-DTX in overload state (ID: 12709808)

**2.2.2.6.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12709810`)

Micro-DTX enabling
When Micro-DTX feature is enabled (see [11148003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWjvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and overload countermeasure for Micro-DTX features is active (see [11203944](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_29-ZNfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11174974](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kufmefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

Then:  
5G-L2-PS shall take into account additional overload restrictions regarding enabling/disabling Micro-DTX described in [11174961](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kufmdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

---

#### 2.2.2.6.2 Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling

##### 2.2.2.6.2.0-1 Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling UE entry in DTX optimized scheduling (ID: 11148047)

**2.2.2.6.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11148071`)

Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling
A UE is assigned to dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class when following conditions are fulfilled (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8232\_replaced([11174950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kufmc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* The Micro-DTX feature is enabled as per 5G\_L2\_5924\_replaced([11148003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWjvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* The UE is not a CA UE with any active SCell (or Micro-DTX has been enabled as per 5G\_L2\_5926\_replaced([11148020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWkPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for [Before CB009333-C] test purpose on [End CB009333-C] CA active UEs).
* For this UE, 5G-L2-PS has received a non-null BSR with dataAdded > 0 for non-GBR DRB (compatible with drbTraffic request class) in absence of previous data to transmit (TotalBufferedNonGbrData = 0)

Note: TotalBufferedNonGbrData is only an approximation of the data remaining in the L2-LO buffer; so the check on dataAdded helps 5G-L2-PS to exclude the UE from DTX optimized scheduling in case of presence of any leftover to transmit.

* if the [Before CB009333-A] NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling [CB009333-A] dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling (see note below) [End CB009333-A] parameter is greater than 0, the delay between the last scheduling which has emptied its associated 5G-L2-LO buffer(s) and the reception of new data shall be lower than this threshold (refer to 5G\_L2\_5903\_replaced([11148230](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24PkqvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Then, dtxMaxRetentionDelay [CB009333-A] (see note below) [End CB009333-A] timer is started.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to data transmission scheduling, likely in a cellular network context. The flowchart uses boxes to represent states or processes and arrows to indicate transitions or data flow.
Here's a breakdown of the elements:
**Vertical Axis:**
\* **Prio+** (Top): Indicates a higher priority level.
\* **Prio-** (Bottom): Indicates a lower priority level.
**Top Box (Higher Priority):**
\* **Title:** "drbTraffic « Standard scheduling » request class"
\* **Content:** Divided into two sections:
\* **Left (Old):** "UE with oldest pending TX"
\* **Right (Fresh):** "Last queued UE"
\* **Scheduling Method:** "ROUND ROBIN FIFO" is highlighted in yellow.
\* **Incoming Arrow (Green):** From the right, labeled "BSRDRB > 0 (Non-eligible to Micro-DTX)". This suggests that if the Buffer Status Report (BSR) for DRB is greater than 0 and the UE is not eligible for Micro-DTX, this state is entered.
\* **Outgoing Arrow (Gray):** To the right, pointing to "TotalBufferedNonGbrData = 0 (L2-PS internal counter)". This indicates that when this state is active, the `TotalBufferedNonGbrData` counter is reset to 0.
\* **Vertical Text (Right):** "N O D A T A"
**Middle Section:**
\* **Arrow (Gray):** A circular arrow labeled "BSRDRB" pointing back to itself, indicating a feedback loop or continuous monitoring of BSRDRB.
\* **Text:** "Update TotalBufferedNonGbrData"
\* **Timer Icon:** An animated alarm clock icon, suggesting a time-based event.
\* **Arrow (Green):** From the timer icon, labeled "dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer expiry". This signifies the expiration of a timer.
**Bottom Box (Lower Priority):**
\* **Title:** "dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class"
\* **Content:** Similar to the top box, divided into:
\* **Left (Old):** "UE with oldest pending TX"
\* **Right (Fresh):** "Last queued UE"
\* **Scheduling Method:** "ROUND ROBIN FIFO" is highlighted in yellow.
\* **Incoming Arrow (Blue):** From the right, labeled "1st BSRDRB > 0 (Eligible to Micro-DTX)". This suggests that if the first BSRDRB is greater than 0 and the UE is eligible for Micro-DTX, this state is entered.
\* **Text:** "Start dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer" (associated with the incoming blue arrow).
\* **Timer Icon (Blue):** A clock icon with a checkmark, likely indicating the timer has started.
\* **Outgoing Arrow (Gray):** To the right, pointing to "TotalBufferedNonGbrData = 0 (before dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer expiry)". This indicates that before the timer expires, the `TotalBufferedNonGbrData` counter is reset to 0.
\* **Arrow (Red):** From the "TotalBufferedNonGbrData = 0" text, pointing downwards, labeled "⇒ Stop dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer". This indicates that stopping the timer is a consequence of this condition.
\* **Red Cross Icon:** A red cross within a circle, likely indicating the timer is stopped or invalidated.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1139.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

If rdDtxMaxRetentionDelaySlotRounding is greater than one and lower than dtxMaxRetentionDelay, a rounding is applied to the slot number of the timer expiry. Although it reduces the retention delay and the bundling opportunities in a cell, it favors transmission in common slots in case several cells are sharing the same radio and may improve the Micro-DTX gain in absence of cell synchro mechanism.

In case of UE having several non-GBR eligible DRBs, reception of BSR for any of the DRBs is sufficient to enter in DTX optimized scheduling. [Before CB009333-A] TotalBufferedNonGbrData and dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer are handled jointly for all these DRBs. [CB009333-A] TotalBufferedNonGbrData is handled jointly for all these DRBs. dtxMaxRetentionDelay is DRB aware and handled separetly for every DRB. [End CB009333-A]

Notes:

* This assignment is part of BSR processing and only described here for the reader convenience.
* PM counters related to entry/exit are described in 5G\_L2\_5907\_replaced([11192279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28i12_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB009333-A]

* dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling is parameter read from NRBTS.NRDRB.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling for current bearer if drbDifferentiationEnabled (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_1862\_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to true and dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_397\_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for current bearer is set, otherwise it is read from NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_1862\_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* dtxMaxRetentionDelay is parameter read from NRBTS.NRDRB.dtxMaxRetentionDelay for current bearer if drbDifferentiationEnabled (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_1862\_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to true and dtxMaxRetentionDelay (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_397\_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for current bearer is set, otherwise it is read from NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxMaxRetentionDelay (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_1862\_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB009333-A]

---

##### 2.2.2.6.2.0-2 Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling UE exit from DTX optimized scheduling (ID: 11148077)

**2.2.2.6.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11148096`)

Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling
If TotalBufferedNonGbrData of the UE returns to 0 before dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer expiry thanks to co-scheduling (refer to 5G\_L2\_5951\_replaced([11148333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24QLufvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), this timer is stopped and the UE is no more assigned to dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class.

Otherwise, on dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer expiry [CB009333-A] for any bearer [End CB009333-A], UE is reassigned to drbTraffic request class to schedule remaining non-GBR data.

Refer to 5G\_L2\_5907\_replaced([11192279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28i12_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for pegging of related PM counters.

When Micro-DTX feature is disabled for CA active UEs as per 5G\_L2\_5926\_replaced([11148020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWkPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the first SCell of a UE is activated, a UE in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class is reassigned to drbTraffic request class and dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer is stopped.

Note that no reassignment takes place upon SCell deactivation of the last SCell.

[CB005788-B]

Note : UE's Data scheduling post DTX optimised scheduling may get delayed due to slot muting. An effect of slot muting could be such that UE's scheduling may or may not be delayed soon after its exit from from DTX optimized scheduling period (dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer expiry or timer stopped). This additional delay depends on the conditions governing the slot muting deicions.

[End CB005788-B]

---

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a timeline graph illustrating data transmission scenarios in a cellular network, specifically focusing on "dtx cycles" and data retention delays. The graph has two main axes: "PRB" (Physical Resource Block) on the y-axis, representing data units, and "t" (time) on the x-axis. Below the main graph, there's a section labeled "BS" (Base Station) which shows a stacked bar representing buffered data.

**Key elements and their interpretations based on the provided text:**
\* **dtx cycle N and dtx cycle N+1:** These represent distinct transmission cycles.
\* **dtxMaxRetentionDelay:** A blue arrow indicates the duration of this delay. Data received outside this delay is the subject of "Case 0".
\* **PRB Axis:** The height of the bars on the PRB axis indicates the amount of data.
\* **BS Section:** The light blue bar represents buffered non-GBR (non-Guaranteed Bit Rate) data. The lighter green bar on top of it represents newly received data.
**Numbered Events and their descriptions:**
1. **1st fresh non-gbr DRB data (totalBufferednonGbrData -> n octets); set to priority class prioDIDtzOptimizedDrbTraffic; start timer:** This event marks the arrival of new non-GBR data, which is then assigned a specific priority class and starts a timer. This is visually represented by the initial light blue bar in the BS section.
2. **dtxMaxRetentionDelay expires; promote to priority class prioDIDrbTraffic:** When the `dtxMaxRetentionDelay` expires, the data is promoted to a different priority class. This is indicated by the blue bars labeled '3' and '8'.
3. **UE scheduled; all data cannot be accomodated in one TB:** This signifies a situation where the User Equipment (UE) is scheduled for transmission, but the available Transmission Block (TB) is not large enough to carry all the buffered data. This is shown by the blue bar labeled '3'.
4. **New data received:** This event is represented by the green bar appearing on top of the light blue bar in the BS section, indicating additional data arriving.
5. **UE scheduled; all data can be accomodated in one TB; totalBufferednonGbrData -> 0:** Here, the UE is scheduled, and all the buffered data can fit into a single TB. This results in the buffered data count becoming zero. This is visually represented by the stacked bar labeled '5'.
6. **1st fresh non-gbr DRB data (totalBufferednonGbrData 0 -> n octets); put in priority class prioDIDtzOptimizedDrbTraffic; start timer:** Similar to event 1, this marks the arrival of new non-GBR data, assigned a priority, and a timer starts. This is shown by the upward arrow labeled '6' and the subsequent light blue bar in the BS section.
7. **dtxMaxRetention Delay expires; promote to priority class prioDIDrbTraffic:** Similar to event 2, the expiration of the retention delay leads to a priority promotion. This is indicated by the blue bar labeled '8'.
8. **UE scheduled; all data can be accomodated in one TB; totalBufferednonGbrData -> 0:** Similar to event 5, the UE is scheduled, all data fits in one TB, and the buffered data count resets to zero. This is represented by the blue bar labeled '8'.
The graph also shows "non-dtx cycle" periods, indicated by dashed lines, which are periods outside the dtx cycles. The overall scenario described is "data received outside a dtxMaxRetentionDelay cycle".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1148.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

**2.2.2.6.2.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11148159`)

**2.2.2.6.2.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11148169`)

Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling
Case VoIP data are received within a dtxMaxRetentionDelay cycle

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a scenario related to VoIP data reception within a Discontinuous Transmission (DTX) cycle. The diagram is divided into two main sections: "PRB" (Physical Resource Block) and "BS" (Base Station). A time axis "t" is shown at the bottom.
The "PRB" section displays stacked colored bars representing data scheduled at different times. The "BS" section shows a timeline with events marked by numbers and arrows, along with a shaded area representing buffered data.
The diagram also includes text annotations describing the events and states.
**Textual Information:**
\* **Title:** Case4a: VoIP data received within an already started dtx cycle
\* **Subtitle:** NOT all non-gbr data scheduled in VoNR slot

\* **DTX Cycles:** The diagram shows "dtx cycle N", "non-dtx cycle", and "dtx cycle N+1".
