\* **Events (Numbered Annotations):**
1. 1st fresh non-gbr DRB data (totalBufferednonGbrData 0 -> n octets); set to priority class prioDtxOptimizedDIDrbTraffic; start timer. This event is associated with a light blue shaded area in the BS section and a blue bar in the PRB section.
2. VoIP 5QI-1DRB data from same UE (totalBufferednonGbrData 0->m octets) received within dtxMaxRetentionDelay; next priority class = prioDIVoip Traffic OR prioDIDeprioritizedVoip. This event is associated with an orange bar in the BS section.
3. UE scheduled (TBS includes m + n-p user octets). This event is associated with a stacked blue and orange bar in the PRB section.
4. dtxMaxRetentionDelay expires; promote to priority class prioDIDrb Traffic. This is indicated by a dashed blue line extending from the end of the "dtxMaxRetentionDelay" arrow.
5. 2nd non-gbr DRB data received in non-dtx cycle. This event is associated with a light green bar in the BS section.
6. UE scheduled; all data can be accomodated in one TB. This event is associated with a stacked blue and green bar in the PRB section.
7. 1st fresh non-gbr DRB data (totalBufferednonGbrData 0-> n octets); set to priority class prioDIDtxOptimizedDrbTraffic; start timer. This event is associated with a light blue shaded area in the BS section.
8. the timer expires; next priority class = prioDIDrb Traffic. This is indicated by a dashed blue line extending from the end of the "dtxMaxRetentionDelay" arrow in the N+1 cycle.
9. UE scheduled; all data can be accomodated in one TB. This event is associated with a blue bar in the PRB section.

Case VoIP data are received within a dtxMaxRetentionDelay cycle

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a scenario of VoIP data reception within a Discontinuous Transmission (DTX) cycle, with non-guaranteed bit rate (non-gbr) data scheduled in a Voice over NR (VoNR) slot. The diagram uses a timeline with two axes: PRB (Physical Resource Block) and BS (Base Station).
The timeline is divided into DTX cycles and non-DTX cycles. The top part of the diagram shows the DTX cycle N and the subsequent non-DTX cycle, followed by DTX cycle N+1 and another non-DTX cycle. Arrows indicate the duration of `dtxMaxRetentionDelay` within DTX cycles N and N+1.
The bottom part of the diagram, labeled "BS", shows events occurring over time. There are numbered events and corresponding descriptions below the diagram.
**Events and Descriptions:**
1. **1st fresh non-gbr DRB data (totalBufferednonGbrData 0 -> n octets); set to priority class prioDtxOptimizedDIDrb Traffic; start timer**
This event is represented by a light blue bar on the BS axis, indicating the reception of non-gbr data. A timer is started.
2. **VoIP 5QI-1DRB data from same UE (totalBufferedGbrDataQci10->m octets) received within dtxMaxRetention Delay; next priority class = prioDIVoip Traffic OR prioDIDeprioritized Voip;**
This event is shown as an orange arrow pointing upwards, indicating the arrival of VoIP data. This data is received within the `dtxMaxRetentionDelay`.
3. **UE scheduled; all data can be accomodated in one TB (TB includes m + n user octets) => totalBufferedBytes (all classes) = 0**
This event is represented by a stacked bar on the PRB axis, with a dark blue section at the bottom and a brown section on top. This indicates that the UE is scheduled, and both the non-gbr and VoIP data can be accommodated in one Transport Block (TB). The total buffered bytes become zero after this scheduling.
4. **stop timer; enter non-DTX cycle**
This event is indicated by a blue dashed arrow pointing from the end of the stacked bar on the PRB axis towards the "non-dtx cycle" label. This signifies the stopping of the timer and the transition into a non-DTX cycle.
5. **1st fresh non-gbr DRB data (totalBufferednonGbrData 0 -> n octets); set to priority class prioDIDtxOptimizedDrbTraffic; start timer**
This event is represented by a light blue bar on the BS axis, similar to event 1, indicating the reception of new non-gbr data in DTX cycle N+1. A timer is started.
6. **the timer expires; next priority class = prioDIDrb Traffic**
This event is indicated by a red arrow pointing to the end of the `dtxMaxRetentionDelay` in DTX cycle N+1. This signifies the expiration of the timer.
7. **UE scheduled; all data can be accomodated in one TB**
This event is represented by a dark blue bar on the PRB axis, indicating that the UE is scheduled and data can be accommodated in one TB. This occurs after the timer expires.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1154.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

##### 2.2.2.6.2.0-4 Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling delay handling (ID: 11148225)

**2.2.2.6.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11148230`)

Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling
dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling delay handling - Pre scheduler part

---

**2.2.2.6.2.0-4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11148249`)

Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling
Upon reception of new BSR non-gbr\* DRB data

If  Conditions to assign UE to dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class are satisfied (refer to 5G\_L2\_5933\_replaced([11148047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24O9k_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) And If

dtxDelaySincelastScheduling > 0 (see note below)

Check buffer of non-gbr\* DRB data

If (totalBufferednonGbrData != 0) before reception of new BSR non-gbr\* DRB data

No change compared with current implementation

UE stays in current request class (either drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic)

Else

Check rrmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling

If rrmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling == undefined

Means rrmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling is not significant

No change compared with current implementation

UE enters in drbTraffic request class

Else

numSlot = current Xsfn – rrmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling

If numSlot < (dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling converted in slot)

Means data received within dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling

Enter in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class

Start dtxMaxRetentionDelay timer

Else

Means data received outside dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling

Continue with current implementation to select the right request class (UE will enter in drbTraffic request class)

EndIf

EndIf

EndIf

EndIf

(\*) non-gbr excluding 5QI5[CB008118-A]/69[End CB008118-A]

Notes:

dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling is parameter read from NRBTS.NRDRB.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling for current bearer if drbDifferentiationEnabled (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_1862\_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to true and dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_397\_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for current bearer is set, otherwise it is read from NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_1862\_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

**2.2.2.6.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11148256`)

Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling
dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling delay handling - Post-Pre scheduler part

---

**2.2.2.6.2.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11148262`)

Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling
After scheduling of non-gbr\* DRB data

Check buffer of non-gbr\* DRB data

If (totalBufferednonGbrData == 0)

rrmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling = current Xsfn

Else

rmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling = undefined

EndIf

(\*) non-gbr excluding 5QI5

Note: This processing is part of Post-Pre scheduler (refer to 5G\_L2\_5992\_replaced([11150839](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1MvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and is described here for the reader convenience.

Case 2: subsequent non-gbr data received after dtxDelaySincelastScheduling

**2.2.2.6.2.0-4.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11148328`)

Entry in and Exit from DTX optimized scheduling
Case 2: subsequent non-gbr data received after dtxDelaySincelastScheduling

#### 2.2.2.6.3 DTX optimized scheduling

##### 2.2.2.6.3.0-1 DTX optimized scheduling Co-scheduling with Physical Signals or Common Channels of the cell or with Delay sensitive UEs (ID: 11148338)

**2.2.2.6.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11148352`)

DTX optimized scheduling
There are two cases depending on the presence of UE(s) from request classes of higher priority than dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic (lowest priority) in CS1 list of current slot (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9471\_replaced([11175687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

-  In absence of higher priority UE(s), transmission of Physical Signals (SSB, CSI-RS for TRS) or Common Channels (SIB or Paging) may be required in this slot. UE(s) in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class could benefit from unused symbols or PRBs of the slot, so they are added to the empty CS1 list.

* In presence of higher priority UE(s), UEs in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class could be appended to the CS1 list for the same reason (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9471\_replaced([11175687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Although PUCCH allocation for UE of higher priority is guaranteed, it was discovered in late phase of the specifications that a retransmission could be discarded when composing the CS2 list due to insufficient number of REs in special slot (will be addressed as part of CB008662 Adaptative retransmission). Thus, it may be that only DTX UE(s) with small amount of PRBs are scheduled (current implementation in Pre-scheduler before composing CS2 list has not been changed in late phase of specifications considering the impact versus gain).

If the [Before CB009333-A] NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling [CB009333-A] dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling (see note below) [End CB009333-A] parameter is greater than 0, in presence of UE(s) receiving non-GNR data outside the delay since last scheduling (in drbTraffic request class), UE(s) in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class could be co-scheduled with this(those) UE(s) in drbTraffic request class as specified above for CB008238-B.

Notes:

Co-scheduling with higher priority request classes of same UE is implicit as Pre-scheduler only considers the request class of a UE with highest priority (refer to 5G\_L2\_226\_replaced([11147731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24NIYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In FD, allocated PRBs to this UE are distributed over request classes as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4538\_replaced([11185470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTexPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB009333-A]

dtxDelaySinceLastScheduling is parameter read from NRBTS.NRDRB.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling for current bearer if drbDifferentiationEnabled (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_1862\_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to true and dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_397\_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for current bearer is set, otherwise it is read from NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxDelaySincelastScheduling (see. 5G\_L2\_IF\_1862\_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB009333-A]

---

##### 2.2.2.6.3.0-2 DTX optimized scheduling Scheduling of Micro-DTX UE(s) able to fill up the slot (ID: 11148357)

**2.2.2.6.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11148364`)

DTX optimized scheduling
PRB threshold & CS1 threshold

---

**2.2.2.6.3.0-2.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11148394`)

DTX optimized scheduling
If UE(s) in dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class cannot be co-scheduled with other transmissions as per 5G\_L2\_5950\_replaced([11148338](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24QLuvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-PS need to assess the occupancy rate of the slot for these users as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9471\_replaced([11175687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The calculation of PRB load per BWP is only required when:

- All UEs in the cs1 List are assigned to dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic priority.

- The size of the CS1 list is less than to rdDtxCS1SizeThreshold (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9392\_replaced([11193397](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvsgVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Estimation of the number of available PRBs per dedicated DL BWP (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8238\_replaced([11175696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

The maximum numbers of available PRBs as per cell configuration, taking PRB blanking into account, are given by numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedPowerSavingDlBwp, numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedSmallDlBwp, numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedMidDlBwp and numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedLargeDlBwp.

The numbers of available PRBs need to be adjusted according to the budget periodically granted to the cell by the BBRM of the PRB pooling feature.

Note that these numbers may not be a multiple of the standard RBG size of the corresponding DL BWP.

Estimation of UE cumulated PRB demand and PRB load ratio per dedicated DL BWP:

All dedicated DL BWP are nested and the PRB demand in a BWP contributes to the PRB demand in the larger ones:

if(BW size of PowerSavingDlBwp(optional ) > BW size of )DedicatedSmallDlBwp(optional )

{

DedicatedSmallDlBwp(optional ) ⊂ PowerSavingDlBwp(optional ) ⊂ DedicatedMidDlBwp(optional ) ⊂ DedicatedLargeDlBwp.

}

else

{

PowerSavingDlBwp(optional ) ⊂ DedicatedSmallDlBwp(optional ) ⊂ DedicatedMidDlBwp(optional ) ⊂ DedicatedLargeDlBwp.

}

Low ends of each dedicated DL BWP are aligned on a common CRB (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1809\_replaced([11110718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpHXNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) so corresponding CSS (Common Search Space) are mapped on a common PRB range with the same size as the CORESET(0) size, included in the smallest dedicated DL BWP.

Therefore, any UE that is granted with a DCI Format 1\_0 into CSS of any dedicated BWP (transient phase of RRC reconfiguration) contributes to the PRB demand of the smallest BWP and larger ones with a granularity of one PRB.

Any other UE contributes to the PRB demand of its active BWP and larger ones with a granularity equal to the RBG size of its active BWP (the RBG on upper edge of the BW may be smaller than regular ones).

The PRB load ratio of a DL BWP is the ratio between the cumulated PRB demand across all UEs with corresponding active DL BWP and the number of available PRBs in this BWP.

The CS1 list content is emptied if the PRB load ratio is lower than NRBTS/NRCELL/dtxOptimizedScheduler.dtxPrbThreshold in each configured dedicated DL BWP.

Detailed computation of cptPrbDemand[] and NbPrbAvailable[]:

nbPrbAvailable[powerSavingBwp]= numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedPowerSavingDlBwp

nbPrbAvailable[smallBwp] = numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedSmallDlBwp

nbPrbAvailable[midBwp] = numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedMidDlBwp

nbPrbAvailable[largeBwp] = numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedLargeDlBwp

cptrPrbDemand[TransitionPhase] = 0;       // Ues in transition phase processing

for ixBwp Є { powerSavingBwp , smallBwp , midBwp, largeBwp}

{

if ((actSlowPrbPooling() = true) or (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = true)){

nbPrbAvailable[ixBwp] = min( nbPrbAvailable[ixBwp], cell.bbrm().numAllocCellPrbDl() )}

[CB012605-E]

if (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = true)

{nbPrbAvailable[ixBwp] = min( nbPrbAvailable[ixBwp], cell.bbrm().numAllocCellLayerPrbDl())}

[End CB012605-E]

cptrPrbDemand[ixBwp] = 0;

}

for each Ue[i] in cs1list

{

If (Ue[i].isUsingForceDCIFormat()= true)

cptrPrbDemand[TransitionPhase] += nbPrb(Ue[i])

else

{

for ixBwp Є { powerSavingBwp > smallBwp? smallBwp : powerSavingBwp, smallBwp > powerSavingBwp ? smallBwp : powerSavingBwp, idBwp, argeBwp}

{

If ( ixBwp = index of active BWP of Ue[i])

cptrPrbDemand[ixBwp] += (nbPrb(Ue[i]) rounding to upper multiple of RbgSize of this Bwp)

}

}

}

if(BW size of PowerSavingDlBwp(optional ) > BW size of )DedicatedSmallDlBwp(optional )

{

cprtPrbdemand[smallBwp] +=  cptrPrbDemand[TransitionPhase];

cptrPrbDemand[powerSavingBwp] += cprtPrbdemand[smallBwp];

cprtPrbdemand[midBwp]  +=  cptrPrbDemand[powerSavingBwp];

cptrPrbdemand[largeBwp] += cptrPrbdemand[midBwp];

}

else

{

if ( actPowerSavingBwp == true)

{

cptrPrbDemand[powerSavingBwp] += cptrPrbDemand[TransitionPhase];

}

cprtPrbdemand[smallBwp]  +=  cptrPrbDemand[powerSavingBwp];

cprtPrbdemand[midBwp]  +=  cptrPrbDemand[smallBwp];

cptrPrbdemand[largeBwp] += cptrPrbdemand[midBwp];

}

if (cptrPrb[powerSavingBwp] >=  dtxPrbThreshold *nbPrbAvailable[powerSavingBwp]/100) or (cptrPrb[smallBwp] >= dtxPrbThreshold* nbPrbAvailable[smallBwp]/100) or  if midBwp is configured (cptrPrb[midBwp] >= dtxPrbThreshold *nbPrbAvailable[midBwp]/100) or (cptrPrb[largBwp] > = dtxPrbThreshold* nbPrbAvailable[largeBwp]/100)

{

All Ues stays in CS1List  (nothing to do)

}

Else

{

Cs1List will be emptied

}

Note: this has been implemented as part of Pre-scheduler for simplification purpose considering initial requirements.

Note: if actPowerSavingBwp = FALSE, numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedPowerSavingDlBwp = numUsablePrbForRbgsInDedicatedLargeDlBwp

if actMultipleDedicatedBWPs = FALSE, smallBwp = largeBwp = midBwp.

---

Typical scenarios: PRB threshold & CS1 threshold

---

##### 2.2.2.6.3.0-3 DTX optimized scheduling Request class switching of UEs with the dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class (ID: 11148453)

**2.2.2.6.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11148459`)

DTX optimized scheduling
When UE with the dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic request class has pending UL RLC Status PDU data, indicated for any of non-GBR DRB by IE isUlRlcStatusPdu from LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_874\_replaced([10984647](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBxx_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rlcStatusPduSupportEnabled (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_1862\_replaced([10969923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgHwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is enabled, then this UE is considered as UE with delay sensitive user data (see 5G\_UP\_4682\_replaced([11348297](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubUL5fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) but no dedicated request class is created.

UE shall then be set temporarily to the appropriate request class, until indication isUlRlcStatusPdu is stopped, but related DTX optimized scheduling timers shall not be stopped.

---

### 2.2.2.7 Slot blanking due to RF high temperature

### 2.2.2.7-1 Slot blanking due to RF high temperature

**2.2.2.7-1.0-5**  (ID: `13447338`)

Slot blanking due to RF high temperature
The TD scheduler shall determine the set of UEs that require the first transmission of DRB data(including NBR in case of NBR bearer). DRB traffic resource request class has two sub categories:  CP2 reference : 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4178\_replaced([11174242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuaG5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If NRCELL.actNbrForNonGbrBearers = TRUE  or NRCELL.actLargeBufferUe , DRB Traffic class shall be further subcategorized as NBR category, subBandBfUeInPG, LargeBufferUe and normal nonGBR category. To facilitate this subcategorization L2-PS software shall add additional priority index nbrDrbTraffic(in addition to existing drbTraffic) to account for NBR category. drbTraffic, subBandBfUeInPG, LargeBufferUe and nbrDrbTraffic shall be under DRB Traffic class. The following table gives the corelation between resource request class and priority index.

The above CP2 requirement will be implemented in L2PS SW as two seperate priority index values that shall be used to differentiate  DRB bearer (NBR and Drb/normal non GBR bearer). This priority indexes are still under same drbTraffic resource request class.

As mentioned in requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4178\_replaced([11174242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuaG5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) TD scheduler shall determine the set of UEs that require first transmission of data(in this case NBR bearer) if there is pending data in DL buffer.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Resource Request Class** | **Priority Index** | **Priority Index****Value**\*\*\*\* |
| rachMsg2 | rachMsg2 | 0 |
| harqTransMsg4 | harqRetxMsg4 | 1 |
| [CB015279-A] pdcchOrder [End CB015279-A] | [CB015279-A] pdcchOrder [End CB015279-A] | Below Priority Index Value is increased by 1 in order, start from 0 - rachMsg2. Note that one Resource Request Class” defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9891\_replaced([11174018](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuYRsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) may mapping to multiple Priority Indexs. |
| harqRetransSrb1 | harqRetxsrb1 |  |
| harqRetransSrb3 | harqRetxsrb3 |  |
| harqRetransSrb2 | harqRetxsrb2 |  |

#### 2.2.2.7.0-1 Slot blanking due to RF high temperature Priority handling for slot blanking (ID: 11148470)

**2.2.2.7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148478`)

Slot blanking due to RF high temperature
The definition of " Priority traffic " is as indicated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18294\_replaced([11175117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Also means " non-Priority traffic " is everything else which is not listed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18294\_replaced([11175117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Priority handling is applied as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18285\_replaced([11175107](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) such that if the current slot contains scheduling requests for Priority traffic, L2-PS shall consider the slot as ' non-mutable ' and proceed with normal scheduling of DL traffic on PDSCH.

Otherwise if there is no presence of priority traffic and all the scheduling request is only for non-priority traffic, then the slot becomes eligible for muting. If the other conditions mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18285\_replaced([11175107](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are also fulfilled, then the slot is muted and no data on PDSCH is scheduled.

Note :

1. If the current slot has the mix of priority and non-priority traffic scheduling request, then slot is non-mutable and hence no restriction imposed on scheduling.

---

#### 2.2.2.7.0-2 Slot blanking due to RF high temperature Priority mapping for slot blanking (ID: 11148485)

**2.2.2.7.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12745486`)

Slot blanking due to RF high temperature
L2-PS shall compute priorty and subpriority for UE data as per 5G\_L2\_223\_replaced([11147688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24MhWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). As indicated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18294\_replaced([11175117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for single and multi-cell cases whever applicable, the priority traffic can be classified into below mentioned categories.

Non-UE specific traffic : SSB/refinement beam, SIB1, OSI, Paging, CSI-RS, TRS, RIM-RS

UE specific traffic : RACH MSG2/MSG4, HARQ retransmission, MAC CE, DL SRB data, GBR, Voip

Note :

1. GBR includes Voip traffic. Hence Voip traffic is always considered as priority traffic from slot muting point of view. Follow allowGbrForSlotMuting configuration to treat GBR and Voip as priority or non-priority traffic for slot muting purposes.
2. deprioritizedVoip and deprioritizedGBR are always considered as non-priority traffic from slot muting point of view
3. All types of CSI-RS is considered as priority traffic from slot muting point of view
4. Paging with Short message is considered as non-Priority traffic since it uses only PDCCH resources (does not use PDSCH resources). Refer 5G\_UP\_267\_replaced([11348157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubS9xvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
5. RACH messages[04800820](Check next point to know the priority of RACH messages Msg2/Msg4) [End 04800820], HARQ retransmissions, DL SRB data are not considered as priority traffic for Multi-cell case. This in combination with allowGbrMutingForRfCooling = false creates a priority inversion condition such that GBR traffic is prioritized over these traffic for slot muting purposes. Its recommended to keep allowGbrMutingForRfCooling = true in multi-cell cases but its still a valid configuration with allowGbrMutingForRfCooling = false resulting in RACH messages, HARQ retransmissions, DL SRB data getting deprioritized over GBR for slot muting.

[04800820]

1. RACH messages Msg2/Msg4 are indicated as priority traffic for multi cell case as per [11175117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_KI7Z4fvOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). However L2-PS uses an RnD parameter 'rdProritizeRachMsg2Msg4' (Refer [12744547](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_2MgiAH0iEfCiUemk-K-C4g)) to further decide the priority as indicated below

rdProritizeRachMsg2Msg4 = 1 (true) -> Implies that RACH messages Msg2/Msg4 are treated as priority traffic

rdProritizeRachMsg2Msg4 = 0 (false) -> Implies that RACH messages Msg2/Msg4 are treated as non-priority traffic

[End 04800820]

---

## 2.2.3 TD Scheduler

### 2.2.3.0-1 TD Scheduler FA: [Internal Domain] TD-Scheduler Document Owner: TBD (KRK) (ID: 11148526)

### 2.2.3.1 Definition of per UE and per subcell scheduling metric for DL

#### 2.2.3.1.0-1 Definition of per UE and per subcell scheduling metric for DL Updating the average 5G UE DL Data Rate (ID: 11148538)

**2.2.3.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11148557`)

Definition of per UE and per subcell scheduling metric for DL
L2-PS SW shall calculate rrmAvgDlUeDataRate\_BytesPerSlot[i,t] for a given UE i following the procedure described below:

* When the DL TD-Scheduler has to calculate the PF metric for the UE and serving cell i.e. UE is a candidate with priority drbTraffic [CB008238-A] or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic [End CB008238-A] in the serving cell, it first checks whether rrmAvgDlUeDataRate\_BytesPerSlot[i, t-1] has to be updated by either a (re-)initialization or by an aging. In which cases either of these operations is required is specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4243\_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IF( (re-)initialization is required )

{

rrmAvgDlUeDataRate\_BytesPerSlot[i, t-1] = rrmAvgDlUeDataRate\_BytesPerSlot[i, 0], where rrmAvgDlUeDataRate\_BytesPerSlot[i, 0] is calculated as per formula in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4243\_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

rrmLastTimeUeDlAvgRateWasUpdated = rrmScheduledXSfn - 1;

}

ELSE

{

rrmAvgDlUeDataRate\_BytesPerSlot[i, t-1] is aged using the formula in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4243\_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with: rrmNumSlotSinceLastDlSched = (rrmScheduledXSfn - 1 - rrmLastTimeUeDlAvgRateWasUpdated) and rrmDlSumOfTransportBlockSize = 0;

rrmLastTimeUeDlAvgRateWasUpdated = rrmScheduledXSfn - 1;

}

Note: If the re-initialization due to rdAvgDataRateReinitProhibitTimer doesn’t kicks in (because the time when UE has no data in any DRB buffer was shorter than rdAvgDataRateReinitProhibitTimer), rrmAvgDlUeDataRate\_BytesPerSlot is aged considering also the time when UE has no data in any DRB buffer. This deviation from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4243\_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shouldn’t have a negative impact on the fairness as this time is anyway short.

* At the end of the scheduling process:

IF(the UE has been scheduled with priority drbTraffic [CB008238-A] or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic [End CB008238-A] in any DL serving cell)

{

rrmAvgDlUeDataRate\_BytesPerSlot[i, t] is updated using the formula in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4243\_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with: rrmNumSlotSinceLastDlSched = 1 and rrmDlSumOfTransportBlockSize calculated as sum of the TBSs allocated to the UE for new transmissions in the current TTI;

rrmLastTimeUeDlAvgRateWasUpdated = rrmScheduledXSfn;

}

where rrmScheduledXSfn is the extended SFN (SFN \* Nslotsframe,μ + slot) under consideration for scheduling. Nslotsframe,μ is the number of slots in one radio frame (see table 4.3.2-1 in 38.211).

Above processing is also applicable accordingly with multi DRBs on the UE, in the case that new DL BSR indicates BS change to BS > 0 for one or several DRBs.

* When one or several DRBs are added to or are deleted from the UE the PF Metric in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4232\_replaced([11175151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0nPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the average DL data rate according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4243\_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are processed as described above.
* When one or several DRBs with different scheduling weights are added to or are deleted from the UE the PF Metric in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4232\_replaced([11175151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0nPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the average DL data rate in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4243\_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are processed above.

Note: In case of activation of non-GBR service differentiation during run-time of a UE existing bearers keep their existing scheduling weights, only new bearers will be setup with new weights. The new bearers enter the above calculations with their new weights provided in bearer setup procedure.

---

#### 2.2.3.1.0-2 Definition of per UE and per subcell scheduling metric for DL Updating the average 5G UE DL Data Rate for Power Saving BWP switch (ID: 11148565)

**2.2.3.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11148572`)

Definition of per UE and per subcell scheduling metric for DL
[Before CNI-73045]

L2-PS measures the Average DL Data rate for the UE as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4243\_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It also is updated when UE enters CandidateSet1 list during PF Metric Calculation in TD Scheduler which takes into account the aging calculation and reduces average DL data rate. This is done based on gap between the current Slot and the last slot when it was scheduled.

During the measurement measurementDurationPsBwp period for BWP switch between larger and PS BWPs, accumulate the Average DL data rate values when the UE gets scheduled and calculate the average DL throughout at the end of measurementDurationPsBwp period. This DL throughput is to be used for evaluation purpose to consider the UE to be eligible for a BWP switch. The average throughput calculation is done by taking into account average of average Dl data rate. This is computed without considering the aging factor, which implies that we apply previous dl data rate to unscheduled slots to increase sample size. At the end of each measurement period, this value is reset and new average of average value is computed which will be used in the current measurement period.

[CNI-73045]

Average DL Data rate rrmAvgDlUeDataRate\_BytesPerSlotForBwpSwitch for BWP switch is computed as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1874\_replaced([11111241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLop_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4243\_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) only when the UE's scheduling class is in DRB priority.

[End CNI-73045]

---

#### 2.2.3.2 UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account

##### 2.2.3.2.0-1 UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account Skip of DL FD-Scheduling for Component Carriers in FR2 (ID: 11148585)

**2.2.3.2.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11148609`)

UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account
In FR2, before starting the DL FD Scheduler processing for the next carrier, L2-PS shall check the remaining time till the end of the slot. If the time left is lower than a configured margin T, L2-PS shall drop the DL FD Scheduling for all the remaining CCs, i.e. nothing is scheduled on those carriers.

By doing this L2-PS shall furthermore guarantee that it’s not always the same CCs that are dropped.

The margin T [Before CNI-134375] is set to rdFdSchedLateThresholdFR2 (5G\_L2\_22738\_replaced([11181877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XKGfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if DL FD scheduler is executed in DL scheduler EO (i.e. DL FD scheduler not run in a separate EO). It [End CNI-134375] is set to rdFdSchedLateThresholdForFdEo (5G\_L2\_22762\_replaced([11181911](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XxIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if FD scheduler is run in a separate EO.

The main purpose of this is to prevent sending late DlData\_ messages to L1-DL which, with current design, can get stuck if it receives late messages and cause a sleeping cell.

CP2 reference(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4101\_replaced([11173728](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuV1dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) DL Scheduling of 5G UEs per L2 PS instance with traffic prioritization

---

##### 2.2.3.2.0-2 UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account Carrier based scheduling according to priority (ID: 11148616)

**2.2.3.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11148628`)

UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account
The order how the Component Carriers are selected for the FD-Scheduling is left to implementation.

CP2 reference(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4258\_replaced([11175719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Composing CS2 list

##### 2.2.3.2.0-3 UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account Handling of DL Re-Transmissions requiring more PDSCH symbols than are available in the current slot (ID: 11148634)

**2.2.3.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11148653`)

UE Selection and subcell / carrier assignment taking the Prioritization and Sub-Prioritization Concept of Resource Requests into account
If the number of PDSCH symbols used in the initial transmission exceeds the number of available PDSCH symbols in the considered slot:

For a FDD cell which is shared with LTE and actLteNrDssLteCatM equals true:

UE is still allowed to be added to CS2 list.

For a FDD/TDD(FR1) cell and actAdaptiveReTxResMcs equals true:

UE is still allowed to be added to CS2 list.

For any other cases

then the re-transmission gets an invalid TD metric value ('Nothing to do' in L2-PS SW) leading to ignore that resource request for the current slot

[CNI-92005-23R2]

For the available PDSCH symbols determination, the mute of last sysmbol shall be considered for SSB slot in case of muteLastSymbolInSSBSlot !=0.

IF "muteLastSymbolInSSBSlot == 1(Muting of last DL symbol only in SSB slot 0)"  AND "current is SSB slot 0" AND "no CsiRs in last sysmbol":

Last PDSCH symbol is muted and exclude from available PDSCH symbols.

ELSE IF "muteLastSymbolInSSBSlot == 2(Muting of last DL symbol in all SSB slots)"  AND "current is SSB slot" AND "no CsiRs in last sysmbol":

Last PDSCH symbol is muted and exclude from available PDSCH symbols.

END

Note, muteLastSymbolInSSBSlot is NIDD parameter and received in PsCell\_CellSetupReq, refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CNI-92005-23R2]

CP2 reference(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4258\_replaced([11175719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Composing CS2 list

### 2.2.3.3 FR2 DL Event-based PF Metric Calculation

#### 2.2.3.3.1 Overview

##### 2.2.3.3.1.0-1 Overview Overview of event-based PF Metric calculation (ID: 11148671)

**2.2.3.3.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148678`)

Overview
In order to further decrease the CPU cost in beam selection procedure when there are multiple UEs and multiple carriers for FR2, event-based PF metric calculation is introduced. Now for each UE in priority list with DRB priority class the PF metric will not be calculated in each DL slot any more as before, instead such UEs will only update PF metric with a relative ratio in idle slot, meanwhile for those UEs which have received the PF metric event, their PF metric would be calculated in the next DL slot based on current DL data rate, average DL data rate and UE scheduling weight. The PF metric events are those events triggered asynchronously which would impact DL UE data rate calculation, the description of each kind of specific event could refer to 5G\_L2\_13387\_replaced([11148685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Sn8PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The UE DL average data rate will also need to be updated according to the relative ratio in idle slot or the slot when UE gets the DL grant.

Following figure is an example of event-based PF metric calculation with 5GC001227 frame structure, assuming that currently there are three UEs in the priority list with DRB priority class:

 UE-1  There’s no PF metric event triggered from slot 10 to slot 19, so PF metric will only be updated in idle slot with *relative ratio and* last updated PF metric.\*\*

 UE-2  There’s one PF metric event triggered in slot 11, so in next DL slot the PF metric is calculated based on DL data rate and UE scheduling weight, then in UL slot 14 the PF metric is updated with PF metric of slot 2 and *relative ratio.*

 UE-3  There is no PF metric event triggered from slot 10 to 13, so in UL slot 14 PF metric is updated with *last updated PF metric and* relative ratio. In slot 16, UE gets DL grant, then the average DL data rate will be updated in post scheduler and then one PF metric event will be triggered, so in slot 17 PF metric calculation will be done due to event, in UL slot 19 the PF metric is updated with PF metric of slot 17 and *relative ratio.*\*\*

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a screenshot of a spreadsheet that visualizes a timeline of events for three different User Equipments (UEs) across various time slots. The timeline is divided into slots, labeled from 10 to 19, with a header indicating "SFN 15". Below the timeline, there are rows for UE-1, UE-2, and UE-3. Each row details events and calculations related to these UEs within specific time slots. The events are described in text and often accompanied by formulas or metric calculations.

| **UE-1 Row** | UE-1 in priority list and with DRB priority class but has no DL grant | pfMetric\_slot[14]= pfMetric\_slot[9]/(1-K)^5   avgUeDataRate\_slot[14]= avgUeDataRate\_slot[9] \* (1-K)^5 | UE-1 in priority list and with DRB priority class but has no DL grant   pfMetric\_slot[19]= pfMetric\_slot[14]/(1-K)^5   avgUeDataRate\_slot[19]= avgUeDataRate\_slot[14] \* (1-K)^5 |
| **UE-2 Row** | UE-2 in priority list and with DRB priority class receives pfMetric event at slot 11 | pfMetric event triggered (e.g. MCS, Rank, ...) | pfMetric\_slot[14]= pfMetric\_slot[12]/(1-K)^5   avgUeDataRate\_slot[14]= avgUeDataRate\_slot[9] \* (1-K)^5 |

Link to "Event-based PF metric calculation":

<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20L2%20Entity%20Level/2%205G-L2-PS%20Component%20Requirements/2.2%20DL%20Scheduler/event-based%20PF%20metric%20calculation.xlsx?d=wf9dbdbb5f1e2436c84d4eb020f7594b0&csf=1&web=1&e=Wl5tjr>

Note:

1) K is a R&D parameter as filter coefficient, the definition could refer to 5G\_L2\_1023\_replaced([11181966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XxK_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

2) For the relative ratio used for PF metric and average data rate update, the binomial formula expression (1 – K) ^ N could use (1 – N \* K) as approximation in implementation when K is a small value.

3) The idle slot in this paragraph means the slot in which the DL scheduler won’t do DL scheduling job.

4) For current DL data rate, average DL data rate, and TBS(Transport Block Size), the definition could refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4242\_replaced([11175309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4243\_replaced([11175317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuiCuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5) The UE scheduling weight could refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9885\_replaced([11175183](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuhbofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.2.3.3.2 PF Metric Calculation Trigger Events

##### 2.2.3.3.2.0-1 PF Metric Calculation Trigger Events List of events that trigger PF Metric calculation (ID: 11148692)

**2.2.3.3.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148697`)

PF Metric Calculation Trigger Events
FR2 DL PF Metric calculation is triggered by following event:

 BSR is received and traffic flow not suspended and bufferedBytes > 0;

 SCell handle activate decision with SCellActivationCmdType = DECISION\_ACTIVATE\_CMD;

 SCell process one CSI report periodic from Remote PCell,and csiType == cqiPmiRi;

 L2-PS process remote SCell CSI report on local PCell when new CsiRs Report is received;

 L2-PS process CQI report, If rd4x4MimoRAEnabled(See 5G\_L2\_1265\_replaced([11186618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_277KwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) != 0 and rrmNumOfLayers is updated;

 Update average Ue data rate on scheduled Ues in post TD scheduler(See 5G\_L2\_7304\_replaced([11150856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1NfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 2.2.3.3.3 Update PF Metric In Idle Slot

##### 2.2.3.3.3.0-1 Update PF Metric In Idle Slot Update UE's DL PF metric in priority lists (ID: 11148712)

**2.2.3.3.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148717`)

Update PF Metric In Idle Slot
If current slot is idle slot, FR2 TDD UE's DL PF metric and average data rate will be updated.

1, Update Relative Ratio

relative ratio = (1 – K) ^ slotNumber;

K is rdAvgDlUeDataRateFilterConst(See 5G\_L2\_1023\_replaced([11181966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XxK_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

slotNumber is number of slots since the last update of PF.

Note:

1) This relative ratio is used for DL average data rate update.

2)  For the relative ratio, the formula expression (1 – K) ^ N could use (1 – N \* K) as approximation in implementation when K is a small value.

2, Update Pf metric in priority list when no Scheduling

Loop all the UE in priority list,  UE’s PF metric will be updated one by one based on last updated PF metric and an increased relative ratio.

increased relative ratio = 1/ (1 – K) ^ slotNumber;

K is rdAvgDlUeDataRateFilterConst(See 5G\_L2\_1023\_replaced([11181966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XxK_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))).

slotNumber is number of slots since the last update of PF.

Note:

For the increased relative ratio, the formula expression 1/(1- K) ^ N could use (1 + N \* K) as approximation in implementation when K is a small value.

3, Reset relative ratio

Reset relative ratio to 0;

---

#### 2.2.3.3.4 PF Metric calculation triggered by PF metric event

##### 2.2.3.3.4.0-1 PF Metric calculation triggered by PF metric event PF Metric Calculation (ID: 11148727)

**2.2.3.3.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11148739`)

PF Metric calculation triggered by PF metric event
1. When there are PF metric event triggered for UE, this UE will be recorded in PfMetricUpdateUes data structure.

2. In each DL slot, for those UEs which receive PF metric event and have DRB priority class, their PF metric will be calculated one by one based on the formula described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4232\_replaced([11175151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kug0nPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

3. After PF metric calculation is done, all the UEs with PF metric event in PfMetricUpdateUes will be cleared.

4. The new updated PF metric will be stored and used for beam selection procedure as before.

[CB012734-D] If actHighNumberOfUEs is true and rdActSinglePfMetricPerUeOnLoad is true and totalActiveUeLoad >= rdSinglePfMetricPerUeThreshold then the PF metric is calculated only for PCell and the resulting value is stored for the PCell and each SCell, otherwise the PF metric is calculated for each serving cell (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26820\_replaced([11175784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kultG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB012734-D]

---

### 2.2.3.4 FDM scheduling

#### 2.2.3.4.0-1 FDM scheduling Overview (ID: 11148752)

**2.2.3.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148756`)

FDM scheduling
in FR1, FDM is used to improve capacity by:

1) Improve PRB allocation such as resource usage is adapted to traffic needs (ie instead of using all the band).

2) Introduce frequency multiplexing of multiple users.

The algorithm is composed of two main steps:

1) UE selection: this step is responsible of finding UEs with all conditions to be multiplexed in same slot.

2) Resource Allocation: this step is responsible of resource allocation/distribution to UEs selected in previous step.

---

#### 2.2.3.4.1 UE selection

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-2 UE selection PDSCH availibility checking (ID: 11148772)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13134080`)

UE selection
Pdsch availability checking is done depending on type of scheduling.

For SRB, 5QI1/5**/65/66/69, retransmissions available PDSCH should ensure a certain amount of predefined resources. In that case not only availability is done but also reservation of these resources (assuming that all other checks ie PDCCH/PUCCH…are passed) ie I know how much I need and I have enough resource for UE. Then UE will continue other checks and UE will be given already at this step PDSCH resources that it is asking for (exact position is not decided just the amount of available PDSCH resource will be reduced by what was given for selected UE). If there is no enough resources to satisfy the UE or other checks fails then UE will not be selected and no reduction of PDSCH resource.**

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a diagram with the label "BWP" on the left. To the right of the label, there are two horizontal bars. The top bar is divided into two sections: a light blue section on the left and a white section on the right. Below the top bar, there is a solid red bar. The red bar is positioned such that it overlaps with the right portion of the white section of the top bar. A black "X" symbol is superimposed on the overlapping area of the red bar and the white section of the top bar, indicating a cancellation or exclusion.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1246.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

In picture above it’s an example of UE selection for a BWP where UE in blue is SRB all other checks passed then the amount of available resource in white is not enough to select another UE in red. Red UE is SRB too and is asking more resources than available, so it’s not selected.

[CB014474-C]

If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = True,

When a UE is High reliable capable, reserve resources for GBR bearer(not applicable for VoNR bearers) in FDM reservation phase based on [[12689358](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_4trMsVZeEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_4trmsvzeefc45ikmrv0u7q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")].

When a UE is High reliable capable and if only MAC-CE need to be scheduled for the UE in the slot, minimum resource reservation (rdMinPrbForRat1AllocHrDrb) is not applied.

If the available PRB for scheduling is lesser than rdMinPrbForRat1AllocHrDrb , then the minimum resource reservation is not applied

Note: Minimum resource reservation (rdMinPrbForRat1AllocHrDrb) for a multi bearer High Reliable (HR) UE is applied per Transport Block though the HR UE may have multiple HRLA enabled DRB's or one HRLA enabled bearer and other bearers are non-HRLA enabled.

[End CB014474-C]

In other cases, initial transmission other than SRB or 5QI1/5**[CB008118-A]/65/66/69**[End CB008118-A] then there is no condition on minimum resources to allocate for UE.  So, check consist of ensuring that there is at least one PDSCH resource to give if UE is selected. Exact amount of resource will be decided in resource allocation step.\*\*\*\*

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, there is a special case in which we can only reserve the lastPartialRbg of a different size instead of a normal size rbg (even if it is available), due to layerPrb constraints.

In this case, we need to ensure that the UE for which the lastPartialRbg is reserved, is also scheduled.

---

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-3 UE selection L1-DL subcell availability checking enhancement for ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_8x4 (ID: 11148807)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11148813`)

UE selection
To carry out the L1-DL subcell availability checking as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4306\_replaced([11177427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuveEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), for each CS2 UE candidate, L2-PS shall additionally taken UE’s DL beam type into consideration as listed below if dlMimoMode is set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4:

 For each X-Pol beam, UE selection can only happen with the same beam type, that is, either within SSB/refined beam or within PMI beam, but never between SSB/refined beam and PMI beam

 For the first UE selection per subcell per X-pol beam, UE is eligible for scheduling no matter it is SSB/refined beam based (i.e. rrmDlBeam::isPmiBeam == FALSE) or PMI beam based (i.e. rrmDlBeam::isPmiBeam == TRUE)

 For the following UE selection per subcell per X-pol beam, UE is only eligible when it has the same beam type as the first UE

 In case of default SSB/refined beam being used for PDCCH/PDSCH scheduling (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3188\_replaced([11139322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), only primary SSB/refined beam (which is always the best beam) shall to be considered.

CP2 references: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4306\_replaced([11177427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuveEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4309\_replaced([11177456](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuveFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-4 UE selection PDCCH availibility checking (ID: 11148818)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11148828`)

UE selection
PDCCH availability checking is performed to ensure that there is enough available CCEs to carry the DL grant.

If UE is transmitting in initial BWP or it’s in transient phase the pdcchResourceManagerCommonBwp will be used to search available resource. If UE is transmitting in dedicated BWP the pdcchResourceManagerDedicatedBwp will be used to search available resource.

In case UE is in dedicated BWP the search of available resource is performed with search space type 1 and the corresponding AL. In case UE is in dedicated BWP the search of available resource is performed with search space type 3 or UeSpecific and the corresponding AL (AL can be dynamic ie depends of UE’s radio conditions).

Search space will point to the coreset associated to the BWP on which UE should be scheduled. CCEs are checked in the coreset at predefined position between startCCE and (StartCCE + AL).  StartCCE is computed according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4090\_replaced([11170944](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBFWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  and AL is defined according to req 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4055\_replaced([11170246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) UE search space according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4036\_replaced([11168496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktwmofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Once a PDDCH allocation is done in one coreset it should pre-empt CCEs in all coresets in same BWP or in other BWPs 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4032\_replaced([11169907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). In picture bellow Pdcch resources were allocated in coreset0 (yellow) then resources that are will be marked as not available red will not be used in coreset1.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays two rows of rectangular cells, each containing text labels. The top row has eight cells labeled "Cce0" through "Cce7". The first four cells ("Cce0" to "Cce3") are highlighted in yellow. To the right of this row, the text "coreset 0" is displayed with a dashed red underline.
The second row also has eight cells labeled "Cce0" through "Cce7". The last two cells ("Cce6" and "Cce7") in this row are highlighted in red. To the right of this row, the text "coreset 1" is displayed with a dashed red underline.
The overall arrangement suggests a representation of two sets, "coreset 0" and "coreset 1", each composed of eight elements labeled "Cce0" to "Cce7". The coloring indicates a distinction or status for certain elements within these sets.

| coreset 0 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Cce0 (Yellow) | Cce1 (Yellow) | Cce2 (Yellow) | Cce3 (Yellow) | Cce4 | Cce5 | Cce6 | Cce7 |

| Cce0 | Cce1 | Cce2 | Cce3 | Cce4 | Cce5 | Cce6 (Red) | Cce7 (Red) |

iif CCEs are not available for any occasion then UE is not kept further in the to\_be\_scheduled list.

---

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-5 UE selection PUCCH availibility checking (ID: 11148833)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11148847`)

UE selection
Pucch availability is performed only for DL. It ensure that there is available resources to carry the HARQ ACK of DL grant on PUCCH.

PUCCH resource is of size of 1 PRB to carry up to two ACKs (Format 0 for short PUCCH or Format1 for long PUCCH). For more than 2 ACKs PUCCH size should up to 16 PRBs (format 2 if short PUCCH or format 3 for long PUCCH).

PUCCH resources (up to 8 per Ue) are configured by CPRT at call setup (via RRC for UE and Ue setup for L2PS) configuration of resources contains : starting PRB, size and symbols ...

PUCCH allocator must find radio resources (among those configured for Ue) that are available ie are not already used by an other UE. If none of resources confugured for ue is available at current slot+K1 [CB008294-H]or current slot + K1 for Msg4 A/N (5G\_L2\_549\_replaced([11156818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25CO0PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if 5G-L2-PS is scheduling Msg4 (RaState of UE is scheduleMsg4WithoutDlCcchData or scheduleMsg4WithDlCcchData)[End CB008294-H] then UE is not kept further in to\_be\_scheduled list.

PUCCH allocator should also consider upgrading of format if for example UE has already 2 Acks then 3rd Ack should be added which means that allocator must find F2 or F3 instead of F0 or F1.

PUCCH allocator manages also multiplexing of PUCCH for CSI report with Ack.

---

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-6 UE selection High buffer UE prioritization (ID: 12707543)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13252161`)

UE selection
When NRBTS/NRCELL/actTdHighBufUEPrio is DL or DL\_UL, the following algorithm shall be apply to select high-buffer UEs firstly among Non-GBR UEs in CS2 list.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating the process of adding high-buffer User Equipments (UEs) into a "To-be-scheduleList". The flowchart starts with a "Start" node and proceeds through various decision points and process steps.
Here's a breakdown of the flowchart:
1. **Start**: The process begins.
2. **1. Select the UEs which priorities are higher than "drb Traffic"**: This is the initial selection step.
\* **sub process**: This leads to a subprocess labeled "Update NBW = sum allocated PRBs of higher priority UEs".
3. **2. Check Condition to apply High buffer UE prioritization**: This is the next main step.
\* **sub process**: This leads to a decision point: "NBW > 0 and number of unvisited Ues in CS2 List > 1".
\* **YES**: If true, proceed to "2.1 Sort UEs in descending order of pending buffer in CS2list".
\* **NO**: If false, proceed to "set flag CanApplyHighBufferUeAlg = false".
4. **Select NonGBR UEs in CS2**: This step follows the "NO" path from the previous subprocess.
5. **set flag CanApplyHighBufferUeAlg = false**: This is a process step.
6. **2.1 Sort UEs in descending order of pending buffer in CS2list**: This is a process step.
7. **2.2 Calculate sum of RBest of the Top (Nsched - dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio) UEs**: This is a process step.
8. **sum of RBest > NBW**: This is a decision point.
\* **YES**: If true, proceed to "set flag CanApplyHighBufferUeAlg = true".
\* **NO**: If false, proceed to "NBW > 0".
9. **set flag CanApplyHighBufferUeAlg = true**: This is a process step.
10. **NBW > 0**: This is a decision point.
\* **YES**: If true, proceed to "3 begin to select High-buffer UE".
\* **NO**: If false, proceed to "3.2 End High buffer UE prioritization set CanApplyHighBufferUeAlg = false".
11. **go next UE in CS2 list and L < Nsched**: This is a decision point.
\* **YES**: If true, proceed to "3 begin to select High-buffer UE".
\* **NO**: If false, the process ends at the "END" node.
12. **3 begin to select High-buffer UE**: This is a process step.
13. **CanApplyHighBufferUeAlg = true and Min(unvisited UES, Nsched - L) <= Nsched**: This is a decision point.
\* **YES**: If true, proceed to "3.1 Select this UE SKIP MUMIMO correlation checking".
\* **NO**: If false, proceed to "Check unvisited UEs which one RBest > NBW/Nsched - L".
14. **3.1 Select this UE SKIP MUMIMO correlation checking**: This is a process step.
15. **3.2 End High buffer UE prioritization set CanApplyHighBufferUeAlg = false**: This is a process step.
16. **Check unvisited UEs which one RBest > NBW/Nsched - L**: This is a decision point.
\* **YES**: If true, proceed to "Insert this UE at current Postion in Cs2 list".
\* **NO**: If false, proceed to "Subcell/PDCCH/ PDSCH/PUCCH Check".
17. **Insert this UE at current Postion in Cs2 list**: This is a process step.
18. **Subcell/PDCCH/ PDSCH/PUCCH Check**: This is a decision point.
\* **Fail**: If false, the process goes to the "Fail" output.
\* **Pass**: If true, proceed to "4.Add UE into To-Be-Scheduled list update NBW= NBW - RBest".
19. **4.Add UE into To-Be-Scheduled list update NBW= NBW - RBest**: This is a process step.
20. **END**: The process terminates.
The flowchart uses standard flowchart symbols:
\* Ovals for Start/End.
\* Rectangles for process steps.
\* Diamonds for decision points.
\* Arrows to indicate the flow of control.
\* Subprocess boxes to denote modular parts of the process.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-11211323.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Procedures:

1.Update NBW = n \* NBW -  sum allocated PRBs of higher priority UEs, when select the UEs which priorities are higher than drbTraffic  [Before CB014044-UPD003] and nbrTraffic [End CB014044-UPD003].

2.Check the condition to apply high buffer UE prioritization: if number of unvisited Ues in CS2 List  > [Before PR852235] Nsched - L [PR852235] 1 [ENDPR852235]and sum of RBest> NBW (ref step 2.1 and 2.2, NBW > 0), enable this algorithm for high buffer UE prioritization(set flag CanApplyHighBufferUeAlg = true), otherwise disable this algorithm.

[Before CB014044-UPD002]

2.1 Sort Non-GBR UEs and NBR UEs in descending order of RBest  in CS2 list.

2.2 Calculate sum of RBest of the Top  (Nsched - L) UEs in CS2 list.

[CB014044-UPD002].

2.1 Sort drbTraffic  UEs  in descending order by their Pending buffer in CS2 list.

2.2 Calculate sum of RBest of the Top  (Nsched \*dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio)  UEs in CS2 list.

[End CB014044-UPD002].

3.Begin to select High-buffer UE from CS2 list   when this algorithm is enabled and [Before PR852235] L ≥ Nsched - Nsched *dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio. [PR852235] min( unvisited Ues UEs in ‘S’, Nsched – L).<= Nsched*dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio[ENDPR852235]

3.1 Select this UE as High-buffer UE if the current UE RBest > NBW / Nsched - L (note: NBW> 0), even if NRCELL.NRDLMUMIMO.actMuAwareTdSch is set to True, regardless of correlation for MU-MIMO UE .

3.2 End High buffer UE prioritization(set flag CanApplyHighBufferUeAlg = false) if there is no available resources(NBW = 0).

4.Add UE into To-be-scheduled list after  Subcell/PDCCH/PDSCH/PUCCH Check are passed. update NBW=  NBW- RBest.

5.End UE selection when L = Nsched or No available resources.

where:

NBW:the total available PRBs in current slot.

n: n = 1 if NRCELL.actDlMuMimoEnh is set to FALSE, else NRCELL.actDlMuMimoEnh is set to True  [Before PR857062]  and NRCELL.NRDLMUMIMO.actMuAwareTdSch is set to False, n = rdChannelBwMultiplierDl (see [12657403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBIEwEkSEfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).[PR857062] n= NRCELL.channelBwMultiplierDl [End PR857062]

Nsched:rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl, see [11179079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku3Z6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

L: number of selected UEs (include SIB/Paging)

RBest:estimated PRBs required by UE, see [11181264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-HkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio: NIDD parameter, NRBTS.NRCELL.dlHighBufferPrioUeRatio.

NOTE: high-buffer-UE could be a NBR UE or a non-GBR UE.

<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Forms/Tree_View.aspx?id=%2Fsites%2F5Gdoc%2FAS%5FTech%5FSpec%2FDrawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G%2FUser%20Plane%2F5G%20L2%20Entity%20Level%2F2%205G%2DL2%2DPS%20Component%20Requirements%2F2%2E2%20DL%20Scheduler%2F2%2E2%2E3%20TD%20Scheduler&viewid=967508b3%2D8e81%2D461c%2Db99d%2D145065cf0c1c&csf=1&web=1&e=V8ishU&cid=9206de7d%2Df76b%2D4167%2D95a0%2D9ed94135ffa1&FolderCTID=0x012000F0A0A3BA325F7648AD307E6959BA7376>

---

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-7 UE selection Composing CS2 list with Several Dedicated BWP (ID: 11148851)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11148863`)

UE selection
If n > 1, the number of dedicated BWP per cell(5G\_UP\_ALG\_8240\_replaced([11110833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpH-RfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

For selecting CS2 UE candidates the algorithm mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4261\_replaced([11175776](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kultGfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be followed.

CP2 reference: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4261\_replaced([11175776](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kultGfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 2.2.3.4.1.0-8 UE selection Slot-based allocations with DlInterferenceAvoidance (ID: 11149914)

**2.2.3.4.1.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11149921`)

UE selection
When rdEnableTdIcic is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30165\_replaced([11194010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvx_5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall perform slot-based allocations depending on the UE classification as either 'normal' or 'high performing' (as dpecified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8432\_replaced([11181306](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-HmvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Rules:

1) For a slot, if its corresponding bit in rdFirstDlSlot is set to 1 and in that slot if the sum of FD resource requirements of the 'normal' UEs is greater than or equal to rdResourceUtilizationThresholdFirstSlot (specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30168\_replaced([11194030](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvx_6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the available channel bandwidth, then 'high-performing' UEs, even if selected by the TD scheduler, shall not be allocated any FD resources. This restriction is only applicable for 'high-performing' UEs having an initial transmission.

2) For a slot, if its corresponding bit in rdFirstDlSlot is set to 0 and in that slot if the sum of FD resource requirements of the 'high-performing UEs' is greater than or equal to rdResourceUtilizationThresholdOtherSlots (specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30171\_replaced([11194040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvx_7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the available channel bandwidth, then 'normal' UEs, even if selected by the TD scheduler, shall not be allocated any FD resources. This is applicable for both initial and retransmission of normal performing UEs.

rdFirstDlSlot is R&D parameter specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30265\_replaced([11194020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvx_6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It is a bitmap, with each bit representing a slot in a frame. Note: It is recommended that when rdEnableTdIcic is enabled, then only the bits corresponding to the first DL slot after an UL slot can be set to 1 in rdFirstDlSlot.

---

#### 2.2.3.4.2 Resources distribution

#### 2.2.3.4.2-1 Resources distribution

**2.2.3.4.2-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148938`)

Resources distribution
If /NRBTS/NRcell/actFdmSchedulingInitialBWP is true

L2-PS support multiple RACH Msg2s are scheduled at one slot, besides enough PDCCH and PDSCH resources are needed, meanwhile the necessary resources or conditions as blow are also needed in RACH Msg3 slot.

1.The number of Msg3 are not beyond rrmMaxNumUesFdmUl defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10654\_replaced([11199273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwMPmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2.The number of Msg3 are not beyond rrmMaxRaMsg3FdmUlInitialBWP defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10663\_replaced([11199313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwM2ofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

3.The number of Msg3 are not beyond (LastUlScheduledUes + Margin):

LastUlScheduledUes is Maximum number of UEs that can be scheduled whithout UE skipping at previous UL slot.

Margin = 1.

4.Available beam for Msg3 at Msg3 slot.

5.Available Pusch resources for Msg3 at Msg3 slot.

#### 2.2.3.4.2-2 Resources distribution

#### 2.2.3.4.2-3 Resources distribution

**2.2.3.4.2-3.0-2**  (ID: `11148964`)

Resources distribution
5G-L2-PS maintains a token bucket [CB008963-A]per non-VoNR GBR [End CB008963-A] to track the allocations made towards non-VoNR GBR flow for every UE. Token bucket can maintain values of token bits in +ve or -ve scales. Details can be checked in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8026\_replaced([11175497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kujQ1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8028\_replaced([11175504](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kujQ2PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The same is applicable for both DL and UL transmission scheduling.

[Before CB008963-A]

A +ve token value indicates the number of bits that are pending to be scheduled for a UE to meet its GFBR demand. In this state, the UE is considered to be in gbrTraffic priority.

[CB008963-A]

A +ve token value indicates the number of bits that are pending to be scheduled for non-VoNR GBR to meet its GFBR demand.

For UE has one or mutiple non-VoNR GBRs, if one of these GBRs is in this state with +ve, the UE is considered to be in gbrTraffic priority.

[End CB008963-A]

The token value gets adjusted(reduced) as the allocations happen to the non-VoNR GBR flow associated with the UE.

[Before CB008963-A]

A -ve token value indicates the number of bits that are already scheduled for a UE above its GFBR demand. In this state, the UE is considered to be in deprioritized gbrTraffic priority.

[CB008963-A]

A -ve token value indicates the number of bits that are already scheduled for a UE above the non-VoNR GBR's GFBR demand.

For UE has one or mutiple non-VoNR GBRs, if ALL of non-VoNR GBRs is in this state with -ve, the UE is considered to be in deprioritized gbrTraffic priority.

[End CB008963-A]

The token value gets adjusted(reduced to become further -ve) as the allocations happen to the non-VoNR GBR flow associated with the UE.

A timer 'Tokenbuckettimer' is started when UE is scheduled and the token bucket value [CB008963-A] of all non-VoNR GBRs[End CB008963-A] is -ve after scheduling. Upon timer expiry the token bucket value increased for the time elapsed [CB008963-A] per non-VoNR GBR[End CB008963-A] and check whether [CB008963-A]any non-VoNR GBR[End CB008963-A] token value becomes +ve or not. The time is stopped if the token value  [CB008963-A]of any non-VoNR GBR[End CB008963-A] becomes +ve and trigger CS1 event to change priority from Depriorityzed GBR to Prioritized GBR. If Token Bucket value is still -ve then restart the timer.

Note:

1. The UE can switch from gbrTraffic priority to deprioritized gbr traffic in the same scheduling cycle. This happens if there are enough resources to schedule a TB size greater than the token bucket size.
2. The token value adjustment as per GBR TBS happens only when the new TX is scheduled. Token Bucket Variable will NOT be adusted during ReTx
3. The token adjustment is reverted if there is a HARQ failure(all retransmissions failed) for a scheduled transmission.

[CB008963-A]4.To reduce timer per non VoNR GBR, Tokenbuckettimer is shared at UE level.  [End CB008963-A]

---

#### 2.2.3.4.2-4 Resources distribution

**2.2.3.4.2-4.0-1**  (ID: `11149938`)

Resources distribution
When Downlink MU MIMO enhancement (CB008305) is enabled along with DlInterferenceAvoidance (CB008955), Then DlInterferenceAvoidance will be applied only in slots where this no Mu-Mimo paired UE’s (see 5G\_UP\_AL G\_14423)

1) After Distribute Resources, if there are no RBG's left for allocation then DlInterferenceAvoidance is not applied to the UE's

2) If any MuEligible retx UE's are scheduled in slot, then  DlInterferenceAvoidance is not applied to the UE's

3) During Distribute Resources, if all the UE's in the distribution list is HighPerformance UE the rbglimit is not applied. The reason is ,even after applying the rbglimit, if all RBG's are distributed then DlInterferenceAvoidance is not applied to the UE's in the slot. However in dlMuMimo Enhance, if there are remaining RBG's , then these RBG's are distributed to UE's for which have still buffer left in the slot.(refer 5G\_L2\_4186\_replaced([11164833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25vZf_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Since the PRB are allocated based on PRBallocDirection in CB008955, to avoid incorrect startPrb for a UE due to re-allocating of remaining RBG in dlMuMimo Enhance.

4) DlInterferenceAvoidance is applied only in slots where there are some RBG's left after distributing to all UE's in the slot. In this case, for the first UE for which resources allocated from TOP, an extra RBG is allocated because of the partial RBG allocation. This is done to avoid dlMuMimo Enhance allocating the remaining RBG because UE would have the buffer left because of partial RBG allocation.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to wireless communication. The flowchart uses rectangular boxes for process steps and a diamond shape for a decision point. Arrows indicate the flow of the process.
Here is the text extracted from the flowchart:
\* **Execute FDM WRR for all non-GBR UEs**
\* **Has free RBGs?** (Decision point)
\* **Y** (Yes branch)
\* **Continue executing 8955 algorithms. No MU-MIMO in current TTI**
\* **N** (No branch)
\* **Clear above FDM WRR allocation result**
\* **Execute FDM WRR for non-GBR UEs which are MU ineligible.**
\* **Continue executing MU algorithms**[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1399.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

##### 2.2.3.4.2.0-1 Resources distribution Conversion Buffer Occupancy to an amount of RBG resources (ID: 11148877)

**2.2.3.4.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148887`)

Resources distribution
Before resource distribution for initial transmissions UEs in the to-be-scheduled list we must convert their buffer occupancy to number of RBG resources.

This is determined by finding the smallest number of RBG resources that would allow the corresponding TBS with the proposed MCS rrmDlProposedMcs to be greater than the UEs bufferedBytes\*8 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4509\_replaced([11181264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-HkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

The left chart is labeled "Buffer occupancy bytes" and the right chart is labeled "Buffer occupancy RBG". Both charts have a horizontal axis labeled with Ue0, Ue1, Ue2, and Ue3.
In the "Buffer occupancy bytes" chart:
- Ue0 has a tall blue bar.
- Ue1 has a short red bar.
- Ue2 has a tall green bar.
- Ue3 has a tall yellow bar.
In the "Buffer occupancy RBG" chart:
- Ue0 has a tall blue bar.
- Ue1 has a short red bar.
- Ue2 has a tall green bar.
- Ue3 has a tall yellow bar.
Below the charts, there are two curved arrows pointing from the charts towards a rectangular box. The box contains the text "TBS table (with rrmDIProposedMcs)" with "rrmDIProposedMcs" underlined with a wavy red line. The arrows suggest a flow of information or a relationship between the buffer occupancy data and the TBS table.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1259.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

##### 2.2.3.4.2.0-2 Resources distribution Distribution Algorithm (ID: 11148892)

**2.2.3.4.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12525189`)

Resources distribution
[CB014861-A]If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true, and NRCELL.actExhaustiveScheduling is set to DL or DLAndUL:

Exhaustive Scheduling is used to FD resources distribution algorithm defined by [12483324](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_qbsGEQ-XEfCvOvZoOJBSnQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9);

else //legacy WRR[End CB014861-A]

Once UE’s are selected FD resources distribution will start with weighted round robin algorithm 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23755\_replaced([11179805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku7ET_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

First weights of UEs in to-be-scheduled are computed (weight of one UE corresponds to sum of scheduling weigh of its DRBs); then weights are normalized by dividing all UE's weight by the smallest one 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23761\_replaced([11179826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku7rUvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Then we start rounds of distribution described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23763\_replaced([11180562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku7rXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as in example bellow where there is four UEs (bleu, red, green and yellow).

1. **Top Left: Scheduling Weights**

The curved arrows suggest a flow or relationship between these different components.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1261.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

In example there are 3 rounds of distribution because highest normalized weight (ratio in picture) is equal to 3. In 1st round each UE will be served with an amount of resources corresponding to rdparam rdFdResPerRoundDl. Then in 2nd round only blue and red will continue to ne served. In 3rd Round blue UE is served alone. This scheme of distribution is repeated until there is no resource left.

A UE is not given more than the maximum FD resources it can get (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4509\_replaced([11181264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-HkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). As it shown in second example (see picture below) where the red UE has less buffer occupancy (reflected in RBG conversion of buffer occupancy). UE stop to be served as soon as it'is satisfied ie it has enough resources compared buffer occupancy RBG ie it doesn't need more resources. Algorithm will distribute resource to next UE still not satisfied (in example below it's the blue UE).

The algorithm stops either if all UEs with initial transmission have been allocated the maximum amount of resources they can get or all the available resources have been allocated. The output of the algorithm is the amount of resources (RBGs) each UE will get from the available resources.

##### 2.2.3.4.2.0-3 Resources distribution Allocation of the number of PRBs (ID: 11148913)

**2.2.3.4.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11148925`)

Resources distribution
If isAnyDlPrbPoolingActive is set to 'false'   (Refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_14\_replaced([10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for this flag), the number of PRBs allocated to the UE is the number of RBGs times the RBG size P (For first and last RBG use value in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4459\_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If isAnyDlPrbPoolingActive is set to ‘true’ (Refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_14\_replaced([10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for this flag), the number of PRBs allocated to the Ue numOfPrb is the number of RBGs times the RBG size P which don't exceed the number of usable RBG of size P computed by the numAllocCellPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4279\_replaced([11177002](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kurzwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (For first and last RBG use value in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4459\_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

In case of a retransmission, if numAllocCellPrb is less than the size needed for the retransmission, then processing mentioned in requirement  5G\_L2\_4109\_replaced([11174562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26lG8fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) should be applied and if the HARQ process is freed, the DLHarqBufferIndex should also be freed.

[CB012605-C]

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, the number of PRBs allocated multiplied by the RANK used to schedule the UE must be equal of smaller to the number of layer PRBs allocated from BBRM, defined as numAllocCellLayerPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25712\_replaced([11214266](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

In case of a retransmission, if numAllocCellLayerPrb is less than the size needed for the retransmission, then processing mentioned in requirement  5G\_L2\_4109\_replaced([11174562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26lG8fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) should be applied and if the HARQ process is freed, the DLHarqBufferIndex should also be freed.

[CB012605-E]

This is also valid when the adaptive re-transmission scheme is activated (/NRBTS/NRCELL/actAdaptiveReTxResMcs is set to TRUE).

Note that the amount of required layer PRBs for retransmission shall not exceed the remaining available layer PRBs in a slot (rrmRemainingPdschLayerPrbPerSlot; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If this is the case, the retransmission is postponed.

[End CB012605-E]

[End CB012605-C]

CP2 Reference:

5G\_UP\_ALG\_4510\_replaced([11181328](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-Hn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) FD resource allocation for FDM (Random)
