#### 2.2.3.4.3 Resources allocation

##### 2.2.3.4.3.0-1 Resources allocation PRB Resource Assignment with DlInterferenceAvoidance (ID: 11149894)

**2.2.3.4.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11149907`)

Resources allocation
When actDlInterferenceAvoidance (5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is enabled, the DlInterferenceAvoidance Parameters are configured(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8282\_replaced([11193288](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvrSOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

FD scheduler categorizes the UE's into 'normal' and 'high performing' UE's (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8432\_replaced([11181306](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-HmvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on configured thresholds.

CB008955 algorithm uses initial estimation of proposed MCS (based on value used in previous scheduled slot of the UE; prior to any rate matching

related adjustments) during categorization of UEs. (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8432\_replaced([11181306](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-HmvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

CB008955 algorithm is implemented at Resource Allocation and later based on number of Prb’s allocated, the TbSize and MCS are updated in the slot.

There can be instances where UE could be categorized as normal UE based on previous slot proposed MCS and since the MCS is updated later in the slot it could fall under High Performing category and vice-versa.

After UE categorization, PRB resource allocation for the categorized UE's are done based on the configured PRB allocation direction (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8282\_replaced([11193288](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvrSOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CNI-129155] When rdEnableTdIcic is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30165\_replaced([11194010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvx_5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall perform slot-based allocations depending on the UE category ('normal' or 'high performing'). See 5G\_L2\_21638\_replaced([11149914](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24YupvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CNI-129155].

---

##### 2.2.3.4.3.0-2 Resources allocation Randomly allocate RBGs in cells with one dedicated BWP (ID: 11149946)

**2.2.3.4.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11149951`)

Resources allocation
In FD Scheduler, the RBGs are allocated to UE as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12660\_replaced([11182732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvFcVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).In each slot, before assigning the RBGs to the UE, the Randomization index is derived using the xSFN and slot number.  This Randomization index is used to select the RBG Randomization sequence from the Randomization table which is generated at cell setup.

For Retx UEs, the randomization of RBG allocation is done as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12664\_replaced([11182875](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvGDbPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Randomization of RBGs is not applied when actDlMuMimo = TRUE and there are MU MIMO UEs paired in the slot. However when actDlMuMimoEnh = TRUE, Randomization of RBGs is applied regardless of whether there is MU MIMO paired UEs in slot or not.(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12666\_replaced([11182912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvGqc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

##### 2.2.3.4.3.0-3 Resources allocation Randomly allocate RBGs in cells with multiple dedicated BWPs (ID: 11149958)

**2.2.3.4.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11149965`)

Resources allocation
If Multiple Dedicated BWP are configured (NRCELL.actMultipleDedicatedBWPs = TRUE / NRCELL.actPowerSavingBWP = TRUE / NRCELL.actEnhMultipleDedicatedBWPs = TRUE) then Randomization of RBGs of the UE are done as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12661\_replaced([11182756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvFcWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12662\_replaced([11182785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvFcXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The Random RBG sequence is generated at cell setup for all configured Dedicated BWPs in form of a static Randomization table and its used in Allocating the RBGs to the UE in Resource Allocation

---

##### 2.2.3.4.3.0-4 Resources allocation Randomly allocate RBGs in cells with DL Interference Avoidance enabled (ID: 11149970)

**2.2.3.4.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11149975`)

Resources allocation
CB008955 (DL Interference Avoidance) is a TDD only feature that minimizes inter-cell interference for high performance (HP) UEs (high MCS, high rank, high data rate, in largest BWP) by allocating resources for HP UEs at one edge of the bandwidth while allocating resources for non-HP UEs at the other edge of the bandwidth.

The interaction of CB008955 (DL Interference Avoidance) with DL RBG randomization (CB009426) for single dedicated bandwidth part is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12665\_replaced([11182890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvGqcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). And with multiple dedicated bandwidth part is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12666\_replaced([11182912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvGqc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

At cellSetup, the DL Randomization table is updated to handle all cases for interaction with CB008955 (DL Interference Avoidance) .In case of single dedicated bandwidth part, the randomized table is generated to address 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12665\_replaced([11182890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvGqcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and for multiple dedicated bandwidth part to address 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12666\_replaced([11182912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvGqc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

In FD resource Allocation for  FDM for 'High performing' and 'normal' UEs See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8194\_replaced([11182952](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvGqe_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), a flag isHpUe is set for HP UE’s. Based on the flag isHpUe, the legacy resource allocation function (based on PRB Allocation Direction) is called for HP UE’s whereas the resource allocation for randomization is called for non-HP UE’s.

---

### 2.2.3.5 Definition of DC-GBR Scheduling Criteria

#### 2.2.3.5.0-1 Definition of DC-GBR Scheduling Criteria DC-GBR data rate monitoring with averaging window(AW) (ID: 11148977)

**2.2.3.5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148982`)

Definition of DC-GBR Scheduling Criteria
L2PS shall maintain an averaging window (AW) for DC-GBR data rate monitoring(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30379\_replaced([11175610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuke8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the DC-GBR bearer's data rate shall be calculated and updated every 10ms, for in which slot to do this update refer 5G\_L2\_23246\_replaced([11188805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28LCa_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

## 2.2.4 SD Scheduler

**2.2.4.0-4**  (ID: `11149029`)

SD Scheduler
PUCCH for HARQ feedback user co-scheduling eligibility check

For the case of FD beamforming is disabled, additional UE eligibility checking shall be done on short PUCCH to avoid invalid DL pairing result:

On each DL slot N, calculate and check that total number of scheduled beams for PUCCH doesn’t exceed the number of beams available for pucch (four beams considered, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2455\_replaced([11116019](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in next slot UL (N + k1).

Beams for periodic CSI reports and HARQ feedback from previous DL slot(s) are taken into account in this check.

Link to the "PucchFilterIntegrationInSDSchedulerAlgorithm.pptx" file:

<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:w:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/8.6%205G-L2-PS%20Component%20Requirements>

Note. This check reduce probability of SD co-scheduled users reject by FDM (see 5G\_L2\_252\_replaced([11149003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24UdIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in its corresponding pucch resources check (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4319\_replaced([11177575](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwFK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more details) and thus potential empty DL slots.

---

### 2.2.4.1 MU pairing

#### 2.2.4.1.1 DL pairing algorithm

##### 2.2.4.1.1.0-1 DL pairing algorithm DL pairing algorithm is described in CP2 requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4365_replaced( 11141965 ) (ID: 11149047)

#### 2.2.4.1.2 MU pairing extension to support PMI beam

##### 2.2.4.1.2.0-1 MU pairing extension to support PMI beam PMI beam based MU pairing (ID: 11149058)

**2.2.4.1.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11149063`)

MU pairing extension to support PMI beam
If dlMimoMode is set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4, UE pairing for MU-MIMO shall be PMI beam based, that is, only UEs which is PMI beam based shall be selected for MU-MIMO pairing, and the pattern ID offset of the first / second beam shall be used as the pairing beam ID of the primary / second beam. If dlMimoMode is not set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4, UE pairing for MU-MIMO shall still be SSB/refined beam based (same as legacy).

Implementation consideration - informative

If dlMimoMode is set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4, MU-MIMO pairing is limited to PMI beam only, and CPRT may not provide any beam correlation information via bfSetup::correlationTable IE of PsCell\_CellSetupReq message. But for extensibility consideration, L2-PS shall not mess up the beam correlation data of SSB/refined beam (received via correlationTable IE of PsCell\_CellSetupReq message) and that of PMI beam (received via correlationTable2 IE of PsCell\_CellPmiBeamDataSetReq message) when storing them to cell context. That is, dedicated structure shall be used for PMI beam correlation data in L2-PS coding.

CP2 reference: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4389\_replaced([11142166](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3JNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

.

## 2.2.5 FD Scheduler

### 2.2.5.0-1 FD Scheduler FA: [Internal Domain] FD-Scheduler Document Owner: Lukasz Filimowski (Nokia) (ID: 11149087)

### 2.2.5.1 PDSCH scheduling in SSB and TRS slots

**2.2.5.1.0-1**  (ID: `11149098`)

PDSCH scheduling in SSB and TRS slots
Possible scenario according to configuration(just for information):

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Parameter type | Detail parameters |
| CellTechnology | FDD/DSS, FR1 TDD |
| BF | actBeamforming, isFdBfSsbTrs=(dlEcpriFdBeamforming & actDlEcpriPhase4(ReMask)), isBeamRefinementValid |
| subcell | numDlSubCellIdxs, dlSubcellTypes |
| PdschPrb | numPdschPrbInSsbSlots(M), numPdschPrbInTrsSlots(N) |
| BW | dlBandWidth(BW) |

X: PDSCH PRB number and RBG bitmap in SSB slot

Y: PDSCH PRB number and RBG bitmap in TRS slot

Z: PDSCH PRB number and RBG bitmap in SSB slot with TRS

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| CASE | Condition | Expected result | subfeature |
| Case0 | isAbove6Ghz or (M=0 & N=0) | X=0, Y=0, Z=0 |  |
| Case1 | M>0, N>0, BW>5, actBeamforming=false | Calculate X, Y, Z, respectively | 2538-A/C |
| Case2 | M>0, N=0, BW>5, actBeamforming=false | Y=0, Z=0, calculate X | 2538-A/C |
| Case3 | M=0, N>0, actBeamforming=false | X=0, Z=0, calculate Y | 2538-A/C |
| Case4 | TDD, M>0, N>0, actBeamforming=false | Calculate X, Y, Z, respectively, can combine with Case1 | 2538-C |
| Case5 | TDD, M>0, N>0, actBeamforming=true, numDlSubCellIdxs≥2 | Calculate X, Y, Z, respectively, can combine with Case1 isRankReductionNeeded=false split subcell usage, one for SSB/TRS, the other for PDSCH | 2538-D |
| Case6 | isBeamRefinementValid=true, numDlSubCellIdxs<2, isFdBfSsbTrs =false | X=0, Y=0, Z=0 | 2538-D |
| Case7 | TDD, M=0, N>=0, actBeamforming=true, numDlSubCellIdxs<2, isFdBfSsbTrs =false | X=0, Y=0, Z=0 | 2538-D |
| Case8 | TDD, M>0, N>=0, actBeamforming=true, numDlSubCellIdxs<2, isFdBfSsbTrs =false | Y=0, Z=0, calculate X isRankReductionNeeded=true | 2534-C 2538-D |
| Case9 | TDD, M>0, N>0, actBeamforming=true, isFdBfSsbTrs =true | Calculate X, Y, Z, respectively, can combine with Case1 isRankReductionNeeded=false | 2538-E |

#### 2.2.5.1.1 PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots

##### 2.2.5.1.1.0-1 PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots (ID: 11149113)

**2.2.5.1.1.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `11149273`)

PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots
This part is to calculate frequency resource of PDSCH scheduled by DCI format 1\_1  in SSB slots due to power limitation. After calculation, one bitmap of usable RBGs and the number of usable PRBs are found. Calculation is done once during Cell Setup procedure [CB009510-A] and during Cell Reconfiguration procedure if numPdschPrbInSsbSlots or numPdschPrbInTrsSlots parameters are modified. [End CB009510-A].

Parameters to be used from PsCell\_CellSetup(5G\_L2\_IF\_61\_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

 numPdschPrbInSsbSlots

 numPdschPrbInTrsSlots

 ssBlockPrbOffset

 ssBlockSubCarrierOffset

 downlinkBwp.location

 csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB

[CB009510-A]

Parameters to be used from PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq(5G\_L2\_IF\_1988\_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

 numPdschPrbInSsbSlots

 numPdschPrbInTrsSlots

[End CB009510-A]

numOfSsbPrb for SSB occupied resources is fixed to be 20PRBs.

If numPdschPrbInSsbSlots < min{ firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize } //from Step2

no need to do calculation

endif

Step1 Calculation of number of usable RBG in dedicated BWP

Calculation is according to 3GPP 38.214 5.1.2.2.1. P is RBG size according to Table 5.1.2.2.1-1 in 38.214.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N RRG" in a stylized font with a rainbow gradient. The letters are slightly blurred, giving them a soft, almost watercolor-like appearance. The background is white, and the text is positioned towards the left side of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1297.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] represents number of RBG in dedicated BWP. There are [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N RRG" in a stylized font with a rainbow gradient. The letters are slightly blurred, giving them a soft, almost watercolor-like appearance. The background is white, and the text is positioned towards the left side of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1297.001.png[/image\_path][/image-1] bits to indicate RBG usable or not.

All [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N RRG" in a stylized font with a rainbow gradient. The letters are slightly blurred, giving them a soft, almost watercolor-like appearance. The background is white, and the text is positioned towards the left side of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1297.001.png[/image\_path][/image-2] bits are set to usable. Bit 0 to bit [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N\_RBG - 1". The text is in a light blue and white color scheme, with a slight gradient effect. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1297.002.png[/image\_path][/image-3] indicate all RBGs in dedicated BWP.

Step2 Remove PRB blanking RBGs

firstUsableRbgIndex inidicates first RBG index of usable RBG in dedicated BWP

lastUsableRbgIndex inidicates last RBG index of usable RBG in dedicated BWP

firstUsableRbgSize inidicates PRB number of first usable RBG, i.e. for firstUsableRbgIndex

lastUsableRbgSize inidicates PRB number of last usable RBG, i.e. for lastUsableRbgIndex

Bit 0 to firstUsableRbgIndex-1 are set to not usable.

Bit lastUsableRbgIndex+1 to [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N\_RBG - 1". The text is in a light blue and white color scheme, with a slight gradient effect. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_1297.002.png[/image\_path][/image-4] are set to not usable.

Step3 Remove SSB occupied RBGs

firstSsbRbgIndex =  rounddown(ssBlockPrbOffset/P) - rounddown(N\_bwp\_start/P)

lastSsbRbgIndex =  rounddown((ssBlockPrbOffset + numOfSsbPrb - 1 + roundup(ssBlockSubCarrierOffset / 12)) / P) - rounddown(N\_bwp\_start/P)

N\_bwp\_start = downlinkBwp.location for this dedicate BWP

if firstSsbRbgIndex <= firstUsableRbgIndex

firstUsableRbgIndex = max{ lastSsbRbgIndex+1, firstUsableRbgIndex }

if firstUsableRbgIndex = lastSsbRbgIndex+1

firstUsableRbgSize = P

endif

endif

if lastSsbRbgIndex >= lastUsableRbgIndex

lastUsableRbgIndex = min{ firstSsbRbgIndex-1, lastUsableRbgIndex }

if lastUsableRbgIndex = firstSsbRbgIndex-1

lastUsableRbgSize = P

endif

endif

If firstUsableRbgIndex > lastUsableRbgIndex

Reset all bit to not usable, end of calculation

endif

Bit firstSsbRbgIndex to bit lastSsbRbgIndex are set to not usable.

If CRI based beam refinement is enabled, i.e. nrBtsBeamRefinementP2 is set to true in NIDD and also PsCell\_CellSetupReq, CSIRS for beam refinement will be sent in SSB slot and if CSIRS are located after SSB.

if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = false or subcellDeactivationDlAllowed = false, This makes RBGs after SSB not usable. So bit lastSsbRbgIndex+1 to bit lastUsableRbgIndex are also set to not usable.  if CSIRS are located below SSB. This makes RBGs below SSB not usable. So bit 0 to bit firstSsbRbgIndex are also set to not usable, refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2667\_replaced([11302851](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqiKqfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) else if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed=true, or subcellDeactivationDlAllowed = true, this makes csirsBeamMgmtNumRBG  RBGs after SSB not usable. So bit lastSsbRbgIndex+1 to bit lastSsbRbgIndex+ csirsBeamMgmtNumRBG  are also set to not usable. if CSIRS are located below SSB. This makes csirsBeamMgmtNumRBG  RBGs below SSB not usable. So bit firstSsbRbgIndex - csirsBeamMgmtNumRBG   to bit firstSsbRbgIndex are also set to not usable, refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2667\_replaced([11302851](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqiKqfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

where

csirsBeamMgmtNumRBG is the number of RBG needed to cover the csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB given in CellSetupReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_113\_replaced([10968876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

if csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB%RBGSize=0, csiRsBeamMgmtNumRBG = csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB/ RBGSize

else csiRsBeamMgmtMumRBG = floor (csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB/RBGSize) +1

---

##### 2.2.5.1.1.0-2 PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots (Step4) (ID: 11149280)

**2.2.5.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11149286`)

PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots
Step4 Remove RBGs due to power limitation

usableRbgNum = number of usable RBG from step3

usablePrbNum = count PRB number from usableRbgNum, firstUsableRbgSize and lastUsableRbgSize.

if SSB slot without TRS

[Before CB008940-B]

if slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'false'

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = numPdschPrbInSsbSlots

Else

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = min(numPdschPrbInSsbSlots,(numAllocCellPrb-numOfSsbPrb))

[CB008940-B]

if isAnyDlPrbPoolingActive is equal to 'false'   (Refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_14\_replaced([10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for this flag)

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = numPdschPrbInSsbSlots

Else

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = min(numPdschPrbInSsbSlots,(numAllocCellPrb-numOfNonUsablePrbInSsbSlot))

if CRI based beam refinement is enabled

numOfNonUsablePrbInSsbSlot = numOfSsbPrb + csirsBeamMgmtNumPRB

Else

numOfNonUsablePrbInSsbSlot = numOfSsbPrb

endif

[End CB008940-B]

Each time when L2-PS scheduler distributes the PDSCH resource to a UE on the Ssbslot, L2-PS determine the min(numPdschPrbInSsbSlots,numAllocCellPrb). Where the numAllocCellPrb is the total amount of usable DL PRB of the cell which is computed every bbPoolingPeriod(NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) by the slow pooling algorithm in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

endif

else if SSB slot with TRS

if slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'false'

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = min { numPdschPrbInSsbSlots, numPdschPrbnInTrsSlots }

Else

pdschPrbInSsbSlots = min(numPdschPrbInSsbSlots, numPdschPrbnInTrsSlots , (numAllocCellPrb-numOfSsbPrb))

endif

endif

endif

if usablePrbNum <= pdschPrbInSsbSlots

return the bitset of step3

else

ConfRbgNumOfPSize = floor(pdschPrbInSsbSlots/P)

ConfLastRbgSize = pdschPrbInSsbSlots  – ConfRbgNumOfPSize \* P

usableRbgNumOfPSize = usableRbgNum

minUsableRbgSize = min{ firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize }

maxUsableRbgSize = max{ firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize }

if minUsableRbgSize < P

-- usableRbgNumOfPSize

else

minUsableRbgSize = 0

endif

if maxUsableRbgSize < P

-- usableRbgNumOfPSize

else

maxUsableRbgSize = 0

endif

if usableRbgNumOfPSize > ConfRbgNumOfPSize

remove (usableRbgNumOfPSize – ConfRbgNumOfPSize) RBG with size of P, starting from around SSB and first remove RBG with size of P after SSB

usableRbgNumOfPSize = ConfRbgNumOfPSize

endif

if usableRbgNumOfPSize < ConfRbgNumOfPSize

ConfLastRbgSize = pdschPrbInSsbSlots – usableRbgNumOfPSize \* P

endif

If ConfLastRbgSize >= (minUsableRbgSize + maxUsableRbgSize)

Do nothing

else if ConfLastRbgSize >= maxUsableRbgSize AND ConfLastRbgSize < (minUsableRbgSize + maxUsableRbgSize)

remove index of minUsableRbgSize, set bit position to not usable

minUsableRbgSize=0

else if ConfLastRbgSize >= minUsableRbgSize AND ConfLastRbgSize < maxUsableRbgSize

remove index of maxUsableRbgSize, set bit position to not usable

maxUsableRbgSize=0

else if ConfLastRbgSize < minUsableRbgSize

remove indexes of minUsableRbgSize and maxUsableRbgSize, set bit position to not usable

minUsableRbgSize=0

maxUsableRbgSize=0

endif

usablePrbNum = usableRbgNumOfPSize \* P + minUsableRbgSize + maxUsableRbgSize

if usablePrbNum > pdschPrbInSsbSlots

warning log

set all bit to not usable, i.e. NO PDSCH PRB ALLOCATED in SSB SLOT.

endif

endif

---

##### 2.2.5.1.1.0-3 PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots (Step5) (ID: 11149292)

**2.2.5.1.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11149305`)

PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots
If the value of actPdschAllocAroundSsb is equal to 'True’, then L2-PS proceeds as follows:

If the RBGs blocked as part of Step4 (5G\_L2\_9467\_replaced([11149280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24VEOPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) entirely obstructs all the RBGs in CORESET0, then:

[PR798504]

- RBGs blocked by the positions of SSB, PRB blanking and CSI-RS for beam refinement calculated in Step2 and Step3 (5G\_L2\_4520\_replaced([11149113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24VEMvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) should remain unchanged.

[End PR798504]

- Shift the RBGs that are blocked above SSB to upper end of the largest BWP (which means full RBGs).

- Relocate the RBGs that are blocked below SSB to bottom end of the largest BWP.

Else

Return bitset from step4

Endif

Else

Return bitset from step4

endif

Rationale: If the PRBs within the CORESET0 are obstructed on SSB slots due to power limitation, it would restrict the available slots to schedule MSG2 on the initial BWP. Furthermore, if the obstructed PRBs entirely encompass a small or power-saving BWP, then the Physical Downlink Shared Channel (PDSCH) grants for User Equipment (UE) operating in those corresponding BWPs would not be granted.

Notes:

- actPdschAllocAroundSsb is contained in PsCell\_CellSetupReq(5G\_L2\_IF\_61\_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_1988\_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

---

##### 2.2.5.1.1.0-4 PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots for multi BWP enabled (ID: 11149310)

**2.2.5.1.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11149317`)

PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots
If there are more than one dedicated BWP configured(actMultipleDedicatedBWPs is TRUE or actPowerSavingBwp is TRUE):

The calculation of PDSCH schedulable RBG in SSB slots is per BWP and based on 5G\_L2\_4520\_replaced([11149113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24VEMvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_9467\_replaced([11149280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24VEOPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In FDM scheduler when prepare holes for RBG can't be used in ssb slots, [before PR767921] only the largest dedicated BWP marked RBG [PR767921] all the RBGs (blanked or not) of the large BWP [End PR767921] need to be taken into calculation because other smaller BWPs range already covered by large dedicated BWP.

[PR767921] note:  with blanking at low edge, first RBG[s] of large BWP is/are not used by PDSCH as first Prb is/are blanked. But for other BWPs, first RBG can be used by PDSCH because first RBG is partial and does not contain blanked Prb. so hole preparation algorith has to consider all RBGs (blanked or not) of the large BWP. [End PR767921]

---

##### 2.2.5.1.1.0-5 PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots PDCCH for PDSCH in SSB slots (ID: 11149321)

**2.2.5.1.1.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13388571`)

PDSCH Schedulable RBG in SSB slots
This part is for DSS specific case when actAsymmetricDss = false or when actAsymmetricDss = true and a coreset > 0 overlaps LTE shared area.

Since PDCCH symbol overlaps with first SSB symbol in DSS, PDCCH power shall be considered. Only static PDCCH is considered.

During cell setup procedure, numOfDciAtSsb which indicate how many DCIs can be supported by power excluding SSB.

AL equals to dciDedicatedAggregationLevel if rd742isPdcchPatternActivated = true or aggregationLevel if rd742isPdcchPatternActivated = false

numOfDciAtSsbByPower = numPdschPrbInSsbSlots / (AL \* 6)

[CB007372-M]

When actAsymmetricDss = false

[End CB007372-M]

If AL = 2, numOfDciAtSsbByPower = numOfDciAtSsbByPower / 2 due to 3dB power boost for AL2

When actAsymmetricDss = false

Available CCEs in SSB slots (availCceNumInSsb) are all possible CCEs on first PBCH symbol (symbol position 2) in cell bandwidth excluding CCEs overlapping SSB.

When actAsymmetricDss = true

Available CCE number in SSB slots (availCceNumInSsb) includes all possible CCEs on first PBCH symbol (symbol position 2) in cell bandwidth excluding CCEs overlapping SSB along with all CCEs in NR dedicated area in occasions on symbols up to first PBCH symbol.

numOfDciAtSsbByCce = availCceNumInSsb / AL

numOfDciAtSsb = min{numOfDciAtSsbByPower, numOfDciAtSsbByCce}

numOfDciAtSsb > 0 shall be considered before scheduling PDSCH in SSB slots.

#### 2.2.5.1.2 PDSCH schedulable RBG in TRS slots

##### 2.2.5.1.2.0-1 PDSCH schedulable RBG in TRS slots frequency resource of PDSCH scheduled by DCI format 1_1  in TRS slots (ID: 11149342)

**2.2.5.1.2.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `11149382`)

PDSCH schedulable RBG in TRS slots
This part is to calculate frequency resource of PDSCH scheduled by DCI format 1\_1  in TRS slots due to power limitation. After calculation, one bitmap of usable RBGs and the number of usable PRBs are found. Calculation is done once during Cell Setup procedure.

Only full band TRS resuorce configuration is supported.

Step1. Remove PRB blanking RBG(already implemented in 5GC002534-A 5G\_L2\_4520\_replaced([11149113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24VEMvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

firstUsableRbgSize first RBG PRB number after removing PRB blanking or startPrb is not 0

lastUsableRbgSize  second RBG PRB number after removing PRB blanking

Step2. Limit available RBG

[Before CB008940-B]

if slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'false'

[CB008940-B]

if isAnyDlPrbPoolingActive is equal to 'false'   (Refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_14\_replaced([10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for this flag)

[End CB008940-B]

if numPdschPrbInTrsSlots >=BWP\_size-PRB blanked RBG PRB number

All PRBs/RBGs after step1 are available for PDSCH scheduling.

else

numOfNonRbgSizePrb = numPdschPrbInTrsSlots % RBG

numOfRgbWithRbgSize = numPdschPrbInTrsSlots / RBG

If downlinkBwp.location = 0

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb < lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used

endif

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= lastUsableRbgSize

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used

endif

Else(downlinkBwp.location > 0)

If firstUsableRbgSize < RBG AND lastUsableRbgSize <RBG

If firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize > RBG AND numOfRgbWithRbgSize >= 1 AND numOfNonRbgSizePrb + RBG >= firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize-1 RBGs in the middle of BW and first RBG and last RBG are used.

Else

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW and first RBG and last RBG are used.

Else if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= max(firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize)

If firstUsableRbgSize > lastUsableRbgSize

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= min(firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize)

If firstUsableRbgSize < lastUsableRbgSize

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Endif

Endif

Else if firstUsableRbgSize < RBG

If numOfNonRbgSizePrb < firstUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Else

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else if lastUsableRbgSize < RBG

If numOfNonRbgSizePrb < lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used

Endif

Endif

endif

else

if min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numAllocCellPrb) >= BWP\_size-PRB blanked RBG PRB number

All PRBs/RBGs after step1 are available for PDSCH scheduling.

else

numOfNonRbgSizePrb = min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numAllocCellPrb) % RBG

numOfRgbWithRbgSize = min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numAllocCellPrb) / RBG

- Each time when L2-PS Sheduler distribute the PDSCH resource to a UE on the TRS slot, it determines the min(numPdschPrbInTrsSlots,numAllocCellPrb).

- RBG is the RBG size,

- numAllocCellPrb is the total amount of usable DL PRB of the cell which is computed every bbPoolingPeriod(NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) by the slow pooling algorithm in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If downlinkBwp.location = 0

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb < lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used

endif

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= lastUsableRbgSize

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used

endif

Else(downlinkBwp.location > 0)

If firstUsableRbgSize < RBG AND lastUsableRbgSize <RBG

If firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize > RBG AND numOfRgbWithRbgSize >= 1 AND numOfNonRbgSizePrb + RBG >= firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize-1 RBGs in the middle of BW and first RBG and last RBG are used.

Else

if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= firstUsableRbgSize + lastUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW and first RBG and last RBG are used.

Else if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= max(firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize)

If firstUsableRbgSize > lastUsableRbgSize

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else if numOfNonRbgSizePrb >= min(firstUsableRbgSize, lastUsableRbgSize)

If firstUsableRbgSize < lastUsableRbgSize

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Endif

Endif

Else if firstUsableRbgSize < RBG

If numOfNonRbgSizePrb < firstUsableRbgSize

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Else

first (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

Endif

Else if lastUsableRbgSize < RBG

numOfRgbWithRbgSize RBGs in the middle of BW are used.

Else

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used.

last (numOfRgbWithRbgSize + 1) RBGs are used

endif

##### 2.2.5.1.2.0-2 PDSCH schedulable RBG in TRS slots PDSCH Schedulable RBG in TRS slots for multi BWP enabled (ID: 11149390)

#### 2.2.5.1.3 PDSCH available RE for TRS slot

##### 2.2.5.1.3.0-1 PDSCH available RE for TRS slot Number of TRS RE calculation (ID: 11149407)

**2.2.5.1.3.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12650509`)

PDSCH available RE for TRS slot
This part is to calculate number of TRS RE within scheduled PDSCH PRBs for UE. Result will be filled in ***numRateMatchingRes* in L1Data\_PdschSendReq.**\*\*

As agreed, both full band and sub band TRS supported(actSubTrsRateMatch set to true) when pooling feature enabled. Note: need to check TRS PRB overlap with PDSCH if not full band TRS.

According to 3GPP 38.214 5.1.6.1.1, TRS resources are configured only with desity 3, i.e. row1 in 38.211 table **7.4.1.5.3-1. So there are always 3 TRS REs per PRB per CSIRS resource for tracking in FR1.**

Store TRS resouce number per slot in SlotAttributes for TRS slots and SSB slots with TRS, naming *numOfTrsResource. Store TRS frequency position of all CSIRS resource for tracking, naming* trsFrequencyPosArray,. It would be array of size 4 by 14, i.e. 4 subcarriers and 14 OFDM symbols to indicate TRS RE position in slot with TRS if actSubTrsRateMatch is true, ZP CSIRS for TRS will configured to occupy whole bandwidth to TRS configured symbols to identify the whole symbols will not used for PDSCH scheduling\*\*

numTrsRePerPrb = 12 \* numOfTrsResource  to indicate how many TRS RE in slot with TRS. *numOfTrsResource shall only consider TRS symbols and PRBs overlap with PDSCH*

If UE is actually scheduled with *numOfPrb which are overlapped with TRS, then numCsirsMappingRes* *=* numTrsRePerPrb \* numOfPrb **if**\*\*\*\*

rateMatchingOption to 1: RATE\_MATCHING\_CSIRS or 3: RATE\_MATCHING\_CSIRS\_AND\_DCI **only if PDSCH is overlapped with TRS,**

if actSubTrsRateMatch is true

rateMatchingOption will be set to 4: RATE\_MATCH\_SYMBOL if no PDCCH and PDSCH overlapped or 6:

RATE\_MATCH\_SYMBOL\_AND\_DCI if PDCCH overlapped with PDSCH for TRS slot.

Note: For TDD FR1 with 52 PRBs configuration CSIRS for tracking (or the bandwidth minus the blanked PRBs is greater than 52 PRBs), not all the BW is considered as the number of PRBs overlapped with PDSCH. More information in req 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7557\_replaced([11125689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[CNI-147211-A]**

if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is true and actTddCsirsOpt is true, the above algorithm shall be applicable as well in case of ecpri

**[End CNI-147211-A]**

#### 2.2.5.1.4 Number of overlapped RE between DL PTRS RE and TRS RE calculation

**2.2.5.1.4.0-1**  (ID: `11149439`)

Number of overlapped RE between DL PTRS RE and TRS RE calculation
If DL PTRS is enabled and PTRS should be sent with PDSCH according to scheduled information, see 38.214 5.1.6.3.

This part is to calculate number of overlapped RE between DL PTRS and TRS resources if overlap happens. Reult will be decreased from numCsirsMappingRes.

Since only time density 1 of PTRS is considered and PTRS dlPtrsResElemOffset is hardcoded as 0 in current PTRS related implementation, PTRS RE postion in PRB would be 0 as well, naming ptrsRePosInPrb=0, see 5G\_UP\_IF\_710\_replaced([11504147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSlZjPv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). RE would be considered overlapping if ptrsRePosInPrb is one of trsFrequencyPosArray per symbol.

Check all TRS resources frequency position which are stored in trsFrequencyPosArray with PTRS RE position, count overlapped number of RE per PRB as numReOverlapTrsAndPtrsInPrb.

Get PTRS frenquency density as ptrsFrequencyDensity,

Number of overlapped RE, naming numReOverlapTrsAndPtrs = numReOverlapTrsAndPtrsInPrb \* ceil(numOfPrb / ptrsFrequencyDensity).

### 2.2.5.2 HARQ Processing

#### 2.2.5.2.0-1 HARQ Processing Bookkeeping table for UCI evaluation (ID: 11149452)

**2.2.5.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11149463`)

HARQ Processing
5G-L2-PS shall maintain a bookkeeping table for each configured subcell, which record the relationship between each HARQ Ack bit in UCI and the carrier index, HARQ process and PDSCH SFN and slot number. This can be used to extract the HARQ Ack/Nack info from HARQ Ack code-book in UCI.

For each item in the table, the following is recorded:

UCI sfn and slot number;

Free indication;

Number of scheduled UE in One TTI; for each scheduled UE:

> RNTI;

> total number of ACK/NACK bits contained in UCI; for each ACK/NACK bit:

>> Carrier Index;

>> PDSCH SFN and slot number

>> Harq process number.

The index of each item in the table is calculated from the SFN and slot number of UCI.

And the length of the table should be long enough to make the HARQ process aging algorithm available (5G\_L2\_284\_replaced([11149481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24WSV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), e.g. the length of table could be 40 TTI.

When a UE is scheduled in DL, the related information shall be recorded in the bookkeeping table of its PCell. Before record the information in the table, 5G-L2-PS shall first check if the position of table is free, if it is not free, 5G-L2-PS shall release the HARQ process previously recorded in the position which  is a similar behavior as HARQ process aging (refer to 5G\_L2\_284\_replaced([11149481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24WSV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and free the position.

If rdUsePucchF2OnlyForHarq is true (5G\_L2\_1189\_replaced([11181836](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XKEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then the first two entries shall not be used as C-DAI is set to 3 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4466\_replaced([11178897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). rdUsePucchF2OnlyForHarq is not applied for PUCCH format 3.

[CNI-109641-G] The information related to the UE scheduled on a remote Scell, received in PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingInd, shall also be recorded in the bookkeeping table of its PCell, see 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_460\_replaced([11197147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bf5AIfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CNI-109641-G]

When 5G-L2-PS receives HARQ information from UCI on PUCCH or UCI on PUSCH, 5G-L2-PS shall find the corresponding position of the table according to the physical UL channel receive time, and check if the RNTI in the table is same as the RNTI of PUCCH or PUSCH carrying the UCI.

If the RNTI is correct, 5G-L2-PS shall handle the HARQ feedback for the carrier, PDSCH SFN and slot number and HARQ process according to the table for each ACK/NACK bit, then free the position of table.

CP2 reference(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18215\_replaced([11187299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvaMdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Handle HARQ Ack code-book for DL HARQ multiplexing ...
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4595\_replaced([11187331](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvaMe_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Dynamic Long PUCCH Token Maintenance for UEs over P(S)Cell Scheduler
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4598\_replaced([11187352](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvaMf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Dynamic Long PUCCH Token Maintenance for UEs over Scell Scheduler

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-2 HARQ Processing DL HARQ buffer indexing towards L2-LO (ID: 11149470)

**2.2.5.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11149474`)

HARQ Processing
For an initial DL HARQ transmission requested via LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq 5G-L2-PS shall provide an unused (free) dlHarqBufferIndex defined in 5G\_L2\_1976\_replaced([11217544](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_ElavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The dlHarqBufferIndex is associated with the requested transport block and shall be used to address this transport block within 5G-L2-LO for any possibly following HARQ retransmission. Earliest by freeing the DL HARQ process the dlHarqBufferIndex can be considered free. 5G-L2-PS doesn’t have to inform 5G-L2-LO about releasing the HARQ process. Note, the management of dlHarqBufferIndex is left to implementation.

[5GC000526-A] For the artificial PDSCH load, there are no HARQ retransmissions; no HARQ buffer nor HARQ process aging are needed; dlHARQBufferIndex = 0 is always used.

CP2 references: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4528\_replaced([11184139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) DL HARQ processing

See also: 5G\_L2\_1976\_replaced([11217544](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_ElavvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G-L2-LO shall implement the DL HARQ Buffer for HARQ operation.

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-3 HARQ Processing Control of the DL HARQ Process Aging (ID: 11149481)

**2.2.5.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13389030`)

HARQ Processing
An allocated DL HARQ Process is made available again (for a re-transmission or new transmission) after the HARQ feedback for the ongoing transmission is received from L1-DL (UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD). This requires that L2-PS handles the case that the L1-L2 message providing HARQ feedback gets lost (for whatever reason), to avoid keeping an HARQ Process indefinitely blocked.**If long PUCCH is configured then DL Harq feedback can be received by UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD too.**

The strategy below is followed:

- Each time that a new HARQ process is allocated (new transmission) or that an HARQ re-transmission is scheduled, L2-PS stamps the corresponding HARQ process i with the current time (tHARQtx(i)) and stores it in the HARQ database;

- When a new transmission has to be scheduled (no higher priority re-transmissions are pending) but no free HARQ Processes are available anymore, L2-PS checks for all the HARQ processes how long they have been waiting for the HARQ feedback; if they have been waiting longer than rrmMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTime\_us, L2-PS assumes that the HARQ feedback got lost and behaves as in case of HARQ failure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4532\_replaced([11184193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

FOR(All the HARQ Processes i of the given UE and subcell)

IF( tcurrent - tHARQtx(i) > rrmMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTime\_us ) THEN ‘behave as in case of HARQ failure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4532\_replaced([11184193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))’;

where:

* rrmMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTime\_us = rdMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTimeSlots \* 125us, for above 6GHz
* rrmMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTime\_us = rdMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTimeSlots \* 500us, for below 6GHz

rdMaxHarqFeedbackWaitTimeSlots is defined in 5G\_L2\_14299\_replaced([11183412](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27jXVvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR868177]

For T+T UL CA, when symbol muting is needed, check if there are any HARQ processes which were allocated before the muting request. If ‘yes’, then increment failShortenSymbolHarqInUseCount. If failShortenSymbolHarqInUseCount is equal rdMaxNumFailShortenSymbolHarqInUse ([13389048](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QgBXEAMzEfGozuGzRUXHpg?oslc_config)) then release all HARQ processes which were allocated before muting request and set failShortenSymbolHarqInUseCount to 0.

[End PR868177]

For the artificial PDSCH load, there are no HARQ retransmissions; no HARQ buffer nor HARQ process aging are needed.

When an HARQ process is released due to HARQ aging, 5G-L2-PS shall obtain the PUCCH receiving time from the HARQ data transmission time. Then according to the PUCCH time, 5G-L2-PS shall free the item in the related position of PUCCH bookkeeping table (5G\_L2\_280\_replaced([11149452](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24WSUvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-4 HARQ Processing Control of the DL HARQ Process Aging for Harq processes to be scheduled (ID: 11149496)

**2.2.5.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11149508`)

HARQ Processing
rdMaxHarqTxWaitTimeSlots [CNI-109641-G], defined in 5G\_L2\_3930\_replaced([11183427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27jXWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), [End CNI-109641-G] is the maximum number of Slots a HARQ Process can await its UE to be scheduled for new/re transmission.

After that Delay, the HARQ is released by a periodic garbage collector.

Its default value 300 is aligned on L1CapacityLimit and determined by features CB006667 and CB007859

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-5 HARQ Processing Control of the DL HARQ Process Aging for DL re-transmission blocking (ID: 11149515)

**2.2.5.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11149523`)

HARQ Processing
A new timer per DL HARQ process ID is defined by rdPerHarqTxWaitSlots (refer to 5G\_L2\_22536\_replaced([11183438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27jXXfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), which shall be started when DL re-transmission is blocked due to lack of PDSCH symbols in case PDCCH symbols increasing.

When the blocked DL re-transmission is unblocked and gets scheduled again, the timer corresponding to this DL HARQ process shall be stopped if it's running.

When this timer expiry per HARQ process ID is detected, the corresponding HARQ re-transmission shall be discarded and HARQ shall be released.

The original transmission shall rely on the RLC re-transmission.

Note:

This is only applicable for DL of TDD FR1 and FDD.

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-6 HARQ Processing Reporting of number of availiable contexts in DL HARQ database (ID: 11149529)

**2.2.5.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11149535`)

HARQ Processing
Reporting of number of DL Harq contexts from DL HARQ database per cellgroup is reported in PsCell\_getResourceUsageResp 5G\_L2\_IF\_1659\_replaced([10973195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Uzpxfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-7 HARQ Processing Maximum number of DL HARQ transmissions (ID: 11149541)

**2.2.5.2.0-7.0-5**  (ID: `11149572`)

HARQ Processing
5G-L2-PS shall support maximum number of DL HARQ transmissions as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3428\_replaced([11153485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksmwFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Msg4 and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4532\_replaced([11184193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for other PDSCH transmissions. [Before CNI-130361]unless rdHARQDisabled (see 5G\_L2\_1882\_replaced([11183313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27iwQvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) equals '1'. In that case no retransmissions are done and 5G-L2-PS shall behave as if maxDlHarqTx, rdMaxDlHarqMsg4 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10801\_replaced([11153242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksk66vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  and maxDlHarqTxDrb (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_397\_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) were equal to '1'.

Notes:

* For maxDlHarqTx definition please see 5G\_L2\_IF\_22\_replaced([10966457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UOa_vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_IF\_47\_replaced([10966782](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UQQMfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CNI-130361]

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-8 HARQ Processing Scheduling of a retransmission (ID: 11149578)

**2.2.5.2.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11149592`)

HARQ Processing
5G-L2-PS shall follow requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4532\_replaced([11184193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to schedule a retransmission.

* If the adaptive re-transmission scheme is activated (/NRBTS/NRCELL/actAdaptiveReTxResMcs is set to TRUE) and applied as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11943\_replaced([11184268](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvRCjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):
* TBS shall be calculated, as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4621\_replaced([11192057](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kviITvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), with the MCS of the initial transmission and conditions of the retransmissions (number of PRB, rank, number of DMRS symbols etc...).

If the retransmission TBS is equal to the initial transmission TBS, the initial MCS shall be used for to schedule the retransmission. If the retransmission TBS is different from the initial transmission TBS, a reserved MCS shall be used for the retransmission.

* If the adaptive re-transmission scheme is deactivated (/NRBTS/NRCELL/actAdaptiveReTxResMcs is set to FALSE) or not applied as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11943\_replaced([11184268](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvRCjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):
* If for a FDD cell actLteNrDssLteCatM is activated and there is rateMatching in the slot (TRS, ZP CSI-RS (CSI-IM), slot 0 or slot 5), the reservedMCS shall be used if the calculated coding rate is higher than 0.95.

**[Before CNI-136855-A] In - If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True, reserved MCS can be applied for a retransmission if the number of PRBs is different than for the initial transmission, that is to say if the last RBG is used in the retransmission and not the initial transmission, or vice-versa.** [End CNI-136855-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-136855-A] If the NIDD parameter NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true,** in case of TDD mode with TRS/SSB slots, if a retransmission of an initial transmission granted as a RAT1 or dynamicswitch RAT1 allocation is scheduled and the PRB granularity is greater than 1 PRB then L2-PS shall roundup the number of PRBs to the next PRB granularity and if the number of PRBs is different from the initial transmission then L2-PS shall apply reserved MSC for retransmission. Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23663\_replaced([11177504](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuveHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **[End CNI-136855-A]**\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-136855-A] The same or different CDM group(s) without data as initial transmission; The different CDM group(s) without data can be used only when reserved MCS(refer to 5G\_UP\_IF\_1897\_replaced([11515718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tUO_Wvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) used in retransmission. Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4532\_replaced([11184193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24656\_replaced([11192358](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvj9ePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** [End CNI-136855-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-136855-A] If NRBTS/NRCELL/actVoNRIncCodingGain is set to TRUE, then a VoNR UE scheduled for retransmission is eligible to get allocated number of PRBs greater than their initial transmission. The UE is scheduled for retransmission with reserved MCS (refer to 5G\_UP\_IF\_1897\_replaced([11515718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tUO_Wvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 3GPP 38.214, clause 5.1.3.1) . Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14946\_replaced([11185337](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvSQp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** **[End CNI-136855-A]**\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-136855-A] In case of scheduling of Transient phase UE using RAT1 in the initial BWP(coreset #0), if the number of RBs used in retransmission is not same as RBs in initial transmission, then reserved MCS shall be used to schedule the UE  to avoid retransmission failure. Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4622\_replaced([11192072](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvivUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** [End CNI-136855-A]\*\*\*\*

If reserved MCS is to be used, the selected reserved MCS shall be the one with the same modulation order as the initial MCS.

In any case, the TBS of the initial transmission is the TBS used to fill DlData\_PdschSendReq.

**[CNI-136855-A]  Note: - If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True, reserved MCS usage is described in dedicated part, see 5G\_L2\_3197\_replaced([11164814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25vZe_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** [End CNI-136855-A]\*\*\*\*

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-9 HARQ Processing Scheduling of the retransmission in case of PDCCH symbol(s) sharing with PDSCH (ID: 11149597)

**2.2.5.2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11149604`)

HARQ Processing
5G-L2-PS shall follow the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25288\_replaced([11183118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvH4nfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to schedule a retransmission with [Before PR766243] n=5 [End PR766243][PR766243] n=20 [End PR766243] slots.

 If   retxPostponeCounter == 5  //the retransmission is being blocked for too long

Drop the retransmission and free the HARQ process.

 If   retxPostponeCounter == 1...4 //there is the same number of symbols in the slot as in an initial transmission. Then 5G-L2-PS schedule a retransmission with the initial transmission MCS, PRBs and symbols and retxPostponeCounter=0.

---

#### 2.2.5.2.0-10 HARQ Processing Blocked transmissions (ID: 11149612)

**2.2.5.2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11149616`)

HARQ Processing
The scheduling of a UE could be blocked in the following cases, leading to a loss of the allocated PDSCH and PDCCH resources. The cases are the following:

* For a cell with actLteNrDssLteCatM activated and adaptiveRetx deactivated, retransmissions on slots with rate Matching for CsiRs or for Pbch are blocked if the number of resources in the retransmission slot is lower than the initial number of resources \* rdDlRetransMinFraction / 100. rdDlRetransMinFraction  is defined in 5G\_L2\_2907\_replaced([11192014](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28hAtfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* No Free Harq has been found to schedule an initial transmission, even after freeing too old Harq process as described in 5G\_L2\_284\_replaced([11149481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24WSV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_3936\_replaced([11149496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24WSWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* No valid SLIV (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2373\_replaced([11115215](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpr--_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has been found

---

### 2.2.5.3 Configuration of 5G-L2-LO for Transport Block Transmission

#### 2.2.5.3.0-1 Configuration of 5G-L2-LO for Transport Block Transmission Requesting Transport Block building from 5G-L2-LO (ID: 11149629)

**2.2.5.3.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `12750115`)

Configuration of 5G-L2-LO for Transport Block Transmission
5G-L2-PS shall request the new to be built Transport Blocks (concerns initial HARQ transmissions only, excludes RA Msg2) by sending the message LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq for each of them to 5G-L2-LO. See 5G\_L2\_IF\_864\_replaced([10984513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WAjr_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details. The DL MAC PDU assembly is described in 5G\_L2\_1960\_replaced([11216443](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2--exPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The Transport Block of RA msg2 is built by 5G-L2-PS (see 5G\_L2\_318\_replaced([11149693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24XgefvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) without L2-LO involvement, therefore no LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq is sent.

In case of above 6Ghz configuration 5G-L2-PS shall send the LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq message with **sfnToL1 and slotToL1 corresponding to the slot for which L2-LO shall send DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq to L1**.\*\*\*\*

The IEs sfn and subframeNumber/NR-Slot represent the TTI when the TB shall be on air. Note, from them 5G-L1-Dl derives the start of the corresponding L1 buffer.

The IE tbStartOffset of LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq represents the relative start offset of the TB within subcell’s L1 buffer (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_79).

The IEs tbIndex & tbStartOffset are set according to 5G\_L2\_319\_replaced([11149707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Xge_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The IE pdschPayloadTbSendReqAddress shall be set to the address where 5G-L2-LO shall send DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq to (containing the built TB). This address is provided by DlData\_AddressResp (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_36).

If rdDlAlwaysScheduled is set to 1 and the TB was not allocated to any logical channel (in case of continuous DL scheduling without data availability, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10510\_replaced([11185475](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTexfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if the number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data is 1, change the number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data to 2, and recalculate the determined Transport Block size (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6874\_replaced([11192598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvlypfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

The IE tbSize shall be set to the determined Transport Block size.

The IE numOfRbs shall be set to the number of logical channels which have been allocated resources in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4543\_replaced([11185517](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTez_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SRBs or in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4550\_replaced([11185672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvUs7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DRBs.

However, if rdDlAlwaysScheduled is set to 1 and no logical channel has been allocated DL TB resources (in case of continuous DL scheduling without data availability) then numOfRbs shall be set to 1.

The corresponding RB parameters are set like this:

amountBytes shall be set to the value determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4543\_replaced([11185517](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTez_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SRBs and in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4550\_replaced([11185672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvUs7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DRBs.

However, if rdDlAlwaysScheduled is set to 1 and no logical channel has been allocated DL TB resources (in case of continuous DL scheduling without data availability) then amountBytes shall be set to tbSize less the size of MAC CEs to be included. L2-PS shall consider the 5G-MAC subheader size, given in 5G\_L2\_1970\_replaced([11215653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-5mSPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and the MAC CE payload size, given in 5G\_L2\_1971\_replaced([11215683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-5mTfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall set the isL2PsLChBufferEmpty IE according to the following condition:

* Shall be set to true, when the amount of data pending in 5G-L2-PS internal buffer for that logical channel before this allocation is greater than zero and less than or equal to the data being allocated (amountBytes), meaning the buffer is emptied with this allocation. The 'data pending in internal buffer' means logical channel buffer size after accounting for any previous allocations in the current slot
* Otherwise shall be set to false

If the Transport Block contains SRB1 data, 5G-L2-PS shall set the logicalChannelIdentity to 1 (corresponds to SRB1)

If the Transport Block contains SRB2 data, 5G-L2-PS shall set the logicalChannelIdentity to 2 (corresponds to SRB2)

If the Transport Block contains SRB3 data, 5G-L2-PS shall set the logicalChannelIdentity to 3 (corresponds to SRB3) and the corresponding IE amountBytes to tbSize.

If the Transport Block contains DRB data, 5G-L2-PS shall set the logicalChannelIdentity to the value of this bearer

[Before CNI-157970] If rdDlAlwaysScheduled is set to 1 and the TB was not allocated to any logical channel (in case of continuous DL scheduling without data availability, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10510\_replaced([11185475](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvTexfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then the logicalChannelIdentity shall be set to one of UE’s logical channels set up (excluding 0). Note, in this case 5G-L2-LO adds only padding bits to the TB. [End CNI-157970]

If the Transport Block contains CCCH data (SRB0), 5G-L2-PS shall set the logicalChannelIdentity to zero (corresponds to SRB0) and the corresponding IE amountBytes to IE sizeOfRrcMsg received in LoCtrl\_CcchDataInd. See also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3453\_replaced([11153402](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksmJBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details.

If the Transport Block contains the MAC CE for Contention Resolution Identity (CRI) (RA Msg4), then 5G-L2-PS shall set the IE ueCriMacCeAvail to true.

If the transmission of a TA command is pending, according to the decision taken by the UL Time Alignment Control (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3303\_replaced([11150011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksRY6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then IEs taMacCeAvail, taMacCeValue are set accordingly, otherwise they are both set to 0. Note: during the integration phase, the sending of DL MAC CE shall not be enabled (taMacCeAvail = 0) as long as it is not supported by the test UE.

If the Transmission Block contains a PDCCH TCI State Indication MAC CE as decided in (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2104\_replaced([11112678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpYc9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the IEs pdcchTciMacCeAvail shall be set to true.

The IE dlHarqBufferIndex shall be set as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4531\_replaced([11184177](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The IE requestType shall be set to "TB build request".

The IE requestType should be set to "dummy TB build request" for the artificial PDSCH load generation. The values for some other elements are defined as below:

* The IEs ueCriMacCeAvail, taMacCeAvail and sCellActDeactMacCeAvail shall be set to “false”.
* numOfRbs, tbIndex, tbStartOffset, dlHarqBufferIndex shall be set to “0”.

If the requestType is set to "TB build request" (request is not for artificial load generation) and actOptimizedFlowControl == OptimizedAllUe, L2-PS shall:

* store eTh values from request in Ue context as lastSentEth to be used in 5G\_L2\_10486\_replaced([11150890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1O_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* (re-)start rdEthUpdateTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15747\_replaced([11193522](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvtucfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), **5G\_L2\_17329\_replaced([11150910](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1PvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

When more than one MAC CE scheduled in one MAC PDU and the total size of all MAC CEs is bigger than MAC PDU size, the MAC CE should be multiplexed according to the following sequence:

1. TA MAC CE
2. Scell Activation/Deactivation MAC CE
3. PDCCH TCI State Indication MAC CE

The IE maxPdschPayloadSize shall be set to the value of IE maxPdschPayloadSize of DlData\_AddressResp.

---

#### 2.2.5.3.0-2 Configuration of 5G-L2-LO for Transport Block Transmission Requesting Transport Block retransmission from 5G-L2-LO (ID: 11149669)

**2.2.5.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11149680`)

Configuration of 5G-L2-LO for Transport Block Transmission
5G-L2-PS shall request the HARQ retransmission of Transport Blocks (5G-MAC PDUs) by sending the message LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq for each of them to 5G-L2-LO. See 5G\_L2\_IF\_864\_replaced([10984513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WAjr_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on the message.

The IEs sfn and subframeNumber/NR-Slot  represent the TTI when the TB shall be on air. Note, from them 5G-L1-Dl derives the start of the corresponding L1 buffer.

The IE tbStartOffset of LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq represents the relative start offset of the TB within subcell’s L1 buffer (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_79).

The IEs tbIndex & tbStartOffset are set according to 5G\_L2\_319\_replaced([11149707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Xge_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The IE pdschPayloadTbSendReqAddress shall be set to the address where 5G-L2-LO shall send DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq to (containing the built TB). This address is provided by DlData\_AddressResp (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_36).

The IE tbSize shall be set to the value used in the corresponding initial HARQ transmission.

The IE requestType shall be set to "TB reTx request".

The IE dlHarqBufferIndex shall be set to the value used in the corresponding initial HARQ transmission.

5G-L2-PS doesn’t need to add information on included logical channels (by e.g. IE amountRbs = 0) or 5G-MAC CEs.

[CB012979-H] The IE maxPdschPayloadSize shall be set to the value of IE maxPdschPayloadSize of DlData\_AddressResp. [End CB012979-H]

---

### 2.2.5.4 Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission

#### 2.2.5.4.0-1 Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission Building Transport Block for RA Msg2 and Requesting PDSCH Payload Transmission from L1-DL (ID: 11149693)

**2.2.5.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11149700`)

Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission
5G-L2-PS shall build the Transport Block of RA Msg2 as described in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_177\_replaced([11186242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Be_oQ_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (without L2-LO involvement).

5G-L2-PS shall request the transmission of the built RA Msg2 Transport Block by sending the message DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq to 5G-L1-DL. See 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_79 for details.

In case of above6GHz 5G-L2-PS shall send the DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq message for RA Msg2 scheduled in NR-slot n in the beginning of the next NR-slot n+1, as depicted in 5G\_L2\_353\_replaced([11151020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24gDUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). By this, the corresponding receive window of L1-DL (defined in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_132) is respected. Note, this isn't needed for below6Ghz configuration.

The IEs sfn and subframeNumber/NR-Slot represent the TTI when the TB shall be on air.

[Before PR527935]

The IE tbFragmentOffset is set to 0

The IE tbIndex is set to 0.

[End PR527935]

[PR527935] The IEs tbIndex & tbFragmentOffset are set according to 5G\_L2\_319\_replaced([11149707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Xge_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR527935]

The IE tbFragmentSize is set to the Transport Block size (payload in bytes).

Note, the MSC related to the contention based RA procedure to be supported by the DL and UL schedulers is specified in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_183\_replaced([11187006](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfDSqfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.2.5.4.0-2 Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission Calculating tbIndex &amp; tbStartOffset_bits (or tbStartOffset) for every transport block requested from L1-DL (ID: 11149707)

**2.2.5.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12806598`)

Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission
For every TB to be requested from L1-DL, the following is calculated:

- The IE tbIndex is set to 0 for the first TB in slot and is incremented by 1 for every Transport block requested.

For the same TB, the same value is set in both LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq & DlData\_PdschSendReq messages.

For Paging Message (when L2PS sends DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq, see 5G\_L2\_824\_replaced([11173540](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26b9DPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) the IE *tbIndex in               DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq is set equal to* tbIndex in DlData\_PdschSendReq.\*\*

- The IE tbStartOffset*\_bits is calculated as follows:*

*tbStartOffset\_bits[i]= 32* [ ( TBStartOffset\_bits[i-1] + tbSize\_bits[i-1] ) DIV 32 + 1],\*

where i represents the current TB and i-1 represents the previous TB & *TBStartOffset\_bits[0]=0*

For the same TB, the IE *tbStartOffset  in LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq is set equal to the IE* tbStartOffset\_bits in DlData\_PdschSendReq\*\*

For RA Msg2 (when L2PS sends DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq, see 5G\_L2\_318\_replaced([11149693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24XgefvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the IE tbFragmentOffset in DlData\_PdschPayloadTbSendReq is set equal to \*tbStartOffset\_bits in DlData\_PdschSendReq

[CB013100-A-UPD004] If UE allocation is affected by FD-POLITE PRB widening loop (see [12533165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_jm0A4Bw4EfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) IE tbStartOffset\_bits shall be calculated based on final tbSize\_bits value in the last successful FD-POLITE attempt. [End CB013100-A-UPD004]\*

---

#### 2.2.5.4.0-3 Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission Sending DlData_PdschSendReq (ID: 11149724)

**2.2.5.4.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11149758`)

Configuration of 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission
**[Before CNI-116869-D]**

For every to-be-scheduled UE, the following information is sent to the L1 DL using DlData\_PdschSendReq : (for artificial load UE, see 5G\_L2\_1816\_replaced([11212192](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-joCvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- subcellId -- as determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4327\_replaced([11177617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **when subcellDeactivationDlAllowed  = false, refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15393\_replaced([11212871](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDyS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when subcellDeactivationDlAllowed = true**

- mcs -- *rrmDlUsedMcs as determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4630\_replaced([11192270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvjWafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (original MCS* rrmDlProposedMcs is calculated while taking the amount of allocated resources into consideration)\*\*

- rat0Bitmap -- created based on the above allocation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4459\_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Note: The MSB of Frequency resource Assignment in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4459\_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is the first RBG of the BWP. The MSB of rat0Bitmap is the first RBG from CRB0.

- startPrb -- The first PRB in the first RBG used by the UE

if isAny**DlPrbPoolingActive is set to 'false'   (Refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_14\_replaced([10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for this flag)**

- numOfPrb -- The number of RBGs times the RBG size *P (For first and last RBG use value in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4459\_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))*

Else

- numOfPrb -- The number of RBGs times the RBG size P which don't exceed the number of usable RBG of size P computed by the numAllocCellPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4279\_replaced([11177002](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kurzwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (For first and last RBG use value in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4459\_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In case of a retransmission, if numAllocCellPrb is less than the size needed for the retransmission, then processing mentioned in requirement  5G\_L2\_4109\_replaced([11174562](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26lG8fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) should be applied and if the HARQ process is freed, the DLHarqBufferIndex should also be freed.

endif

- tbSize\_bits -- *tbSize as determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4630\_replaced([11192270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvjWafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*

- Nscid – its value is provided by SD scheduler for each CS2 list (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4412\_replaced([11142400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- antPort – the DMRS ports for PDSCH. Its value is provided by SD scheduler for each CS2 list (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4412\_replaced([11142400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- dlDmrsLen – the number of frontload DMRS symbols. Its value is provided by SD scheduler for each CS2 list (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4412\_replaced([11142400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- dmrsScramblingSequenceInt – the initial scrambling ID for DMRS of PDSCH. Its value is provided by SD scheduler for each CS2 list (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4412\_replaced([11142400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

The parameters startPrb &  numOfPrb are redundant with rat0Bitmap but they are needed in L1 in order to facilitate rate maching.

**[CNI-116869-D]**

For every to-be-scheduled UE, a DlData\_PdschSendReq is created with the grant filled according to 5G\_L2\_887\_replaced([11178401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26_9tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For artificial load UE, see 5G\_L2\_1816\_replaced([11212192](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-joCvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[End CNI-116869-D]**

Whenever a DlData\_PdschSendReq message is sent, the parameter *rrmNumScheduledUesDlSlot shall be incremented by the number of UEs handled by the message (e.g. 1 msg per UE for non-bundled interface messages). The parameter is reset to 0 with every slot. After DL scheduling is complete, L2PS updates the PM counters in 5G\_L2\_348\_replaced([11197550](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_29M9KvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) using this parameter.*

**[Before CNI-116869-D]**

CP2 reference:

5G\_UP\_ALG\_4510\_replaced([11181328](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku-Hn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) FD resource allocation for FDM (Random)

**[End CNI-116869-D]**
