5G-L2-PS will align PucchAreaBoundaries-->eCpriConfig-->numCeAxCIndex and ceAxCIndex same as eCpriConfig under each RNTI. (PucchAreaBoundaries will be used for eCPRI enabled cases alone, so will be set to default value (reset) in other cases.

Common PUCCH Boundary creation 5G-L2-PS will  send the boundaries of the fragment (start and end PRB) that specifies the common PUCCH allocation. This includes both the upper and lower edge , before and after frequency hopping. However unlike dedicated PUCCH, this fragment will specify  the PRBs that are actually scheduled in common PUCCH instead of sending the whole region for common PUCCH.

But if there are empty PRB's identified in the Common PUCCH area (ex:case: 3 Upper and 3 Lower PRB Common PUCCH scenarios, Scenario 12 in xls below) sending absolute PRB will not be feasible with 5G\_L1\_IF\_14907\_replaced([11514064](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0zLfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) interface. Hence 5G-L2-PS shall create common PUCCH area boundary considering the empty PRB into the area identified Such that the empty PRBs are not present in top and bottom of the area sent to L1.

This approach is adapted to ensure that all the scheduled PRBs in Common PUCCH are included the PUCCH boundaries sent to L1

Possible combination of PUCCH area boundary examples with different configurations are captured in CB008941\_PossibleBoundaryCombination\_L1L2.xlsx

<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Forms/Tree_View.aspx?csf=1&web=1&e=vxrqTw&cid=2ee64709%2D1b3a%2D4d43%2Db388%2D0324540f3d3c&RootFolder=%2Fsites%2F5Gdoc%2FAS%5FTech%5FSpec%2FDrawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G%2FUser%20Plane%2F5G%20L2%20Entity%20Level%2F2%205G%2DL2%2DPS%20Component%20Requirements&FolderCTID=0x012000F0A0A3BA325F7648AD307E6959BA7376>

---

###### 2.2.7.1-1.0-2 PM Counter Support UlData_PucchReceiveReq (ID: 11150803)

**2.2.7.1-1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11150820`)

PM Counter Support
5G-L2-PS shall send a single UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message to 5G-L1-UL of each subcell with at least one allocated PUCCH resource on a given slot for PUCCH reception.

For UE configured with Carrier Aggregation with at least one SCell PUCCH transmission is allocated only on PSCell (Joint-UCI), 5G-L2-PS shall send a UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message to 5G-L1-UL of an PSCell to request the reception of PUCCH on that subcell.

If HARQ feedback is expected at a given slot, UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message shall be sent to the corresponding subcell managing the PUCCH reception after DL scheduling of the last DL slot mapped to this slot and include any CSI or SR report reception which is expected in the same slot. Otherwise, message timing is relative to any CSI or SR report reception

For the timing requirement when UlData\_PucchReceiveReq is expected to be received by 5G-L1-UL please refer to 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_293 and 5G\_L2\_353\_replaced([11151020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24gDUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For analog beamforming for eCPRI RUs, L2 PS shall indicate beam of the corresponding UE through ceAxcIndex and patternId in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq according to 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_215 as

ceAxcIndex  eAxC index of default data for D2 subcell type according to 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1516 and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5161\_replaced([11204321](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

patternId  map beam Id to pattern Id according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1909\_replaced([11111524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE: Linked to both 5GC000399 and 5GC000918 features to avoid creating a dependency on their mutual implementation order. And based on CP3 discussion, 5GC000399-KX will fill ceAxcIndex and patternId.

In the Scell of FDD-TDD CA (FR1) [5GC001167-H]or FDD-FDD CA [End 5GC001167-H], L2-PS will not send UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message to 5G-L1-UL after each PDSCH scheduling but send the scheduling result, including scheduling info[5GC001167-H](not applicable to FDD-FDD CA)[End 5GC001167-H]for CA-UE and allocated PUCCH resource[5GC001167-H](not applicable to FDD-FDD CA)[End 5GC001167-H] to P(S)Cell L2-PS.

Before sending UlData\_PucchReceiveReq for any subcell, 5G-L2-PS shall judge whether certain subcell shall be buffered according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5214\_replaced([11209976](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw298fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). bufferedUlConfig is a structure used in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq to control buffered UL usage and it shall be filled regardless of whether buffered UL is used or not (5G\_L1\_5G21A\_264).

CP2 reference:

5G\_UP\_ALG\_4602\_replaced([11187378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvazhPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PUCCH Reception request with Long PUCCH

---

##### 2.2.7.1.1 Requesting PUCCH reception

###### 2.2.7.1.1.0-1 Requesting PUCCH reception Transmission timing of  UlData_PucchReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL (ID: 11150472)

**2.2.7.1.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11150490`)

Requesting PUCCH reception
In the implementation, PUCCH Reception Request is sent after the FD scheduling for each subcell because for carrier aggregation UE, the total number of ACK/NACK bit is needed. The PUCCH Reception Request sending is put together with PDCCH sending as 5G\_L2\_278\_replaced([11150432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24cY8fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Further timing aspects concerning Long PUCCH are given in 5G\_L2\_9898\_replaced([11150497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24cY_PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq for the UEs with Harq-Ack timing N+K1aCsi (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4331\_replaced([11177668](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be delayed until the slot N’ corresponding to the latest DL scheduler occasion with regular k1 timing (i.e. that slot N’ for which N + k1aCsi = N’ +k1), is completed. [CB009510-A-UPD001] Precalculated K1 timing can be redundant and may not coincide with the fact that the slot is schedulable (for that actual K1 timings, set at the very moment needs to be checked). [End CB009510-A-UPD001] The transmitted UlData\_PucchReceiveReq shall be unified with the PUCCH reception requests corresponding available in last DL scheduling N’ for non A-CSI UEs.

---

###### 2.2.7.1.1.0-2 Requesting PUCCH reception Instance handling UlData_PucchReceiveReq (ID: 11150497)

**2.2.7.1.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11150507`)

Requesting PUCCH reception
In FDD [CB006064-A] and TDD FR1 [End CB006064-A], with long PUCCH configured, k1 > k2 > 1 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2473\_replaced([11116092](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2484\_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Hence DL and UL scheduler have at least ca. 2 slots time to synchronize wrt. requesting PUCCH or PUSCH reception from L1, based on the time duration between end of UL scheduling and end of corresponding L1 PUCCH/PUSCH receive windows (see also 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_280). It is up to implementation to decide whether the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message handling shall be kept in DL Scheduler or moved to UL Scheduler, both should be possible with the time budget.

---

##### 2.2.7.1.2 PUCCH reception handling

###### 2.2.7.1.2.0-1 PUCCH reception handling Reception of UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD or UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD (ID: 11150521)

**2.2.7.1.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11150531`)

PUCCH reception handling
Upon reception of UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD or UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD, 5G-L2-PS shall perform:

* DL HARQ Handling (5G\_UP\_ALG\_12737\_replaced([11184145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),
* R&D Counter Handling for ACK/NACK bits on PUSCH as described in 5G\_L2\_302\_replaced([11150602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24dAD_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),
* [CB009189-B] Counter handling as described in 5G\_L2\_8084\_replaced([11150707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOIPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_8086\_replaced([11150721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_8099\_replaced([11150731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOJPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_8101\_replaced([11150745](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB009189-B].

Notes:

* The ACK/NACK bits of ackNack IE are representing ACK/NACK of TB sent via each scheduled Cell in the UE according to counter DAI and total DAI in the DCI. In implementation, the mapping between bit and SCell info can be obtained from the bookkeeping table in 5G-L2-PS which is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4592\_replaced([11187305](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvaMdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 2.2.7.1.2.0-2 PUCCH reception handling Reception of xPUCCH Information from 5G-L1-UL (ID: 11150538)

**2.2.7.1.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13362778`)

PUCCH reception handling
For each UlData\_PucchReceiveReq, 5G-L2-PS shall receive xPUCCH information from 5G-L1-UL via the messages UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD[CNI-136896-A], see [11514174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ),[End CNI-136896-A] and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs[CNI-136896-A], see [11514246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BUPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)[End CNI-136896-A].

For each UlData\_PuschReceiveReq requesting reception of UCI multiplexed in PUSCH, L2-PS shall receive UCI information from 5G-L1-UL via the message UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD.

---

###### 2.2.7.1.2.0-3 PUCCH reception handling Decoding of F1 SR overlapping with F3 HARQ for UEs configured with power saving BWP (ID: 11150549)

**2.2.7.1.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11150554`)

PUCCH reception handling
This requirement applies only when actPowerSavingBwp is set to TRUE in the cell (5G\_L2\_IF\_95\_replaced([10968336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UXk5_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

When the UE has and both PUCCH F1 (for SR) and F3 (for HARQ feedback reporting) resources configured, L2-PS shall:

1) On SR occasion in slot with allocated F3 PUCCH resources for DL HARQ, request PUCCH reception from L1 for both resources (see 5G\_L2\_947\_replaced([11180342](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27MK8_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_954\_replaced([11180444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27MyA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), respectively).

Note: if SR is expected to be multiplexed in PUCCH F3 due to periodic CSI report, F1 request shall be skipped.

In case PUCCH response is received from L1 for both of these PUCCH resources, L2-PS shall:

1) Determine for both above-mentioned PUCCH formats, if positive SR can be detected there (from F1 – directly, from F3 – where SR can be multiplexed with HARQ feedback).

2) If positive SR can be found in any of these PUCCH resources, proceed with SR handling.

SFS reference and rationale: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31796\_replaced([11187407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvazifvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

See also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29170\_replaced([11111382](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpM2zPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rdActPuschDtxOnSrSlotForBwpScanning, R&D parameter that enables capability to consider a Dtx PUSCH on SR slot as a Dtx PUSCH triggered by an UL grant due a positive SR.

---

###### 2.2.7.1.2.0-4 PUCCH reception handling Routing of the PUCCH Response Messages to L2-PS (ID: 11150561)

**2.2.7.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11150567`)

PUCCH reception handling
UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs addresses in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq shall be configured such that both responses are directed to the DL Scheduler.

[5GC000885-A] If UCI is expected to be multiplexed in PUSCH then UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD address of UlData\_PuschReceiveReq shall be configured such that L1 sends UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD to the DL Scheduler. [end 5GC000885-A]

---

##### 2.2.7.1.3 PM Counter Support

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-1 PM Counter Support Scheduling Request (SR) on PUCCH format 1 R&amp;D Counter Support for successful reception (nonDTX case) (ID: 11150577)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11150583`)

PM Counter Support
In case of pucch format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220), that carried a successful received positive SR as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4615\_replaced([11187513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbamfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) the below specified R&D counters shall be incremented.

[5GC000885-E] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4615\_replaced([11187513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbamfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) describes how to distinguish successful and unsuccessful receptions of PUCCH format 1 if one or two DL HARQ A/N are expected in same slot as SR. [end 5GC000885-E].

For each grant with successfully received positive SR the cell related R&D counter

M55303CRD58001, aka SUCC\_SR\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1, shall be incremented. It describes the number of positive Scheduling Request (SR) indications that are successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) via message using PUCCH format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220).

SUCC\_SR\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1 =  SUCC\_SR\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1 + 1

Note: The R&D counter for SR reception via Pucch format 3 is described in 5G\_L2\_300\_replaced([11150590](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24dADfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

CP2 requirement(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-2 PM Counter Support Scheduling Request (SR) &amp; Periodic CSI on PUCCH format 3 R&amp;D Counter Support for successful reception (nonDTX case) (ID: 11150590)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11150596`)

PM Counter Support
Upon reception of ulData\_pucchReceiveRespPs message including grants of pucch format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220), that carry a successful received positive SR multiplexed with periodic CSI report below specified R&D counters shall be incremented.

For each grant including a successfully received positive SR the cell related R&D counter

M55303CRD59001, aka SUCC\_SR\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3, describe the number of Scheduling Request indications that are successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) via using PUCCH format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220) shall be increased.

SUCC\_SR\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3 = SUCC\_SR\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3 + 1

Note: The R&D counter for SR reception via Pucch format 1 is described in 5G\_L2\_298\_replaced([11150577](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24dAC_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For each grant including a successfully received periodic CSI report the cell related R&D counter

M55303CRD60001, aka SUCC\_PCSI\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3, describe the number of periodic CSI report indications that are successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) using PUCCH format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220).

SUCC\_PCSI\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3 =  SUCC\_PCSI\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3 + 1

These counters are an R&D counter.

CP2 requirement(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-3 PM Counter Support HARQ A/N on PUSCH R&amp;D Counter Support (ID: 11150602)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11150606`)

PM Counter Support
Upon reception of ulData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD message (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_209) L2-PS shall evaluate for each grant inside the meassage the structure ackOnPuschReportAndDtxMeas (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_210) regarding whether it was received correctly, contains ACK/NACK and increase respective R&D counter.

[CB006064-A]

Depending of the number of ACK/NACK bits N received in ackOnPuschReportAndDtxMeas structure the following processing shall be performed:

In the case that N=1 A/N bit is expected the values for 1 A/N bit feedback (dtxAck1bit and ackNack1bitUci) shall be evaluated:

[End CB006064-A]

If (dtxAck1bit == nonDtx) {

M55303CRD62001 = M55303CR62001 + 1 , aka PUSCH\_UCI\_NON\_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

grants that could be received due to nonDTX on UCI.

if (ackNack1bitUci = ack) {

M55303CRD56001 = M55303CRD56001 + 1 , aka HARQ\_ACK\_PUSCH\_BIN1.  This (histogram) R&D counter shall provide the               number of successfully received HARQ A/N indications containing 'ACK' via PUSCH, when A/N there is only 1 ACK/NACK bits                 on PUSCH.

}

else if (ackNack1bitUci == nack) {

M55303CRD57001 = M55303CRD57001 + 1 , aka HARQ\_NACK\_PUSCH\_BIN1.  This (histogram) R&D counter shall provide               the number of received HARQ A/N containing 'NACK' indications via PUSCH, when A/N there is only 1 ACK/NACK bits on               PUSCH.

}

else if (dtxAck1bit == Dtx) {

M55303CRD61001 = M55303CRD61001 + 1 , aka PUSCH\_UCI\_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

grants that could not be received due to DTX on UCI.}

}

[CB006064-A]

In the case that N>=2 A/N bits feedback are expected the values for more than 1 A/N bit feedback (dtxAckMoreThan1Bit and ackNackUciMoreThan1Bit) shall be evaluated:

If (dtxAckMorethan1Bit == nonDtx) {

M55303CRD62001 = M55303CR62001 + 1 , aka PUSCH\_UCI\_NON\_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

grants that could be received due to nonDTX on UCI.

for (n=0, n<N, ++n) {

if (ackNackUciMoreThan1Bit[n] == ack) ++ACKS

else if (ackNackUciMoreThan1Bit[n] == nack) ++NACKS

}

M55303CRD5600 = M55303CRD5600 + 1, aka HARQ\_ACK\_PUSCH\_BIN. This (histogram) R&D counter shall provide the number of successfully received HARQ A/N indications containing ACKS 'ACK' via PUSCH.

M55303CRD5700 = M55303CRD5700 + 1, aka HARQ\_NACK\_PUSCH\_BIN. This (histogram) R&D counter shall               provide the number of received HARQ A/N containing NACKS 'NACK' indications via PUSCH.

ACKS=0; NACKS=0;

}

else if (dtxAckMoreThan1bit == Dtx) {

M55303CRD61001 = M55303CRD61001 + 1 , aka PUSCH\_UCI\_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

grants that could not be received due to DTX on UCI.}

}

[end CB006064-A]

Note: For 885-A (FDD) there is only 1 ACK/NACK bit included. For later subfeatures the single R&D counters become histogram counter with 8 bins.

[5GC000885-E] Note: For 885-E the PM Counters were extended by CSI reports according to 5G\_L2\_304\_replaced([11150612](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24dnEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

CP2 requirement(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-4 PM Counter Support CSI on PUSCH R&amp;D Counter Support (ID: 11150612)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11150619`)

PM Counter Support
Upon reception of ulData\_PuschReceiveRespPs message (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_199) L2-PS shall evaluate for each report inside the meassage the structure csiOnPuschDtxMeas (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_202) regarding whether it was received correctly and increase respective R&D counter.

If (dtxCsiPart1 == nonDtx) {

M55303CRD62001 = M55303CR62001 + 1 , aka PUSCH\_UCI\_NON\_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

reports that could be received correctly due to nonDTX on UCI.

}

else if (dtxCsiPart1 == Dtx) {

M55303CRD61001 = M55303CRD61001 + 1 , aka PUSCH\_UCI\_DTX. This R&D counter shall provide the number of

reports that could not be received correctly due to DTX on UCI.}

}

Note: For 885-A the HARQ A/N on PUSCH was implemented for this PM Counters (see 5G\_UP\_1496\_replaced([11359646](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucpBlPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

CP2 requirement(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-5 PM Counter Support HARQ A/N on PUCCH R&amp;D Counter Support for successful reception (nonDTX case) (ID: 11150627)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11150635`)

PM Counter Support
"UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message (5G\_L1\_5G21A\_223) is received by L2-PS from UL-L1 cell related R&D Counters on UL UCI on PUCCH of class 'NR UL Signal Quality Level' shall be handled. For each grant/pucch allocation the 'dtx' field in the 'pucchDtxMeasurement' struct shall be evaluatied and for sucessful reception (dtx=nonDTX) the following R&D counters shall be processed.

The R&D counter are only used in cell configuration with long PUCCH. So depending on the Pucch format field ('pucchFormat' 1 or 3) of each pucch allocation two cases shal be distinguished:

Case 1: HARQ A/N on PUCCH format 1 successful detection

In case of pucch format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220) the following cell related R&D counters shall be incremented:

[5GC000885-E] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4615\_replaced([11187513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbamfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) describes how to distinguish successful and unsuccessful receptions of PUCCH format 1 if one or two DL HARQ A/N are expected in same slot as SR. [end 5GC000885-E].

The HARQ A/N R&D Counters for pucch format 1 shall be done the following steps:

1.) The number of HARQ bits nANPucch ( see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_218) in corresponding uldata\_pucchReceiveReq message shall be  assessed and in the array 'ackNack' (with up to 8 elements) of the pucch allocation insdie UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD   shall be evaluated. The number of ack ( =1 ) - bits called = 'numOfAcks' and nack (=0) bits called 'numOfNacks' inside the              ackNack array are counted.

2.)Depending on 'numOfAcks' ( 0.. 2 ):

M55303CRD52001 … M55303CRD52002 aka HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_BIN1 … HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_BIN2 dscribe the histogram for the number of 'acked' HARQ A/N indications included in the successfully received (dtx=nonDTX)               message using PUCCH format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220)

Switch ( numOfAcks) {

Case 1: HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_BIN1 = HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_BIN1 + 1;

Case 2: HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_BIN2 = HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT2\_BIN1 + 1;

}

3.)Depending on 'numOfNacks' ( 0.. 2 ):

M55303CRD53001 … M55303CRD53002 aka HARQ\_NACK\_AN\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_BIN1 … HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_BIN2 dscribe the histogram for the number of 'nacked' HARQ A/N indications included in the successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) message using PUCCH format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220)

Switch ( numOfNacks) {

Case 1: HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_BIN1 = HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_BIN1 + 1;

Case 2: HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_BIN2 = HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_BIN2 + 1;

}

Case 2: HARQ A/N on PUCCH format 3 successful detection

In case of pucch format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220) the follwoing cell related R&D counters shall be incremented:

The HARQ A/N R&D Counters for pucch format 3 shall be handled with the following steps:

1.) The number of HARQ bits nANPucch ( see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_218) in correspnding uldata\_pucchReceiveReq message shall be  assessed and in the array 'ackNack' (with up to 8 elements) of the pucch allocation insdie UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD  shall be evaluated. The number of ack ( =1 ) - bits called = 'numOfAcks' and nack (=0) bits called 'numOfNacks' inside the ackNack array are counted.

2.)Depending on 'numOfAcks' ( 0.. 8 ):

M55303CRD54001 … M55303CRD42008 aka HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN1 … HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN8  dscribe the histogram for the number of 'acked' HARQ A/N indications included in the successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) message using PUCCH format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220).

Switch ( numOfAcks) {

Case 1: HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN1 = HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN1 + 1;

Case 2: HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN2 = HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN2 + 1;

...

Case 8: HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN8 = HARQ\_ACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN8 + 1;

}

3.) Depending on 'numOfNacks' ( 0.. 8 ):

M55303CRD55001 … M55303CRD55008 aka HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN1 … HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN8 dscribe the histogram for the number of 'nacked' HARQ A/N indications included in the successfully received (dtx=nonDTX) message using PUCCH format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220)

Switch ( numOfNacks) {

Case 1: HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN1 = HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN1 + 1;

Case 2: HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN2 = HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN2 + 1;

...

Case 8: HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN8 = HARQ\_NACK\_PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_BIN8 + 1;

}

CP2 requirement(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-6 PM Counter Support UL PUCCH OFDM Symbol Usage PM Counter Support (ID: 11150642)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11150648`)

PM Counter Support
Upon sending of a "UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message (according to 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_215) by L2-PS to UL-L1 PM Counters of class 'NR Cell Utilitzation' related to used PUCCH OFDM symbols shall be incremented for the related subcell.

M55308C03004, aka PUCCH\_OFDM\_SYMBOLS, indicates the accumulated number (sum) of OFDM symbols used for PUCCH in the related subcell.

The UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message (5G\_L1\_5G21A\_215) shall contain a list of PUCCH resources per subcell that shall be used by 5G-L2-PS to trigger 5G-L1-UL to decode the NR UL slot. These UL resources shall be evaluated one-by-one:

1.) First the number of subcells in the message shall be determined

2.)  For each subcell the related cell shall be identified via subcellID mapping and shall be stored.

3.) Then the number of PUCCH resources inside the subcell shall be identifed via parameter 'numOfPucchResources'

4.)  Loop through the UL PUCCH resources by evaluation the parameters.

5.)  With parameter 'firstSymbol and numOfPucchSymbols' the number of OFDM PUCCH symbols shall be assessed

6.)  For the related cell's PM counter shall be incremented:

PUCCH\_OFDM\_SYMBOLS = PUCCH\_OFDM\_SYMBOLS + 'numOfPucchSymbols'

Note: Above process description is general considering multiple subcells per message and multiple PUCCH resources  per subcell. Starting with 1 subcell per cell and 1 PUCCH resource per subcell these numbers will be increased step-by-step by later features.

CP2 requirement(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-7 PM Counter Support UL PUCCH Quality PM Counters for successful (nonDTX) reception case (ID: 11150654)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-7.0-4**  (ID: `12526768`)

PM Counter Support
When a valid (dtx=nonDTX) "UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message (5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220) is received by L2-PS from UL-L1 PM Counters of class 'NR UL Signal Quality Level' shall be handled. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4615\_replaced([11187513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbamfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) describes how to distinguish successful and unsuccessful receptions of PUCCH format 1 if one or two DL HARQ A/N are expected in same slot as SR.

These PM counter statistics describe the distribution UL PUCCH Quality values by 6, 18- or 44 bin-histograms.

These PM counter(s) are defined per subcell and every UE's nonDTX UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs messages in this subcell are contributing to these counters.

The following PM counters / counter bins shall be incremented +1 in the non-DTX case.

1.) **PUCCH format 0 successful detection**

M55303C12001, aka PUCCH\_FORMAT0\_NON\_DTX, describes the number of valid (dtx=nonDTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 0 ('pucchFormat' == 0 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220).

2.) **PUCCH format 2 successful detection**

M55303C16001, aka PUCCH\_FORMAT2\_NON\_DTX, describes the number of valid (dtx=nonDTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 2 ('pucchFormat' == 2 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220).

3.) **UL RSSI on PUCCH Histogram**

M55303C09001… M55303C09044, aka UE\_RSSI\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_01 ... UE\_RSSI\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_44, are describing the received UE related RSSI for PUCCH Level xx. It is the UE related Received Signal Strenth Indicator  (RSSI) distribution for PUCCH containing also interference and noise. Measurement is calculated over all PRBs allocated for a UE and normalized to a single PRB. It is measured in the gNB and provided by UL-L1 in the parameter field 'rssi' (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220). The value is received in the unit dBm.

**[CB009543-A]**

In case of FDD supercell, RSSI considered for updating this set of counters is measured only from the PUCCH received from the UE's UL serving subcell. **[End CB009543-A]** [CB009543-B] RSSI values received from UE's UL non serving subcells are ignored for counter update.\*\*\*\*

**[End CB009543-B]**

The UL PUCCH RSSI histogram consists of 44 bins with 2dBm-width:

UE\_RSSI\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_01: [rssi <= -114dBm]

UE\_RSSI\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_02: [-114dBm < rssi <= -112dBm]

UE\_RSSI\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_03: [-112dBm < rssi <= -110dBm]

…

UE\_RSSI\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_44: [-30dBm < rssi]

Value -140dBm shall be considered as invalid and counter shall NOT be updated.

4.) **UL SINR on PUCCH Histogram**

M55303C08001… M55303C08018, aka UE\_SINR\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_01 ... UE\_SINR\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_18, are describing the received UE related SINR for PUCCH Level xx. It is the UE related Signal to Interference and Noise Ratio (SINR) distribution for PUCCH, measured in the gNB and provided by UL-L1 in the parameter field 'sinr'  ( see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220). The value is received in the unit dB.

**[CB009543-A]**

In case of FDD supercell, SINR considered for updating this set of counters is measured only from the PUCCH received from the UE's UL serving subcell. **[End CB009543-A]** [CB009543-B]SINR values received from UE's UL non serving subcells are ignored for counter update.\*\*\*\*

**[End CB009543-B]**

The UL PUCCH SINR histogram consists of 18 bins with 2dB-width:

UE\_SINR\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_01: [sinr <= -8dB]

UE\_SINR\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_02: [-8dB < sinr <= -6dB]

UE\_SINR\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_03: [-6dB < sinr <= -4dB]

…

UE\_SINR\_PUCCH\_LEVEL\_18: [24dB < sinr]

Only 1 layer transmission is supported. NO SINR averaging over two layers is not done.

When two separate SINR values for the two layers are received, dB-average shall be calculated and counter shall be updated only once. Introduced by multi-layer feature.

5.) **PUCCH format 1 successful detection**

M55303C14001, aka PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_NON\_DTX, describes the number of valid (dtx=nonDTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220). L2-PS shall not count/consider PUCCHs reporting SR only.

6.) **PUCCH format 3 successful detection**

M55303C18001, aka PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_NON\_DTX, describes the number of valid (dtx=nonDTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220).

7.) **PUCCH format 3 successful detection** with Rel.16 DMRS\*\*\*\*

Refer to 5G\_L2\_16103\_replaced([11193174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28pjivvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If useLatestPcsiMeasWhenSkipped is true, if a UlData\_PucchReceiveReq is skipped due to handling with actRedPeriodicCsiProcessing='True' as in [11173150: Control the ratio of PCSI/BM report recieve request reduction](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26ZgxPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), the counter for RSSI in 3.) and SINR in 4.) are updated according to the latest PUCCH PCSI measurement for the UE. The parameter useLatestPcsiMeasWhenSkipped is from PsCell\_CellSetupReq in [10974651: PsUser\_UserSetupReq Message Content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and can be modified by PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq in [10971056: PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq Message Content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

CP2 requirement(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-8 PM Counter Support UL PUCCH Quality PM Counters for unsuccessful (DTX) reception case (ID: 11150675)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-8.0-3**  (ID: `13362782`)

PM Counter Support
When a "UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message (5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220) is received by L2-PS from UL-L1 with the indication field 'dtx' = DTX, then PM Counters of class 'NR UL Signal Quality Level' shall be handled. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4615\_replaced([11187513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbamfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) describes how to distinguish successful and unsuccessful receptions of PUCCH format 1 if one or two DL HARQ A/N are expected in same slot as SR.

These PM counter statistics describe the distribution UL PUCCH Quality values by 6, 18- or 44 bin-histograms.

They provide information about the dtx metric distribution for the different PUCCH formats and UCI sizes for further evaluation and optimization. Different methodologies and algorithms are used for determination of the figures already in the hardware and provisioned by L1 to L2-PS. Therefore different decoding rules and bin borders for the histogram are applicable for the different cases.

These PM counter(s) are defined per subcell and every UE's not successful received ( dtx = DTX ) PUCCH transmission and its dedicated UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs messages from L1 to L2-PS messages in this subcell are contributing to these PM counters.

The following PM counters / counter bins shall be incremented +1 in the DTX case.

A. PM counters shall evaluate the unsuccessful reception of different PUCCH formats

The following PM counters shall be incremented + 1 in the DTX case, when the criteria are met in the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message arrives.

**a1.) PUCCH format 0 un-successful detection**

M55303C11001, aka PUCCH\_FORMAT0\_DTX, describes the number of invalid (dtx=DTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 0 ('pucchFormat' == 0 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220).

L2-PS shall not count/consider PUCCHs reporting SR only as from 3GPP pov. the negative SR is indicated by DTX which is no sign of bad signal quality.

**a2.) PUCCH format 2 un-successful detection**

M55303C15001, aka PUCCH\_FORMAT2\_DTX, describes the number of invalid (dtx=DTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 2 ('pucchFormat' == 2 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220).

**a3.) PUCCH format 1 un-successful detection**

M55303C13001, aka PUCCH\_FORMAT1\_DTX, describes the number of invalid (dtx=DTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 1 ('pucchFormat' == 1 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220). L2-PS shall not count/consider PUCCHs reporting SR only as from 3GPP pov. the negative SR is indicated by DTX which is no sign of bad signal quality.

**a4.) PUCCH format 3 un-successful detection**

M55303C17001, aka PUCCH\_FORMAT3\_DTX, describes the number of invalid (dtx=DTX) message receptions using PUCCH format 3 ('pucchFormat' == 3 in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_220).

**a5.) PUCCH format 3 un-successful detection with Rel.16 DMRS**

Refer to 5G\_L2\_16102\_replaced([11193166](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28pjiPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR864105]Note: For unsuccessful PUCCH F1 or F3 detection and during the BWP switch procedure: when SR is multiplexed with HARQ A/N, 5G-L2-PS shall acknowledge the resources allocated to SR, based on the srBit parameter, see [13332218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y6wgJtW_EfCnq6aYkXj8Pw), value received in the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message, see [11514174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). DTX counters shall be increased only for SR resources. This note does not apply to Loner l1variant.[End PR864105]

CP2 requirement(s):

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PM Counters for 5G-L2-PS

---

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-9 PM Counter Support CSI report on PUXCH Counter Support for 8 port (ID: 11150693)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `13365638`)

PM Counter Support
Upon reception of UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs (5G\_L1\_IF\_221\_replaced([11514182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs (5G\_L1\_IF\_200\_replaced([11513831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall evaluate each report inside the meassage whether increase respective customer counter.

The report with DTX will not considered for the corresponding counters update.

**1. For UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs,**

If (dtxMeas.dtx == nonDtx)

{

swith ( UE's configured CSI-RS value)

case 1 [CB008577-O] for 8 port [End CB008577-O]:

M55308C22001 = M55308C22001 + 1; break;

[CB008577-O] case 1 for 32 port :

M55308C00180(see [13365637](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRAdMPaLEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) = M55308C00180+ 1; break;[End CB008577-O]

case 2:

if( 0 == CRI decoded in uciBits)

M55308C22002 = M55308C22002 + 1; break;

else if( 1 == CRI in uciBits )

M55308C22003 = M55308C22003 + 1; break;

case 4:

if( 0 == CRI decoded in uciBits )

M55308C22004 = M55308C22004 + 1; break;

else if( 1 == CRI decoded in uciBits )

M55308C22005 = M55308C22005 + 1; break;

else if( 2 == CRI decoded in uciBits )

M55308C22006 = M55308C22006 + 1; break;

else if( 3 == CRI decoded in uciBits )

M55308C22007 = M55308C22007 + 1; break;

}

**2. For UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs**

If (CsiOnPuschDtxMeas.dtxCsiPart1 == nonDtx)

{

swith ( UE's configured CSI-RS value)

case 1 [CB008577-O] for 8 port [End CB008577-O]:

M55308C22001 = M55308C22001 + 1; break;

[CB008577-O] case 1 for 32 port :

M55308C00180(see [13365637](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRAdMPaLEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) = M55308C00180+ 1; break;[End CB008577-O]

case 2:

if( 0 == CRI decoded in uciCsiPart1Bits )

M55308C22002 = M55308C22002 + 1; break;

else if( 1 == CRI in uciCsiPart1Bits )

M55308C22003 = M55308C22003 + 1; break;

case 4:

if( 0 == CRI decoded in uciCsiPart1Bits )

M55308C22004 = M55308C22004 + 1; break;

else if( 1 == CRI decoded in uciCsiPart1Bits )

M55308C22005 = M55308C22005 + 1; break;

else if( 2 == CRI decoded in uciCsiPart1Bits )

M55308C22006 = M55308C22006 + 1; break;

else if( 3 == CRI decoded in uciCsiPart1Bits )

M55308C22007 = M55308C22007 + 1; break;

}

**Notes:**

1. CA scenario is supported, and Pcell or Scell will counter its own CSI report separately.
2. For the corresponding counters defination and description, refer to <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/5GSystemEngineering/_layouts/15/Doc.aspx?sourcedoc=%7B44BAFA4B-1D38-4951-95E7-28A266078EBD%7D&file=PM_counters_5G-L2-PS%20(3GPP%20NR).xlsx&action=default&mobileredirect=true&cid=849bfdcd-3251-47ac-af89-19d0ebfdb7c6>

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-10 PM Counter Support Number of failed receptions of DL TBs at UE after reaching DRB specific max HARQ reTx by gNB (ID: 11150707)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11150713`)

PM Counter Support
For 'NR DL HARQ' class, according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PM Counter M55300C12002 (DL\_TB\_F\_MAX\_RTX\_DRB\_MAX\_LM) shall be incremented each time a maximum number of HARQ transmissions has been reached for transport block for which DRB-specific transmissions limit was selected (please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12742\_replaced([11185319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvSQpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_7971\_replaced([11144196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_234YSvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_7973\_replaced([11145642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24A7IvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-11 PM Counter Support Num of successfully received DL TBs after any Txn for TBs with DRB specific HARQ maxTx limit applied (ID: 11150721)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11150724`)

PM Counter Support
For 'NR DL HARQ' class, according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PM Counter M55300C12005 (DL\_TB\_S\_ANY\_TX\_DRB\_MAX\_LM) shall be incremented each time successful HARQ feedback (ACK) is received for transport block for which DRB-specific transmissions limit was selected (please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12742\_replaced([11185319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvSQpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_7971\_replaced([11144196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_234YSvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_7973\_replaced([11145642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24A7IvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

###### 2.2.7.1.3.0-12 PM Counter Support Number of initial transmissions of DL TBs for which DRB specific HARQ maxTx limit applied (ID: 11150731)

**2.2.7.1.3.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11150738`)

PM Counter Support
For 'NR DL HARQ' class, according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PM Counter M55300C12003 (DL\_TB\_INTX\_MAX\_DRB\_MAX\_CF) shall be incremented each time any HARQ feedback (ACK, NACK or DTX) is received for an initial transmission of the transport block for which DRB-specific transmissions limit was selected (please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12742\_replaced([11185319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvSQpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_7971\_replaced([11144196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_234YSvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_7973\_replaced([11145642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24A7IvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**2.2.7.1.3.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `11150749`)

PM Counter Support
For 'NR DL HARQ' class, according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6272\_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PM Counter M55300C12004 (DL\_TB\_RETX\_DRB\_MAX\_LM) shall be incremented each time any HARQ feedback (ACK, NACK or DTX) is received for a retransmission of the transport block for which DRB-specific transmissions limit was selected (please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12742\_replaced([11185319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvSQpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_7971\_replaced([11144196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_234YSvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_7973\_replaced([11145642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24A7IvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

## 2.2.8 Post Scheduling

### 2.2.8.0-1 Post Scheduling FA: [Internal Domain] Post-Scheduler handler Document Owner: Michal Dudek (Nokia) (ID: 11150832)

### 2.2.8.1 Post-Pre scheduler

#### 2.2.8.1.0-1 Post-Pre scheduler Micro-DTX (ID: 11150844)

**2.2.8.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11150850`)

Post-Pre scheduler
When Micro-DTX feature is activated, the Post-Pre scheduler may disable/enable the feature according to Cell load as specified in 5G\_L2\_5924\_replaced([11148003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24OWjvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008238-F] The Post-Pre scheduler updates the rrmNumSlotSinceLastScheduling as specified in 5G\_L2\_5899\_replaced([11148256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24PkrvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB008238-F].

### 2.2.8.2 Post TD scheduler

#### 2.2.8.2.0-1 Post TD scheduler Determine the number of UEs sharing given PRB (ID: 11150861)

**2.2.8.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11150877`)

Post TD scheduler
If basic MU-MIMO is activated for a cell (actDlMuMimo is set to true & actDlMuMimoEnh is set to false (ref. 5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_IF\_109\_replaced([10968696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UZaEfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_IF\_1871\_replaced([10968710](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UZaE_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), a specialized PRB bookkeeping method needs to be applied (ref. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8352\_replaced([11191477](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvhhOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

In order to calculate PRB bookkeeping factors (rrmPrbBkFactor) and number of unallocated PRBs (rrmInstPrbFree) in Pair Size based PRB Bookkeeping (ref. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8156\_replaced([11191504](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvhhPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) distribution of UEs between PRBs must be known.

L2-PS shall convert rat0Bitmap (ref. [Before CNI-116869-D] 5G\_L2\_321\_replaced([11149724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24XgfvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[CNI-116869-D] 5G\_L2\_887\_replaced([11178401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26_9tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CNI-116869-D]) to prbAllocation for all scheduled UEs within a given cell and then sum up prbAllocation for all scheduled UEs to determine the number of UEs sharing given PRB:

prbAllocation for UE1: [x1\_0, x1\_1, ..., x1\_lastIdx]

prbAllocation for UE2: [x2\_0, x2\_1, ..., x2\_lastIdx]

...

sum of prbAllocation for all scheduled UEs:

ueSumInEachPrb = [x1\_0 + x2\_0 + ..., x1\_1 + x2\_1 + ..., ..., x1\_lastIdx + x2\_lastIdx + ...]

where:

x = 0 | 1

lastIdx <= 272

Calculated array determines how many UEs share given PRB within a given cell.

Number of UEs sharing given PRB equal to 0 means that this PRB is unallocated (free).

Number of unallocated PRBs (rrmInstPrbFree) equal to number of zeros in ueSumInEachPrb.

---

#### 2.2.8.2.0-2 Post TD scheduler Create Best NK list (ID: 12736750)

**2.2.8.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12736765`)

Post TD scheduler
select UEs from CS1  list at current slot to create Best NK list, the algorithm see [12517582: Prepare best N and K list](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_U2PXwBiDEfC3upM2pE5-4w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

Note:

BestNKListSize = Ceil (BestNKListRatio \* [Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size [CNI-136895-A] cs1ListMaxSizePreventive [End CNI-136895-A]);

K UEs = Ceil (BestNKListSize \* BestKRatio);

N UEs = BestNKListSize - K UEs;

where

BestNKListRatio:NRBTS/NRCELL/dlBestNListRatio.

[Before CNI-136895-A] avgCs1Size:avgCs1Size of next scheduling slot type(DL or BI slottype), see [11212749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)  
[CNI-136895-A]cs1ListMaxSizePreventive: cs1ListMaxSizePreventive of next scheduling slot type(DL or BI slottype), see [11212749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-n5cPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)  [End CNI-136895-A])

BestKRatio:rdDlHighBuffBestKRatio (see [12532524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_bfiC4BuXEfC3upM2pE5-4w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

---

#### 2.2.8.2.0-3 Post TD scheduler BLER calculation for SSB slots (ID: 12745472)

**2.2.8.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12745473`)

Post TD scheduler
[CB012623-A]

L2-PS shall  calculate BLER for mute slots based on the PDSCH real transmitions, the algorithm see [12709975: BLER calculation for SSB slots](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_eBYD8mXaEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

L2-PS shall run the algorithm of the SSB interference Mitigation for non-BF as the bellow:

1. Upon reception of cell set up or reconfig, (for conditions [12709089: Basic functionality](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_pAtj4GOsEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. Start/stop PRB muting and BLER calculation based on NRCELL.actSsbIMForNonBF, note: the start of BLER calculation shall be slot 0 after cell set up or reconfig.
3. Start/reset the r&d timer rdPeriodForSsbIM to start SSB slot BLER statistics
4. Store new SSB muted parameters
   1. If slotForSsbIM, blerThresForSsbIM shall be changed , PRB muting shall be stopped and reinitialized
   2. If cRbStartForSsbIM changes, the new value shall be applied in PRB muting
5. Initialize the BLER calculation
6. In the end of each 10 rdPeriodForSsbIM periods,
7. Run the BLER for SSB Slots algorithm, (for conditions refer to [12709975: BLER calculation for SSB slots](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_eBYD8mXaEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
8. Decide whether or not, (for conditions refer to  [12709089: Basic functionality](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_pAtj4GOsEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
   1. The specified PRBs shall be muted for the candidate DL slot([12707696: Configuration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_8CsJcWLPEfC3KtQ77je1xA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
   2. The prohibit timer([12731408: rdProhibitTimerForSsbIM](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_p4zdEnNQEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) shall be started/restarted
9. During each of rdProhibitTimerForSsbIM (20 rdPeriodForSsbIM) in muted PRB of the slots defined by [12709089: Basic functionality](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_pAtj4GOsEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
10. Not allocate the muted SSB PRB except common channel(SIB,Paging)
11. If there are timer out of the 10 rdPeriodForSsbIM periods for SSB muted slot BLER statistics during the prohibitTimer and BLER falls below the threshold, then muted PRBs shall still be muted and can not used

Based on the above procedure of the algorithm and the configuration of rdProhibitTimerForSsbIM and default 10 rdPeriodForSsbIM periods for SSB interference mitigation, there are three case listed as the bellow( A,B,C.b is the step of the above algorithm of the SSB interference Mitigation.   :

1. Default prohibitTimer as rdProhibitTimerForSsbIM (20 rdPeriodForSsbIM)are equal to the default 2\*10 rdPeriodForSsbIM periods for SSB interference mitigation, the diagrammatic sketch is as the bellow

### 2.2.8.3 Optimized Flow Control

#### 2.2.8.3.0-1 Optimized Flow Control Idle Timer Expiry (ID: 11150890)

**2.2.8.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12733843`)

Optimized Flow Control
**[Before PR843369]  
On rdEthUpdateTimer expiry, L2-PS**[PR843369]  
When both of the following conditions are met:\*\*\*\*

1. rdEthUpdateTimer has expired for the given UE
2. and the [12733172: Limit of maximum number of eTh updates for idle UEs in the given slot](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CyemUnRXEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) has not been reached,

then 5G-L2-PS [End PR843369]**shall schedule eTh recalculation for associated Ue (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4676\_replaced([11192682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvmZtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

This recalculation shall be performed in non real-time context to reduce impact on real-time scheduling performance. In high load scenario calculations may be postponed to next slots (as they are done in non real-time context).  If eTh recalculations triggered in the previous two slots haven't finished, 5G-L2-PS shall postpone triggering new eTh recalculations to next slots.

If calculated eTh is sufficiently different from lastSentEth (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15751\_replaced([11192830](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvnn0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details), L2-PS shall:

* sent eTh to L2-LO using LoCtrl\_DlUuStatusUpdateInd message (5G\_L2\_IF\_4305\_replaced([10985413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WH4Yfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  
  Note: If the maximum number of bearers in message is exceeded L2\_PS should send multiple messages. All bearers related to the single Ue should be sent within one message and should not be split between separate messages.
* store eTh in Ue context as lastSentEth to be used in next eTh update

---

#### 2.2.8.3.0-2 Optimized Flow Control Idle Timer Start/Restart (ID: 11150910)

**2.2.8.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11150926`)

Optimized Flow Control
L2-PS shall start a timer for each UE to trigger eTh calculation in absence of DL scheduling. The timer interval is [Before PR784119] specified by rdEthUpdateTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15747\_replaced([11193522](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvtucfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). On the timer expiry L2-PS shall re-start it, set interval to rdEthUpdateTimer and follow 5G\_L2\_10486\_replaced([11150890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1O_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

To prevent triggering overload control in high load scenarios, L2-PS during DL scheduling shall restart  eTh update timer and set interval to: rdEthUpdateTimer + additional load adjusted interval. Additional interval value shall be calculated using data from overload control, ‘skippedUes’ to ‘numToBeScheduledUes’ ratio (5G\_L2\_1859\_replaced([11213118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_1675\_replaced([11203797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299yIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and shall not exceed 100 ms.

For example:

If calculated ratio is 0 (no UEs are skipped), additional load adjusted interval shall be 0

If calculated ratio is 1 (all UEs are skipped), additional load adjusted interval shall be 100 ms

[PR784119] rdEthUpdateTimer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15747\_replaced([11193522](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvtucfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + load adjusted interval. On the timer expiry 5G-L2-PS shall restart the timer, set interval to rdEthUpdateTimer + load adjusted interval and follow 5G\_L2\_10486\_replaced([11150890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1O_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

To prevent triggering overload control or using too many resources in high load scenarios, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate load adjusted interval. This interval is calculated as follows:

(1) 5G-L2-PS shall monitor the completion status of previously triggered eTh calculations. It shall calculate the ratio of slots where new calculations were postponed due to ongoing previous calculations (see 5G\_L2\_10486\_replaced([11150890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24e1O_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over the past 10 eTh calculation triggers. Based on this ratio, 5G-L2-PS shall calculate the load adjusted interval using the formula: ratio \* 100 [ms].

For example:

If calculated ratio is 0 (none of the eTh recalculations were postponed), the load adjusted interval shall be 0 ms

If calculated ratio is 1 (all of the eTh recalculations in previous slots were postponed), the load adjusted interval shall be 100 ms

For FR2:

Interval shall be calculated by choosing max value calculated in (1) and value calculated using data from overload control, mean ‘skippedUes’ to ‘numToBeScheduledUes’ ratio from 5 slots (5G\_L2\_1859\_replaced([11213118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_1675\_replaced([11203797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_299yIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))using the formula: mean ratio \* 100 [ms].

For example:

If calculated mean ratio is 0 (no UEs were skipped in 5 slots), the load adjusted interval shall be 0

If calculated mean ratio is 1 (all UEs were skipped in 5 slots), the load adjusted interval shall be 100 ms

[End PR784119]

---

#### 2.2.8.3.0-3 Optimized Flow Control Limit of maximum number of eTh updates for idle UEs in the given slot (ID: 12733172)

**2.2.8.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12733174`)

Optimized Flow Control
When updating the estimated throughput for idle UEs, then 5G-L2-PS shall limit the number of updates in the given slot to the maximum value defined by one of the following parameters, based on the cell's frequencyRange (obtained from the [10966093: PsCnfg\_AddressDistributionReq message content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UL-vvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) from the [0966124: L2RtPoolDeploymentInformations structure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)):

* If frequencyRange is FR2: [12733120: rdMaxNumOfIdleUeEthUpdatesPerFr2Slot](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_LE-sMHRQEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
* Otherwise: [12733116: rdMaxNumOfIdleUeEthUpdatesPerFr1Slot](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_h-Au4HRPEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

---

### 2.2.8.4 Slot blanking due to Rf high temperature

#### 2.2.8.4.0-1 Slot blanking due to Rf high temperature Achieved muting ratio calculation (ID: 11150937)

**2.2.8.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11150942`)

Slot blanking due to Rf high temperature
achievedMutingRatio computation is explained in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20824\_replaced([11183727](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvMxFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Additional conditions to be applied at L2-PS are listed below

1. achievedMutingRatio must be computed in every DL/Special Slot (irrespective of the slot muting decision) as long as rfCoolingMode = true
2. When PsCell\_SlotBlankingReq (with rfCoolingMode = True and with modified tgtMutingRatio) is received at L2-PS in slot n, the achievedMutingRatio shall be initialized / reset to the value of new tgtMutingRatio not later than in slot n+1.
3. When rfCoolingMode = False or when the feature is turned off, L2-PS internally maintains the value of tgtMutingRatio and achievedMuting Ratio as 1.00 (100%).

[PR720039]

1. In case of special slot, SlotmutingOutcomeNormalized shall be used instead of SlotmutingOutcome during the achievedMutingRatio computation.

[End PR720039]

---

#### 2.2.8.4.0-2 Slot blanking due to Rf high temperature Slot muting outcome calculation (ID: 11150950)

**2.2.8.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11150966`)

Slot blanking due to Rf high temperature
SlotMutingOutcome computation is explained in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20825\_replaced([11183747](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvMxGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Additional conditions to be applied at L2-PS are listed below

1. SlotMutingOutcome must be computed in every DL/Special Slot (irrespective of the slot muting decision) as long as rfCoolingMode = true
2. SlotmutingOutcome[i] shall be initialized with value 0 when (i) rfCoolingMode = false OR (ii) In the first slot when rfCoolingMode = true
3. nSym\_not\_used [Before CB011114-B] shall comprise the total unused symbols after PDCCH + PDSCH + all other resource allocation [CB011114-B] is equal to  nSym\_total - total number of symbols used  [End CB011114-B] on the DL/Special slot
4. nSym\_not\_used shall be computed/considered even when there are symbols left unused due to natural scheduling (DL/Special slots with 1 or more unused symbols)
5. SlotMutingOutcome shall be computed after computing achievedMutingRatio in a given DL/Special slot
6. SlotmutingOutcome for special slots shall be normalized based on total number of symbols for DL slot as mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20825\_replaced([11183747](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvMxGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The method to apply normalization shall be

SlotmutingOutcomeNormalized[i] =  SlotmutingOutcome[i] x (nSym\_total\_spl(i) / nSym\_total\_dl(i))

with:

i                                                    index of DL/special slot

SlotmutingOutcome[i]                      SlotmutingOutcome before normalization computed as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_   20825

SlotmutingOutcomeNormalized[i]        SlotmutingOutcome after normalization

nSym\_total\_spl                                total DL symbols per special slot

nSym\_total\_dl                                 total DL symbols per DL slot (non special slot). Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2313\_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB011114-A]

1. For FDD, nSym\_total is the total number of DL symbols per DL slot. It is equal to 14 OFDM Symbols.

[End CB011114-A]

[CB011114-B]

If the FDD cell is shared with LTE, then nSym\_total is the number of symbols applicable for NR DL transmissions. It is equal to 12 OFDM Symbols.

1. For a FDD Cell shared with LTE, symbols used for LTE CRS Rate Matching are considered as symbols applicable for NR DL transmissions.

[End CB011114-B]

---

## 2.2.9 Slot Timing

### 2.2.9.0-2 Slot Timing Slot Start (ID: 11150981)

**2.2.9.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `13382954`)

Slot Timing
The DL Scheduler shall start the NR-slot-based processing at a time which guarantees that the L1-DL constraints wrt. the various message receive windows (described in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_121 ff.) are respected.

Based on those, the DL Scheduler processing for an NR-slot shall start x us before the NR-slot boundary at the gNB antenna

* following synchronization procedure described in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_671\_replaced([11177460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeTrwfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_672\_replaced([11177470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeTrwvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

whereby x is set

* to (SlotOffsetDl + OneWayHwDelayDlc + AdditionalFddOffset), where
* AdditionalFddOffset is set to 750us if FDD cell is on Loki or Thor [CB014419-SR-EC] or Odin [End CB014419-SR-EC] based BB board, 30us if FDD cell is on ABIL based BB board, 0 otherwise.
* **FDD: *SlotOffsetDl = constant 1000us (1 slot) with SCS15kHz.***
* *SlotOffsetDl = constant 1000us (2 NR-slots) for below 6GHz configuration (SCS30kHz)*
* *SlotOffsetDl = constant 375us (3 NR-slots) for above 6GHz configuration (SCS120kHz)*
* *SlotOffsetDl can be overriden in testing with R&D parameter rdSlotOffsetAdjustmentDl by setting it to value other than 0xFFFFFFFF. Unit is microseconds.*
* *OneWayHwDelayDl =  Value is read from PsCell\_CellSetupReq if rd579LongFiberActivated is set to “1” and rdSlotTimerServiceEnabled is set to “1”. Otherwise it remains at initialization value of 50us.*
* **OneWayHwDelayDl =  Value is always read from PsCell\_CellSetupReq for All in Cloud product**
* *OneWayHwDelayDl can be overriden in testing with R&D parameter rdOverrideOneWayHwDelayDl (5G\_L2\_3476\_replaced([11182008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27YYNPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) by setting it to value other than 0xFFFFFFFF. Unit is microseconds.*
* In case the configured *OneWayHwDelayDl is longer than slot duration then a correction is applied:*
* **SlotOffsetDl is extended by RoundDownToInt(OneWayHwDelayDl/SlotDuration) slots**
* *OneWayHwDelayDl is shortened to OneWayHwDelayDl mod SlotDuration microseconds*
* For example, if *OneWayHwDelayDl is (1.6 slots \* slotduration) microseconds then the correction  increases* SlotOffsetDl by one slot and *OneWayHwDelayDl becomes (0.6 slots \* slotduration) microseconds.*\*\*
* When the actFlexibleBiSlotDurationMode is not set to "disabled" and the 750us timing pattern is activated (as described in 5G\_L2\_22818\_replaced([11157164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25EEEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the SlotOffsetDl is extended by one slot. (refer to 750us timing pattern defined in 5G\_UP\_13436\_replaced([11388805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufMmUfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* When FR1 TDD frame structure is configured with tdLte Config0, the slotOffsetDl for each slot is not a fixed value any more, flexible slotOffsetDl value shall be used based on the table as described in 5G\_L2\_23169\_replaced([11157417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25FSLvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5GTimer is always used.

Note, also 5G\_L2\_353\_replaced([11151020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24gDUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) depicts the affected messages and timings including L2-LO.

---

## 2.2.10 DL L1-L2 timing requirement

### 2.2.10.0-5 DL L1-L2 timing requirement Statistics of Late DL Messages Sent to L1: L2-PS must maintain late DL data send messages sent to L1 and total DL data send messages sent to L1 over a period of second. These statistics are printed using VIP logs if there exists any late message during 1 second observation period. These counters are maintained for each message mentioned in 12710358: Time stamping of L2-PS DL messages to L1 . (ID: 12712456)

## 2.2.11 DL Pipeline Scheduling

### 2.2.11.1 Overview (informative)

#### 2.2.11.1.0-1 Overview (informative) Concept (ID: 13448744)

**2.2.11.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448745`)

Overview (informative)
Basic concepts with DL pipeline scheduling introduced.

DL TD EO: Includes DlPre Scheduler, DlTd Scheduler, DlPost Scheduler and DlNrt.

DL FD EO: Includes DlFdm Scheduler and DlFd Scheduler.

UL EO: Includes all UL Schedulers and UlNrt. No change with DL pipeline scheduling introduced.

DL Core: Where DL TD EO is running, DL FD EO will run on this core on non-pipeline slot(see [13448749: Slot Processing Type](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_8thWsCiyEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

UL Core: Where UL EO isrunning, DL FD EO will run on this core on pipeline slot(see [13448749: Slot Processing Type](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_8thWsCiyEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

---

#### 2.2.11.1.0-2 Overview (informative) Scheduling Type (ID: 13448747)

**2.2.11.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13451409`)

Overview (informative)
Sequential Scheduling

---

**2.2.11.1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448748`)

Overview (informative)
Sequential scheduling means that schedlers are run as planned order, Pre -> Td -> Fdm -> Fd -> Post.  
At the same time, when schedulers are running, Nrt messages can’t be handled.

---

**2.2.11.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13451419`)

Overview (informative)
Parallel Scheduling

---

**2.2.11.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13451420`)

Overview (informative)
Parallel scheduling means that DlNrt and Dl FD EO can run on the two cores parallelly.   
But the critical path (DlPre, DlTd, DlFdm, DlFd, DlPost) still run sequentially as planned order.

This scheduling mode is introduced by CB012971-WB. will be obselete by CB014670?

---

**2.2.11.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13451421`)

Overview (informative)
Pipeline Scheduling

---

**2.2.11.1.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13451422`)

Overview (informative)
Pipeline scheduling means that DL TD EO(DlPre, DlTd, DlPost and DlNrt) run on DL Core and DL FD EO(DlFdm and DlFd) run on UL Core parallelly.

Note:   
1. Because DlFdm/DlFd is triggered by DlTd, so DlPre/DlTd/DlPost and DlFdm/DlFd with the same xsfn are always run sequentially although they are run on two cores.  
2. For same component, the sequence shall be kept. e.g. DlPost(N) shall alwasy run ahead of DlPost(N+1).

---

#### 2.2.11.1.0-3 Overview (informative) Slot Processing Type (ID: 13448749)

**2.2.11.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13451411`)

Overview (informative)
Normal Pipeline Slot

---

**2.2.11.1.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448750`)

Overview (informative)
Normal pipeline slot are slots which pipeline scheduling(see [13451421: Pipeline Scheduling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_zjhxoCmJEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is applied except the last one before UL scheduling slot.

Pipeline scheduling is applied when feature flag(will be define in CB014670-C) is enanbled and pipeline scheduling switched to ON(see [13448854: Dynamic Switch](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FlE4UCjWEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), will be define in CB014670-C).

In normal pipeline slots, the DL TD EO and DL FO EO run concurrently on the DL Core and UL Core.

---

**2.2.11.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13451415`)

Overview (informative)
Last Pipeline Slot

---

**2.2.11.1.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13451416`)

Overview (informative)
Last pipeline slot are the last slots before UL scheduling slot which pipeline scheduling(see [13451421: Pipeline Scheduling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_zjhxoCmJEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is applied.

Pipeline scheduling is applied when feature flag(will be define in CB014670-C) is enanbled and pipeline scheduling switched to ON(see [13448854: Dynamic Switch](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FlE4UCjWEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), will be define in CB014670-C).

In last pipeline slots, the DL TD EO and DL FO EO run concurrently on the DL Core and UL Core.

---

**2.2.11.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13451412`)

Overview (informative)
Non-Pipeline Slot

---

**2.2.11.1.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13451413`)

Overview (informative)
Non-pipeline slot are the slots sequential scheduling (see [13451409: Sequential Scheduling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ddxi0SmGEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is enabled.

In non-pipeline slots, both DL TD EO and DL FO EO run on DL Core.

---

#### 2.2.11.1.0-4 Overview (informative) Overall Example (ID: 13448751)

**2.2.11.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13448752`)

Overview (informative)
This is an example to explain the basic scheduling process of pipeline enabled.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a timeline or Gantt chart illustrating a process with different stages and activities over time. The timeline is divided into columns representing time slots, labeled from -3 to 9. There are several rows representing different aspects of the process:
**Top Section:**
\* **5G001116 3ms shift:** This appears to be a title or identifier for the timeline.
\* **Air:** This row seems to indicate the general environment or state.
\* **DL Sch:** This row likely represents Downlink Scheduling activities.
\* **UL Sch:** This row likely represents Uplink Scheduling activities.
\* **loadType:** This row indicates different load types, such as "Mixed" and "Idle".
**Middle Section (Core Activities):**
\* **DL Core:** This row, highlighted in green, represents core Downlink activities. It contains various sub-activities like "Pre+TD0", "DL NRT", "POST0", "Pre+TD1", "DL NRT", "POST1", "Pre+TD2", "DL NRT", "POST2", "DL NRT", "Pre+TD3", "POST3", "DL NRT", "Pre+TD4", "POST4", "DL NRT", "POST5", "Pre+TD6", "FDM+FD6", "POST6", "DL NRT", "Pre+TD7", "FDM+FD7", "POST7", "DL NRT". There are also annotations explaining the conditions and logic for these activities, such as "150us advanced", "Add Cs2 UEs in Cs2Filter", "Only UEs NOT in Cs2Filter can be handled", "Remove UEs from Cs2Filter", "Low Load, POST before Pre. Cs2Filter is empty, all UEs can continuous scheduling", "No Enough time for POST Move to after Pre+TD", "High Load, POST after Pre. Only UEs are NOT in Cs2FilterList can be selected", and "FDM/FD move back to DL Core".
\* **UI Core:** This row, highlighted in yellow, represents core Uplink activities. It contains sub-activities like "FDM+FDO", "UL NRT", "UL", "FDM+FD1", "UL NRT", "UL", "FDM+FD2", "UL", "UL NRT", "FDM+FD3", "UL", "FDM+FD4", "UL", "FDM+FD5", "UL Pre>TD>FDM>FD8", "UL NRT", "UL Pre>TD>FDM>FD9", "UL NRT". Annotations here include "Send FdmScheduleResp to DL core with non-selected UEs after FDM to reduce filtered/blocked UEs", "Next UL is Non-sch slot, UL delay can be accepted. OLC may not needed.", and "Next UL is sch slot, OLC is needed to ensure POST has enough time and UL sch start on time".
**Topmost Rows (DL/UL Slots):**
These rows, colored in various shades of blue, gray, and cyan, seem to represent specific time slots or configurations for Downlink (DL) and Uplink (UL) operations. For example, "DLO", "DL1", "DL2", "DL3", "DL4", "DL5", "DL6", "UL8", "UL9" are labeled within these colored blocks, corresponding to the time columns. Some cells in these rows are also labeled with "DL" or "UL".
The overall diagram appears to be a detailed schedule or simulation of a communication system's operation, likely within a 5G context, showing how downlink and uplink transmissions are managed, including scheduling, filtering, and load handling over a series of time slots.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-03260930.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

doc link: [13442684\_DL Pipeline Scheduling.xlsx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20L2%20Entity%20Level/2%205G-L2-PS%20Component%20Requirements/2.2%20DL%20Scheduler/13442684_DL%20Pipeline%20Scheduling.xlsx?d=wf5880a1bf9934423909903375729edc6&csf=1&web=1&e=IIDkuz)

### 2.2.11.2 Cs2 Filter

#### 2.2.11.2.0-1 Cs2 Filter Introduction (ID: 13448755)

**2.2.11.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448756`)

Cs2 Filter
Since DL TD EO(DlPre, DlTd, DlPost and DlNrt) and DL FD EO(DlFdm and DlFd) can run on different cores parallelly which will introduce data race while the two EOs may visit the same UE context/DB.

To avoid the conflict, cs2Filter is introduced. cs2Filter is a UE list including the UEs selected by Pre/TD in Cs2List for current slot.

cs2Filter is maintained and used in DL TD EO to avoid data race with DL FD EO. The idea is that when UEs are scheduling on DL FD EO, these UEs shall not be visited/handled in DL TD EO at the same time.

---

#### 2.2.11.2.0-2 Cs2 Filter Housekeeping (ID: 13448764)

**2.2.11.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13452038`)

Cs2 Filter
Initialization

---

**2.2.11.2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448765`)

Cs2 Filter
Cs2Filter shall be set as empty at the startup, e.g. during cell setup.

---

**2.2.11.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13452316`)

Cs2 Filter
Add UEs into cs2Filter

---

**2.2.11.2.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13452317`)

Cs2 Filter
At the end of DlTd scheduling(cs2List is ready), all UEs in cs2List shall be added into Cs2Filter before DL TD EO sends the cs2List with message FdScheduleReq/FdmScheduleReq(see [13448852: New Internal Messages](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FlFfYCjWEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) to the DL FD EO.

---

**2.2.11.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13452318`)

Cs2 Filter
Remove UEs from cs2Filter

---

**2.2.11.2.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13452319`)

Cs2 Filter
Upon FdmScheduleResp(see [13448852: New Internal Messages](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FlFfYCjWEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) or FdScheduleResp is received, the UEs included in the messages shall be removed from Cs2Filter.

Rational:

* After DlFdm is done, the Ues which are not selected to be scheduled in current slot shall be scheduling eligble UEs as soon as posible in next slot.
* For Ues which is dropped by FD-UE skipping (see [11213118: FD-UE Skipping](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-purfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall be send back up DL TD EO in FdScheduleResp to avoid zombie UEs in cs2Filter.

---

#### 2.2.11.2.0-3 Cs2 Filter Apply on UE message (ID: 13448766)

**2.2.11.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13452391`)

Cs2 Filter
Filter UE message

---

**2.2.11.2.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13448767`)

Cs2 Filter
When the UE related messages are received and the UE(s) in the message is in cs2Filter, the messages can NOT be handled immediately to avoid data race.

The message(s) shall be buffered into BufferedEvents(a list stores the messages blocked by Cs2Filter), and recorded the related (UE, msg) information in FilteredEvents(includes [UE, message] pair blocked by Cs2Filter).

If there are more than one UEs in single message, the UEs are not in Cs2Filter can be handled immediately. The message still shall be buffered in case there are other UEs in cs2Filter in the message. The handled UEs in the message shall be skipped when the message is retrieved to handle.

Once the UE is removed from Cs2Filter, the buffered message shall be retrieved and handled as soon as possible.

The impacted messages refer to [Message.xlsx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB014500%20-%20CB014999/CFAM/CB014670%20Extended%20downlink%20processing%20configuration%20for%20FR1-TDD/Message.xlsx?d=w635cc1f1a29545469c0a8febba482e6a&csf=1&web=1&e=1IzQui) .

---

**2.2.11.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13452392`)

Cs2 Filter
Restriction

---

**2.2.11.2.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13452393`)

Cs2 Filter
With Cs2Filter is applied on UE message handling, the following rules shall be obeyed.

* The messages priority shall not be changed.
* For a single UE, the message handling may be delayed, but the messages handling sequence of the UE shall not be changed.
* For a UE, when it is removed from Cs2Filter, NRT message handling shall not exceed time budget limitations of current slot (OLC applied).

---

#### 2.2.11.2.0-4 Cs2 Filter Cell Message Handling (ID: 13448762)

**2.2.11.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13448763`)

Cs2 Filter
According to CellDb Split solution in Feature CB014822, Dl FD EO can visit CellDb directly. So, if DL TD EO is modifying CellDb when DL FD EO is reading, data race will be introduced.

To avoid conflict, when the cell level messages received,

If FdScheduleReq N (N is the xsfn) is send but the corresponding FdScheduleResp N is not received/handled, the cell messages shall be buffered and set cs1Size([11212970: Control based on run-time measurements](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) as 1.

When FdScheduleResp N is received and handled, before FdScheduleReq N+1 sending, the buffered cell messages can be handled.

After all buffered cell message handled,

cs1Size shall restore as [11212970: Control based on run-time measurements](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-pHlfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

The impacted messages refer to [Message.xlsx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB014500%20-%20CB014999/CFAM/CB014670%20Extended%20downlink%20processing%20configuration%20for%20FR1-TDD/Message.xlsx?d=w635cc1f1a29545469c0a8febba482e6a&csf=1&web=1&e=1IzQui) .

---

#### 2.2.11.2.0-5 Cs2 Filter Message Tracking with cs2Filter (ID: 13448964)

**2.2.11.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13448965`)

Cs2 Filter
This requirement defines the bitset to record the messages filtered by cs2Filter or buffered cell messages in a specific period.

Bits and messages mapping table as below.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |

**2.2.11.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13451425`)

DL Parallel Scheduler
pre/td/post/nrt can parallely run with fdm/fd in pipeline slot

post(n) may before or after pre(n+1) normal pipeline slot

post(n) shall before pre(n+1) in last pipeline slot

same as legacy in non-pipeline slot

Details decided by implementation
